Conclusion: 本研究构建的词汇感官运动规范数据库为汉语具身认知研究提供了宝贵资源。研究结果支持具身认知理论，表明语言模型中蕴含的分布统计信息能够部分映射并重构具身空间结构，为理解机器如何通过语言习得概念知识提供了有力证据。

Abstract: Understanding how conceptual knowledge is grounded in bodily experience, and to what extent machine systems can acquire such knowledge without direct sensorimotor experience, are central questions in both cognitive science and embodied artificial intelligence research. Large-scale normative resources are essential for investigating these questions empirically, yet such resources remain sparse for non-Indo-European languages. We present a novel normative database for 3,000 lexicalized concepts in Mandarin Chinese, comprising 11-dimensional sensorimotor ratings and unidimensional embodiment ratings collected from 378 native Mandarin speakers. The ratings demonstrate high reliability and strong cross-norm validity with existing Chinese resources, each of which covers fewer words and a subset of the 11 sensorimotor dimensions. In a validation study, we tested new variables derived from a theoretically motivated metric, Perceptual Strength of Embodiment (PSE) (Huang et al., 2025), together with seven common composite variables, on lexical decision tasks. The results suggest that PSE-Sensorimotor and Minkowski-3 are the strongest composite predictors of lexical decision performance, capturing the facilitatory effects of sensorimotor information on lexical processing. A further exploratory study showed that sensorimotor ratings are substantially recoverable from purely linguistic representations using simple regression models (mean Spearman r = .62 across dimensions), though recovery varied markedly: visual and auditory dimensions yielded higher correspondence than chemosensory ones. Representational similarity analysis further showed that the relational geometry of the sensorimotor space is also partially recoverable (r = .540), consistent with the view that distributional language use encodes aspects of embodied conceptual structure.

### [43] [More Context, Larger Models, or Moral Knowledge? A Systematic Study of Schwartz Value Detection in Political Texts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22641)
*Víctor Yeste,Paolo Rosso*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文分析了在政治文本中检测价值观的有效途径，发现盲目增加上下文长度或模型规模并非万能，结合检索增强的道德知识库及针对性的融合策略，才能更有效地处理复杂的价值观分类任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在政治文本中识别隐晦的价值观往往依赖于周围的论点和细微的语境差异，现有技术在处理这类细微差别时面临挑战。研究旨在探究上下文信息及显式道德知识库在句子级价值观检测中的实际作用，并评估不同模型配置对提升检测性能的效果。

Method: 研究采用了多维度的比较方法：1. 输入维度：比较句子级、窗口级和全文档级上下文；2. 知识维度：评估无RAG与利用精选道德知识库的检索增强生成（RAG）效果；3. 模型架构：对比有监督的DeBERTa-v3（base/large）编码器与12B至123B参数的零样本大语言模型（LLMs）；4. 融合策略：评估早期融合、后期融合及交叉注意力机制在RAG中的表现。

Result: 研究发现：1. 增加上下文对有监督的DeBERTa模型有显著提升（提升3.8-4.8 macro-F1），但对零样本LLM效果不一；2. 检索增强的道德知识库在所有测试模型中均有稳健的性能提升；3. 模型规模的扩展并不总能带来性能增益；4. 简单的“早期融合”方法优于复杂的后期融合或交叉注意力RAG变体；5. 上下文和检索对于社会情境化或易混淆的价值观检测尤为有效。

Conclusion: 本文研究表明，在政治文本中检测施瓦茨价值观（Schwartz values）时，单纯依赖增加上下文长度或模型规模并不总是有效。上下文、外部道德知识和模型架构之间存在复杂的交互作用。因此，该领域的研究应采取综合评估方法，而非盲目追求模型规模或输入长度的增加。

Abstract: Detecting Schwartz values in political text is difficult because implicit cues often depend on surrounding arguments and fine-grained distinctions between neighboring values. We study when context and explicit moral knowledge help sentence-level value detection. Using the ValuesML/Touch{é} ValueEval format, we compare sentence, window, and full-document inputs; no-RAG and retrieval-augmented settings with a curated moral knowledge base; supervised DeBERTa-v3-base/large encoders; and zero-shot LLMs from 12B to 123B parameters. The results show that more context is not uniformly better: full-document context improves supervised DeBERTa encoders by 3.8--4.8 macro-F1 points over sentence-only input, but does not consistently help zero-shot LLMs. Retrieved moral knowledge is more consistently useful in matched comparisons, improving each tested model family and context condition under early fusion. However, scaling from DeBERTa-v3-base to large and from 12B to larger LLMs does not guarantee gains, and simple early fusion outperforms the tested late-fusion and cross-attention RAG variants for encoders. Per-value analyses show that context and retrieval help most for socially situated or conceptually confusable values. These findings suggest that value-sensitive NLP should evaluate context, knowledge, and model family jointly rather than treating longer inputs or larger models as universal improvements.

Experimental results demonstrate that the LLM detectors based on our method outperform baseline detectors based on plain text, and even surpass the best-performing traditional detector, RoBERTa. The Gemini detector using our method achieves a Macro-F1 score of 85.65%, reaching the state-of-the-art level. Abstract: Moral language is subtle and culturally variable, making it difficult to translate faithfully across languages. Idiomatic expressions, slang, and cultural references introduce hard-to-avoid translation artifacts. Yet automated moral values classification depends on language-specific annotated corpora that exist almost exclusively in English. We investigate whether LLM-based translation can bridge this gap, taking Polish as a test case. Using $\sim$50k morally-annotated social media posts from a diverse range of topics, we apply a principled four-method validation pipeline: LaBSE cross-lingual embedding similarity, Centered Kernel Alignment (CKA), LLM-as-judge evaluation, and deep learning classifier parity tests. We show that despite shortcomings in handling slang, vulgarity, and culturally-loaded expressions, direct translation preserves subtle moral cues well enough to be harvested by cross-lingual machine learning -- with mean cosine similarity of 0.86 and AUC gaps of 0.01--0.02 across all foundations closing further under fine-tuning of language models. ### [46] [Self-Policy Distillation via Capability-Selective Subspace Projection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22675)
*Guangya Hao,Yitong Shang,Yunbo Long,Zhuokai Zhao,Hanxue Liang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有自蒸馏方法依赖外部信号或噪声干扰大的痛点，本文提出了自策略蒸馏（SPD），通过在激活空间内提取特定任务的低秩子空间来过滤噪声，在无需额外反馈的情况下显著提升了 LLM 的任务性能与泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自蒸馏方法依赖昂贵的外部信号（如代码执行反馈或奖励模型）来筛选输出，或者直接对所有原始输出进行训练，导致能力提升受限且难以泛化。此外，模型生成的输出通常混合了任务无关的噪声（如格式习惯、模型特有错误），稀释了对特定核心能力的优化效果。

Method: 提出了自策略蒸馏（Self-Policy Distillation, SPD）方法：1. 通过模型在定义正确性的标记上的梯度，提取出一个低秩能力子空间；2. 在模型自生成过程中，将键值（KV）激活值投影到该子空间中，从而过滤掉风格、格式等非核心噪声，仅聚焦于目标能力；3. 利用这些经过筛选的输出执行标准的下一词预测损失进行微调。

Result: 实验结果显示，SPD 在代码生成、数学推理及多选题任务中，对比同类无外部信号的自蒸馏方法提升了高达 13%，较原始预训练基线提升了 16%。特别是在跨领域泛化任务中，SPD 的性能表现提升了 15%。

Conclusion: SPD 通过无需外部反馈的自蒸馏机制，成功从模型自身的生成产物中提取并强化特定能力，证明了在无需额外标注或奖励模型的情况下，通过对内部激活值的精细控制，能显著提升大语言模型的泛化性能与特定领域能力。

Abstract: Self-distillation bootstraps large language models (LLMs) by training on their own generations. However, existing methods either rely on external signals to curate self-generated outputs (e.g., correctness filtering, execution feedback, and reward search), which are costly and unavailable for the best-performing frontier models, or skip curation entirely and train on all raw outputs, an approach that is often domain-specific and hard to generalize. Both also share a deeper weakness that self-generated outputs entangle task-relevant capability with others, such as stylistic patterns, formatting artifacts, and model-specific errors, diluting the signal for the specific capability one aims to improve. In this paper, we propose Self-Policy Distillation (SPD), which achieves generalizable, capability selective without any external signal. Specifically, SPD extracts a low-rank capability subspace from the model's own gradients on correctness-defining tokens, projects key-value (KV) activations into this subspace during self-generation, and fine-tunes on the resulting raw outputs with standard next-token prediction loss. Through extensive experiments across code generation, mathematical reasoning, and multiple-choice QA, we show that SPD achieves up to 13% improvement over state-of-the-art self-distillation methods without external signals and up to 16% improvement over pre-trained baselines. Notably, SPD demonstrates superior generalizability, achieving 15% better performance under out-of-domain generalization settings.

</details>


### [47] [Tokenization with Split Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22705)
*Craig W. Schmidt,Michael Krumdick,Adam Wiemerslage,Seth Ebner,Varshini Reddy,Yuval Pinter,Chris Tanner*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ToaST 是一种新的基于拆分树的优化分词方法，通过整数规划优化词汇表，有效减少了 Token 数量并显著提升了语言模型的下游性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的分词方法（如 BPE、WordPiece、UnigramLM）在压缩效率和词汇表构建上存在局限性，导致 Token 序列过长，限制了模型的上下文处理能力。研究旨在通过直接优化压缩目标，提高分词的效率与信息密度。

Method: 提出 Tokenization with Split Trees (ToaST)：1. 使用预计算的字节 n-gram 统计信息，将预分词贪婪地拆分为完整二叉树；2. 采用递归推理程序，在树中搜索并输出第一个在词汇表中的节点；3. 词汇表选择被建模为整数规划（IP）问题，以最小化总 Token 数为目标，并通过线性规划（LP）松弛实现近最优解。

Result: 在英语文本上，相比 BPE、WordPiece 和 UnigramLM，在 40,960 及以上词汇表大小时，Token 数量减少超过 11%；在 1.5B 参数模型实验中，ToaST 的 CORE 得分最高，在 22 项任务中的 13 项表现最优，显著提升了 Renyi 效率。

Conclusion: ToaST 是一种高效的子词分词方法，通过基于拆分树的优化实现了更优的压缩率。它不仅能够有效缩短序列长度、扩展模型有效上下文窗口，还在多项语言建模任务中展现了显著的性能提升，证明了在词汇表构建中引入优化目标的有效性。

Abstract: We introduce Tokenization with Split Trees (ToaST), a subword tokenization method that directly optimizes compression under a new recursive inference procedure. ToaST greedily splits each pretoken into a full binary tree using precomputed byte n-gram counts, independent of any vocabulary. Given a vocabulary, inference recursively descends each split tree and emits the first in-vocabulary node reached on each path. Vocabulary selection is formulated as an Integer Program (IP) that minimizes the total token count over all split trees under this inference procedure. The Linear Programming (LP) relaxation is near-integral in practice, yielding provably near-optimal vocabularies, with training time empirically scaling quadratically in the number of split trees. On English text, ToaST reduces token counts by more than 11% compared to BPE, WordPiece, and UnigramLM at vocabulary sizes of 40,960 and above, reducing the number of inference tokens for models using this tokenizer, thus extending the effective context length. ToaST also uses common single-byte tokens less frequently than these baselines, leading to a substantial improvement in Renyi efficiency. In experiments training 1.5B parameter language models, ToaST achieves the highest CORE score, outperforming baselines by 2.6%--7.6%, with significance for two of three, and scoring best on 13 of 22 individual tasks.

</details>


### [48] [ChronoMedKG: A Temporally-Grounded Biomedical Knowledge Graph and Benchmark for Clinical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22734)
*Md Shamim Ahmed,Farzaneh Firoozbakht,Lukas Galke Poech,Jan Baumbach,Richard Röttger*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 研究者提出了 ChronoMedKG，这是一个具备时间维度的生物医学知识图谱，通过多智能体 LLM 系统从文献中自动提取带有时序特征的医疗知识，有效解决了现有静态图谱无法支持临床纵向推理的痛点，显著提升了检索增强临床系统的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的生物医学知识图谱（如 PrimeKG、Hetionet 等）大多将疾病关联视为静态事实，忽略了时间信息在临床推理中的关键作用（如相同症状在不同年龄阶段可能指向不同疾病）。这种静态特性限制了这些图谱在纵向临床推理和检索增强系统中的应用。

Method: 研究团队构建了一个由疾病自主的多智能体流程，利用多个前沿大语言模型从 PubMed 和 PMC 文献中独立提取知识。通过多模型共识机制、可信度过滤以及本体对齐，从 1300 万条原始提取中筛选出 46 万条带有时间属性（如发病窗口、进展阶段）的证据关联，并附带可溯源的 PMID 和多信号可信度分数。

Result: ChronoMedKG 在与 Orphadata 的比对中达到 92.7% 的一致性，并为 6,250 种疾病提供了时间标注，填补了现有数据库的空白。实验表明，在 ChronoTQA 基准测试中，使用 ChronoMedKG 进行检索能使模型在时间相关问题上的性能显著提升，纠正了 47-65% 的长尾错误，远超传统的 HPOA-RAG 方法。

Conclusion: ChronoMedKG 通过引入时间维度，填补了现有生物医学知识图谱在纵向临床推理方面的空白。该图谱证明了在检索增强生成（RAG）系统中集成时间属性对于提升临床决策准确性的重要性，为未来构建更具动态感知的临床医疗系统奠定了基础。

Abstract: Biomedical knowledge graphs (KGs) treat disease associations as static facts, but temporal information is crucial for clinical reasoning, e.g., a symptom diagnostic of one disease at age 3 may imply a different disease at age 13. Existing KGs such as PrimeKG, Hetionet, and iKraph do not encode when a finding becomes clinically relevant over the course of a disease. This limits their usefulness for longitudinal clinical reasoning and retrieval augmentation.
  We introduce ChronoMedKG, a temporal biomedical knowledge graph that contains 460,497 evidence-linked triples (filtered from 13M raw extractions) covering 13,431 diseases. Each association is tied to temporal components like onset window or progression stage, which are backed by PMID-traceable evidence and a multi-signal credibility score. The graph is constructed through a disease-autonomous multi-agent pipeline in which multiple frontier LLMs independently extract knowledge from PubMed and PMC literature. Only those relations are kept that are supported by multi-model consensus, survive credibility filtering, as well as ontology alignment.
  ChronoMedKG scored 92.7% agreement against Orphadata and adds temporal grounding for 6,250 diseases absent from HPOA, Orphadata, and Phenopackets, including 1,657 Orphanet-coded rare diseases. We further introduce ChronoTQA, a benchmark of 3,341 questions across eight task types (six temporal plus two static controls), with a 12-question supplementary probe. Frontier LLMs lose roughly 30 points moving from static to temporal questions; ChronoMedKG retrieval rescues 47-65% of their long-tail failures, against 17-29% for HPOA-RAG. As such, ChronoMedKG provides a crucial temporal axis for retrieval-augmented clinical systems that was previously absent.

</details>


### [49] [Understanding Data Temporality Impact on Large Language Models Pre-training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22769)
*Pilchen Hippolyte,Fabre Romain,Signe Talla Franck,Perez Patrick,Grave Edouard*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入时间顺序预训练，在不损失通用能力的前提下，有效提升了大语言模型获取时效性事实知识的能力，打破了传统乱序预训练导致知识陈旧和时间感缺失的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型通常在乱序数据集上训练，导致其知识在训练结束后即被“冻结”，且模型对时间维度的理解非常有限。作者旨在探索训练数据的顺序对模型习得具有时效性事实知识的影响，从而解决模型知识滞后和时间定位不准的问题。

Method: 1. 构建了一个包含超过 7000 个时间维度事实问题（temporally grounded questions）的基准测试集及配套的评估协议。
2. 对比实验：在 6B 参数规模的模型上，对比了按时间顺序组织的 Common Crawl 快照训练（Sequentially trained）与传统的乱序预训练（Shuffled pre-training）。

Result: 1. 顺序训练的模型在通用语言理解和常识知识方面与乱序基线持平。
2. 顺序训练的模型在事实知识的最新性（freshness）和时间精确度方面表现显著更优。
3. 乱序训练倾向于“偏向”较旧的数据，这可能是由于数据中事实的重复出现导致旧知识被强化，而顺序训练能有效缓解这一偏差。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在预训练阶段引入时间顺序对于大语言模型获取时效性知识至关重要。与传统的乱序训练相比，按时间顺序训练不仅不会损害模型的通用语言能力，还能显著提升模型对事实知识的时间定位能力和时效性。这一发现为大语言模型的持续学习与知识更新提供了新的范式和理论支撑。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are typically trained on shuffled corpora, yielding models whose knowledge is frozen at train time and whose temporal grounding remains poorly understood. In this work, we study the impact of pre-training dynamics on the acquisition of time-sensitive factual knowledge, focusing specifically on data ordering. Our main contributions are twofold. First, we introduce a comprehensive benchmark of over 7,000 temporally grounded questions and an evaluation protocol that enables analysis of whether models correctly associate facts with their corresponding time periods. Second, we pretrain 6B-parameter models on temporally ordered Common Crawl snapshots and compare them against standard shuffled pre-training. Our results show that sequentially trained models match shuffled baselines on general language understanding and common knowledge while consistently exhibiting more up-to-date and temporally precise knowledge. Temporally ordered pre-training yields improved factual freshness, while shuffled pre-training peaks on older data, possibly due to increased factual repetition. These findings, along with the release of our code at https://github.com/kyutai-labs/kairos , checkpoints, and datasets at https://huggingface.co/collections/kyutai/kairos provide a foundation for future research on continual learning for LLMs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 提出了两种度量隐蔽偏见的指标：情感一致性（Sentiment Consistency）和有用性一致性（Helpfulness Consistency）；2. 引入了政治一致性训练（PCT），这是一种基于强化学习（RL）的训练方法，包含情感一致性训练和有用性一致性训练两个互补的范式。

Result: 实验结果表明，所提出的PCT方法能够显著降低隐蔽的政治偏见，同时保持模型整体的有用性，并且在未见过的基准测试中展现了良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过政治一致性训练（PCT），可以在不牺牲大模型整体有用性的前提下，显著降低其在处理敏感政治议题时的隐蔽性偏差，为构建更中立、客观的AI系统提供了有效的技术路径。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) exhibit systematic political bias across a variety of sensitive contexts. We find that LLMs handle counterpart topics from opposing political sides asymmetrically. We refer to this phenomenon as covert political bias and identify 7 categories of techniques through which it operates. We propose two metrics for covert bias: Sentiment Consistency measures symmetry in rhetoric and framing across paired political prompts; Helpfulness Consistency measures symmetric depth and engagement. To reduce both types of covert bias, we introduce Political Consistency Training (PCT), an RL training method with two complementary paradigms: Sentiment Consistency Training and Helpfulness Consistency Training. We show that PCT preserves overall helpfulness, substantially reduces covert political bias, and generalizes to held-out benchmarks. We release our work at https://political-manipulation.ai

### [51] [Evaluating Commercial AI Chatbots as News Intermediaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22785)
*Mirac Suzgun,Emily Shen,Federico Bianchi,Alexander Spangher,Thomas Icard,Daniel E. Ho,Dan Jurafsky,James Zou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究评估了六款主流AI聊天机器人在处理多语种、即时新闻事实时的表现，发现虽然模型整体准确率较高，但存在明显的语言区域偏见、检索环节薄弱以及极易受错误问题诱导等核心隐患。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI聊天机器人成为人们获取新闻的重要渠道，但此前尚无研究系统地评估这些系统（结合了专有搜索集成与检索-合成管线）在处理跨语言、跨地区突发事实时的准确性，以及它们在应对虚假信息和检索偏差方面的表现。

Method: 研究者在2026年2月9日至22日期间，针对六款AI聊天机器人（包括Gemini、Grok、Claude、GPT系列）进行了为期14天的评估。实验使用了2100个基于BBC六大区域（美加、阿拉伯、非洲、印地语、俄语、土耳其语）当天新闻报道的事实问题，通过多项选择和自由回答两种方式进行测试，并分析了模型在处理虚假前提问题时的表现。

Result: 1. 最优模型在多项选择题中准确率超过90%，但在自由回答中准确率下降11-13%。2. 存在显著的“英语中心”检索偏差，模型在处理印地语新闻时准确率最低。3. 超过70%的错误源于检索失败而非推理失败。4. 模型极易受到虚假前提问题的误导，且虚假信息检测能力与答案恢复能力之间存在悖论。

Conclusion: AI聊天机器人在处理即时新闻时展现了较高的准确率，但这种表现掩盖了系统性的区域不平等（如对印地语内容的支持不足）、对检索基础设施的极度依赖以及在面对含错误前提的问题时的脆弱性。研究强调，仅评估多项选择题无法全面反映模型的可靠性，未来的开发需要重点解决检索偏差和对虚假信息的甄别能力。

Abstract: AI chatbots are rapidly shaping how people encounter the news, yet no prior study has systematically measured how accurately these systems, with their proprietary search integrations and retrieval-synthesis pipelines, handle emerging facts across languages and regions. We present a 14-day (February 9-22, 2026) evaluation of six AI chatbots (Gemini 3 Flash and Pro, Grok 4, Claude 4.5 Sonnet, GPT-5 and GPT-4o mini) on 2,100 factual questions derived from same-day BBC News reporting across six regional services (US & Canada, Arabic, Afrique, Hindi, Russian, Turkish). The best systems achieve over 90% multiple-choice accuracy on questions about events reported hours earlier. The same systems, however, lose 11-13% under free-response evaluation, and 16-17% across the cohort. We further characterize three failure patterns. First, every model achieves its lowest accuracy on Hindi (79% vs. 89-91% elsewhere) and citations indicate an Anglophone retrieval bias (e.g., models answering Hindi queries cite English Wikipedia more than any Hindi outlet). Second, retrieval, not reasoning, failures drive over 70% of all errors. When models retrieve a correct source, they often extract the correct answer; the problem is to land on the right source in the first place. Third, models achieving 88-96% accuracy on well-formed questions drop to 19-70% when questions contain subtle false premises, with the most vulnerable model accepting fabricated facts 64% of the time. We also identify a detection-accuracy paradox: the best false-premise detector ranks second in adversarial accuracy (abstention rate), while a weaker detector ranks first, showing that premise detection and answer recovery are partially independent capabilities. Overall, these suggest that high accuracy can mask systematic regional inequity, near-total dependence on retrieval infrastructure, and vulnerability to imperfect queries real users pose.

### [52] [Tokenisation via Convex Relaxations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22821)
*Jan Tempus,Philip Whittington,Craig W. Schmidt,Dennis Komm,Tiago Pimentel*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: ConvexTok 是一种基于凸优化的词元化新算法，通过解决线性规划问题取代贪心策略，实现了更优的词汇表构建，显著提升了语言模型的压缩效率并接近全局最优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的词元化算法（如 BPE 和 Unigram）均采用贪心策略，在构建词汇表时仅做局部最优决策，缺乏对整体词汇表质量的全局考量。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ConvexTok 的词元化算法，将词元化器的构建过程重新表述为线性规划问题，并利用凸优化工具进行求解，而非使用传统的贪心算法（如 BPE 或 Unigram）。

Result: ConvexTok 在内部词元化指标和语言模型的字节比特数（BpB）上均优于传统方法；同时，该方法能提供相对于目标函数的理论下界，实验证明其词汇表质量在常用规模下与全局最优值差距小于 1%。在下游任务中，性能也有所提升，但表现不及压缩指标显著。

Conclusion: ConvexTok 提供了一种基于凸优化的词元化新范式，能够保证词元化结果接近全局最优，且在语言模型训练中展现出比贪心算法更优的压缩效率和部分任务性能提升。

Abstract: Tokenisation is an integral part of the current NLP pipeline. Current tokenisation algorithms such as BPE and Unigram are greedy algorithms -- they make locally optimal decisions without considering the resulting vocabulary as a whole. We instead formulate tokeniser construction as a linear program and solve it using convex optimisation tools, yielding a new algorithm we call ConvexTok. We find ConvexTok consistently improves intrinsic tokenisation metrics and the bits-per-byte (BpB) achieved by language models; it also improves downstream task performance, but less consistently. Furthermore, ConvexTok allows the user to certify how far their tokeniser is from optimal, with respect to a certain objective, via a lower bound, and we empirically find it to be within 1\% of optimal at common vocabulary sizes.

### [53] [From TF-IDF to Transformers: A Comparative and Ensemble Approach to Sentiment Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22003)
*Dip Biswas Shanto,Mitali Yadav,Prajwal Panth,Suresh Chandra Satapathy*

TL;DR: 本文对比了多种机器学习和深度学习模型在IMDb电影评论情感分析任务中的表现，发现RoBERTa模型效果最好（准确率93.02%），且集成学习方法能进一步提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电影评论文本包含丰富的意见信息，但传统的机器学习模型往往依赖于统计词表示，难以准确捕捉文本的深层语境和潜在情感。因此，本研究旨在探索并评估多种模型在电影评论情感极性分类任务中的表现。

Method: 研究采用了多种机器学习和深度学习方法，包括朴素贝叶斯、逻辑回归、SVM、LightGBM、LSTM以及基于Transformer的RoBERTa和DistilBERT模型。预处理阶段使用了NLP相关技术，最终通过准确率、精确率、召回率、F1分数和ROC-AUC等指标进行评估，并引入了软投票集成学习方法。

Result: 在IMDb数据集上的实验表明，RoBERTa模型取得了最佳表现，准确率达到93.02%。同时，通过将多个模型结合的软投票集成方法，进一步优化了情感分类的整体性能。

Conclusion: RoBERTa在电影评论情感分析任务中展现出卓越的性能，证明了预训练Transformer模型在处理自然语言语境方面的优势。此外，软投票集成学习策略能够有效整合不同模型的长处，进一步提升分类准确度。

Abstract: Sentiment analysis, also referred to as opinion mining, primarily tries to extract opinion from any text-based data. In the context of movie reviews and critics, sentimental analysis can be a helpful tool to predict whether a movie review is generally positive or negative. It can be difficult for the ML models to understand the context or metaphysical sentiment accurately, as ML models rely largely on statistical word representations. The objective of this paper is to examine and categorise movie reviews into positive and negative sentiments. Diverse machine learning models are considered in doing so, and Natural Language Processing (NLP) methodologies are employed for data preprocessing and model assessment. The IMDb dataset is used. Specifically, Naive Bayes, Logistic Regression, Support Vector Machines (SVM), LightGBM, LSTM, and transformer-based models such as RoBERTa and DistilBERT were evaluated. After a lot of testing with accuracy, precision, recall, F1-score, and ROC-AUC, RoBERTa performed better than all the other models, with an accuracy of 93.02%. A soft voting ensemble that combined all the models also improved classification performance, showing that model ensembling works well for sentiment analysis.

</details>

### [54] [Temporal Contrastive Transformer for Financial Crime Detection: Self-Supervised Sequence Embeddings via Predictive Contrastive Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21490)
*Danny Butvinik,Yonit Marcus,Nitzan Tal,Gabrielle Azoulay*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于对比学习的时序转换器模型（TCT），用于从金融交易数据中自动提取特征。虽然TCT能有效捕捉时序行为模式，但在现有强特征工程基线之上，尚未表现出显著的增量价值，说明其学习到的表征与手工特征高度重合，但具有减少人工特征工程需求的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融欺诈检测高度依赖复杂的人工特征工程，耗时且难以捕捉深层的时序行为动态。研究旨在通过自监督学习方法自动挖掘序列数据中的行为模式，以减轻对人工特征的依赖并提升检测性能。

Method: 提出了时序对比转换器（Temporal Contrastive Transformer, TCT），利用自监督对比学习目标训练模型，旨在从金融交易序列中学习并编码时序行为特征，并将所学习的嵌入向量输入到梯度提升分类器中进行下游的欺诈检测评估。

Result: 实验结果显示，TCT学习到的表征具有显著的预测能力（AUC 0.8644）；但在与现有的强基线特征结合使用时，相比纯手工特征基线（AUC 0.9205 vs 0.9245），并未观察到明显的性能提升，表明学到的表征与现有特征在信息上存在高度重叠。

Conclusion: TCT作为一种时序表征学习框架，能够有效捕捉金融交易中的行为模式并近似替代部分人工特征工程。尽管目前在强基线模型上尚未实现显著的性能叠加，但它证明了无需手动工程即可提取有效特征的潜力，为降低金融犯罪检测对领域专家特征的依赖提供了重要的研究方向。

Abstract: We introduce the Temporal Contrastive Transformer (TCT), a representation learning framework designed to capture contextual temporal dynamics in sequences of financial transactions. The model is trained using a self-supervised contrastive objective to produce embeddings that encode behavioral patterns over time, with the goal of supporting downstream fraud detection tasks. We evaluate TCT in a realistic setting by using the learned embeddings as input features to a gradient boosting classifier. Experimental results show that embeddings alone achieve meaningful predictive performance (AUC 0.8644), indicating that the model captures non-trivial temporal structure. However, when combined with domain-engineered features, no measurable improvement is observed over the baseline (AUC 0.9205 vs. 0.9245), suggesting that the learned representations largely overlap with existing feature abstractions. These findings position TCT as a promising representation learning approach that captures relevant behavioral signal, while highlighting the challenges of achieving additive value over strong domain features. The results reflect an intermediate stage in the development of temporal representation learning for financial crime detection and motivate further research on model architecture, training objectives, and integration strategies. At this early stage, achieving performance comparable to a strong feature-engineered baseline is itself a meaningful outcome, indicating that learned representations approximate domain-specific features without manual engineering. While not yet production-ready, these results point to a promising direction for reducing reliance on feature engineering in financial crime detection.

</details>


### [55] [A Reproducible Log-Driven AutoML Framework for Interpretable Pipeline Optimization in Healthcare Risk Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21528)
*Rui Huang,Lican Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个名为 yvsoucom-iterkit 的自动化机器学习框架，通过确定性日志记录实现了疾病预测流水线的全链路可追踪与优化，揭示了算法性能主要由极少数关键组件驱动，并有效降低了搜索空间的冗余度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 疾病风险预测面临特征异构、样本量有限及严重的类别不平衡问题，目前的机器学习预测方法往往缺乏准确性和可重复性，且缺乏对流水线中各组件贡献度的深度洞察。

Method: 提出了一种名为 yvsoucom-iterkit 的确定性、日志驱动的自动机器学习框架。该框架将流水线优化建模为可追踪的配置级系统，支持组件归因分析、交互分析、组件相似度度量以及跨种子（cross-seed）鲁棒性评估。通过在 Pima Indians Diabetes 和 Stroke 数据集上运行超过 18,000 种流水线配置进行实证研究。

Result: 实验发现搜索空间存在结构性冗余，性能主要由少数关键组件决定。Pima 数据集中，数据增强（0.454）、模型选择（0.198）和不平衡处理（0.101）是关键驱动因素；在 Stroke 数据集中，不平衡处理（0.406）占主导地位。分析还量化了组件间的冗余度（如某些特征选择算法和增强方法效果相似），并验证了集成模型在性能与鲁棒性（变异度 0.023-0.026）上的优越性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，有效的自动机器学习（AutoML）优化可以聚焦于少数高影响力的组件，而非全空间的盲目搜索。通过识别关键驱动因素和冗余组件，研究人员可以构建更可解释、可重复且鲁棒性更强的疾病预测模型。

Abstract: Accurate and reproducible disease risk prediction remains challenging due to heterogeneous features, limited samples, and severe class imbalance. This study introduces yvsoucom-iterkit, a deterministic and log-driven automated machine learning framework that formulates pipeline optimization as a fully reproducible, configuration-level system. Each pipeline is encoded as a traceable log entity, enabling analysis of component attribution, interactions, similarity, and cross-seed robustness. Experiments on the Pima Indians Diabetes and Stroke datasets across more than 18,000 pipeline configurations reveal a structured and partially redundant search space, where performance is governed by a small subset of interacting components. Random Forest importance analysis identifies augmentation (0.454), model choice (0.198), and imbalance handling (0.101) as key drivers on Pima, while imbalance handling dominates Stroke (0.406). Component similarity analysis shows strong redundancy, with feature selection variants (biMax-biMean) exhibiting low RMS distance (0.0252), mixup closely matching no augmentation (0.0279), and TomekLinks aligning with no imbalance handling (0.0325), whereas Gaussian noise shows greater divergence from no augmentation (0.10). The framework achieves strong and stable performance using ensemble models (Weighted-F1 0.89, Macro-F1 0.88 on Pima; Weighted-F1 0.94 on Stroke), while Macro-F1 remains lower on Stroke (0.67) due to class imbalance. Cross-seed analysis reveals a performance-robustness trade-off, with ensembles showing lower variability (0.023-0.026) than SVM. These results indicate that effective AutoML optimization can focus on a reduced set of high-impact components.

### [56] [Provable Joint Decontamination for Benchmarking Multiple Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21543)
*Zhenlong Liu,Hao Zeng,Hongxin Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型评估中的基准数据污染挑战，本文提出了一种名为JECS的共形选择方法，通过联合统计处理实现对跨模型全局污染率的严格控制，解决了现有方法在模型对比时缺乏公平性和理论保证的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型评估中普遍存在基准数据污染问题，导致性能虚高。现有的基于得分的检测方法缺乏理论保证，而传统的单模型共形预测方法在跨模型比较时会导致不公平。因此，需要一种能够提供理论保证且适用于跨模型全局评估的去污染方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“联合包络共形选择”（Joint Envelope Conformal Selection, JECS）的框架。该方法首先计算每个模型的共形p值，通过逐项取最大值进行聚合；接着从数据驱动阈值以上的右尾观测值中重构最大p值零分布的保守包络；最后应用自适应Benjamini-Hochberg（BH）过程对重缩放后的值进行处理，以实现对全球污染率的严格控制。

Result: 广泛的实验表明，与传统的max-p基线相比，JECS在维持目标全球污染率（GCR）控制的同时，展现出了更高的污染检测效能（power），能更可靠地识别出受污染的基准测试样本。

Conclusion: 本文提出的JECS方法通过联合选择策略，有效解决了大语言模型评估中的基准测试污染问题，在保证全球污染率（GCR）的前提下，提高了识别污染数据的统计功效，为跨模型比较的公平性提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: Benchmark data contamination has become a central challenge in LLM evaluation: when evaluation examples appear in the training data of one or more audited models, reported performance can be inflated and cross-model comparisons become unreliable. A broad line of training-data detection work designs scores to quantify how strongly a model memorizes a given data point, but these score-based methods lack theoretical guarantees. Recent conformal approaches provide provable false-identification control for a single model; however, applying them separately to each model can produce model-specific benchmarks, undermining fair comparison across models. In this work, we formalize multi-model benchmark decontamination as a joint selection problem and propose Joint Envelope Conformal Selection (JECS), a conformal procedure that enables global contamination rate (GCR) control under stated assumptions. Specifically, JECS computes per-model conformal p-values, aggregates them by the per-item maximum, and reconstructs a conservative envelope of the max-p null distribution from right-tail observations above a data-driven threshold. By applying the adaptive Benjamini-Hochberg (BH) procedure to the envelope-rescaled values, we select a benchmark with provable GCR control. Extensive experiments across various models and benchmarks demonstrate that JECS achieves higher power than the max-p baseline while consistently maintaining the target GCR control.

</details>


### [57] [Calibration, Uncertainty Communication, and Deployment Readiness in CKD Risk Prediction: A Framework Evaluation Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21566)
*Michael O. Eniolade*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究指出，CKD预测模型在内部数据上的“完美”表现无法泛化到外部数据。在临床部署前，必须优先评估模型的校准能力和不确定性，而非仅仅依赖准确率等区分指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的慢性肾脏病（CKD）机器学习预测模型往往过度关注区分度（如AUROC），而忽视了概率输出的校准质量和不确定性量化，导致临床医生无法判断模型预测结果的可靠性。

Method: 研究人员在UCI CKD数据集上训练了五种分类器（逻辑回归、随机森林、XGBoost、带Platt缩放的SVM、高斯朴素贝叶斯），并利用Platt缩放和等渗回归进行校准。同时，通过分裂一致性预测（split conformal prediction）进行不确定性量化，并引入八项指标的部署就绪框架。最后，利用MIMIC-IV演示数据集进行分布偏移和特征缺失下的压力测试。

Result: 所有模型在内部UCI测试集中表现极佳（AUROC达1.00），但迁移到MIMIC-IV数据集后性能显著下降：AUROC跌至0.48-0.58，校准误差（ECE）升高，一致性预测覆盖率大幅低于预期的90%。此外，没有模型在部署就绪框架中得分超过4分（满分16分）。

Conclusion: 在临床预测模型部署前，仅依赖内部数据集的评估是不够的。必须对校准稳定性和一致性预测覆盖率进行外部数据验证，以评估模型在实际临床环境中的鲁棒性与可靠性。

Abstract: Machine learning models for chronic kidney disease (CKD) risk prediction often post strong discrimination scores on internal test sets. Calibration and uncertainty quantification get far less attention, leaving clinicians without reliable information about whether the probability outputs are accurate.
  We trained five classifiers on the UCI CKD dataset (400 patients, 62.5% CKD prevalence): logistic regression, random forest, XGBoost, SVM with Platt scaling, and Gaussian naive Bayes. We evaluated each across calibration quality, conformal prediction coverage, and an eight-criterion deployment readiness framework. A distributional stress-test applied the best-calibrated variant of each model to the open-access MIMIC-IV demo cohort (97 patients, 23.7% CKD) to assess behaviour under prevalence shift and feature missingness. We measured calibration before and after Platt scaling and isotonic regression using Expected Calibration Error and Brier Score, and quantified uncertainty through split conformal prediction targeting 90% marginal coverage.
  All five models reached AUROC 1.00 on the UCI test set. Isotonic recalibration reduced internal ECE to 0.000-0.022. On MIMIC-IV, AUROC fell to 0.48-0.58, ECE rose to 0.68-0.76, and conformal coverage dropped from 0.80-0.98 to 0.21-0.25 against a 90% target. No model scored above 4 out of 16 on the deployment readiness checklist.
  Near-perfect internal performance did not transfer. Calibration stability and conformal coverage should be evaluated on external data before any clinical prediction model moves toward deployment.

</details>


### [58] [ConTact: Contact-First Antibody CDR Design via Explicit Interface Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21600)
*Mansoor Ahmed,Spencer VonBank,Nadeem Taj,Sujin Lee,Naila Jan,Murray Patterson*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ConTact 是一种新型抗体 CDR 设计架构，通过显式预测抗体-抗原接触关系并针对性地优化关键位点，显著提升了抗体结构的准确性和表位结合能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的计算抗体 CDR 设计方法未能区分“识别接触位点”与“确定氨基酸序列”这两个本质不同的子问题，导致模型在处理时将抗原信号均匀分布在所有位置，从而削弱了对关键结合区域的关注。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ConTact 的“先接触后行动”（contact-then-act）架构，包含三个级联阶段：学习表面互补特征、预测 CDR-抗原接触点、以及注入接触门控后的抗原特征。此外，引入了距离偏置交叉注意力机制（distance-biased cross-attention）以利用几何先验，并使用接触加权交叉熵损失函数来增强关键位点的学习。

Result: 在 CHIMERA-Bench 数据集上，ConTact 取得了显著优势：结构质量提升了 7%（RMSD），表位感知能力（F1 分数）比 GNN 基准模型高出 10%，并在 CDR-H3 序列恢复率（AAR 0.38）方面表现出极强的竞争力。

Conclusion: ConTact 通过将 CDR 设计分解为“接触预测”和“序列生成”两个阶段，成功解决了以往架构中抗原信号被稀释的问题，证明了显式建模接触关系对提升抗体设计性能至关重要。

Abstract: Computational antibody CDR design methods condition on antigen structure to generate binding loops, yet existing architectures conflate two fundamentally distinct sub-problems: identifying which CDR positions will contact the antigen, and selecting amino acids at those positions. This conflation forces models to learn contact reasoning implicitly through uniform message passing, diluting antigen signal across all positions equally. We introduce ConTact, a contact-then-act architecture that explicitly decomposes CDR design into three cascaded stages: learning surface complementarity fingerprints, predicting CDR-antigen contacts, and injecting contact-gated antigen features into the sequence head. A distance-biased cross-attention module encodes geometric priors favoring spatial neighbors, while a contact-weighted cross-entropy loss concentrates gradient signal on binding-critical positions. On CHIMERA-Bench dataset, ConTact achieves the best structural quality (7% RMSD improvement over the next-best baseline), best epitope awareness (10% F1 score over GNN baselines), and competitive sequence recovery (AAR 0.38) among several CDR-H3 design baselines.

</details>


### [59] [When Are Teacher Tokens Reliable? Position-Weighted On-Policy Self-Distillation for Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21606)
*Xiaogeng Liu,Xinyan Wang,Yingzi Ma,Yechao Zhang,Chaowei Xiao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发现推理任务中教师模型的可靠性与序列位置高度相关，并据此提出了“位置加权在线策略自蒸馏”（PW-OPSD）算法，在不增加额外计算开销的前提下，显著提升了模型的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）方法将所有生成的词元视为同等可靠，而现有的基于熵的调整方法无法有效区分教师在推理过程中表现出的“不确定性”与“多样性”，导致监督信号存在噪声。因此，需要一种更有效的方法来判断教师生成内容在不同推理阶段的可靠性。

Method: 1. 引入“分支可行性诊断”（branch-viability diagnostic）：通过在不同步骤强制执行教师的候选项，验证其对最终正确答案的影响，以此评估教师预测的可靠性。
2. 提出“位置加权策略”（PW-OPSD）：发现推理过程中后期的预测更为关键，因此在策略蒸馏中引入随序列位置增加而增长的权重，对不同的预测位置进行差异化监督。

Result: 1. 分支可行性诊断发现，序列中的位置信息是衡量教师可靠性的最强指标（AUROC达到0.83），远高于局部熵指标（0.57）。
2. 在Qwen3-4B模型上应用PW-OPSD，在AIME 2024和2025竞赛数据集上分别提升了1.0和1.1个点。
3. 在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B和Olmo-3-7B-Think模型上的泛化实验也证明了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 教师模型在推理任务中的置信度具有轨迹结构特性，而非单纯取决于局部的不确定性。利用“基于位置的加权”策略，无需增加额外的教师推理成本，即可显著提升学生模型的学习效果和性能。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) trains a student on its own rollouts using a privileged teacher, but its standard objective weights all generated tokens equally, implicitly treating the privileged teacher target as equally reliable at every student-visited prefix. Existing entropy-based OPD methods relax this uniformity by modulating token-level supervision with teacher entropy, but high teacher entropy in reasoning has an ambiguous reliability meaning: it can reflect either non-viable uncertainty or benign solution diversity. To identify this phenomenon, we introduce a branch-viability diagnostic. Specifically, we record next-token alternatives from the privileged-answer teacher prompt, force each alternative after the student prompt plus its on-policy spine prefix, and test whether the resulting student-template continuation recovers the correct answer. On Qwen3-4B, we find that an oriented within-sequence position score is the strongest tested predictor of teacher-token reliability, reaching an area-under-ROC-curve (AUROC) of 0.83; local uncertainty scores are at most 0.57. Motivated by this trajectory-level structure, we propose Position-Weighted On-Policy Self-Distillation (PW-OPSD), which applies an increasing position weight while keeping the same student rollout, privileged teacher pass, and clipped forward-KL target as OPSD. In our comprehensive evaluations with different random seeds, the diagnostic-derived PW-OPSD improves AIME 2024 and AIME 2025 Avg@12 by +1.0 and +1.1 points, and a generalization evaluation on two larger-scale models from different families, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B and Olmo-3-7B-Think, also demonstrates consistent aggregate Avg@12 improvements. These results show that teacher-token reliability in reasoning distillation is trajectory-structured and can be utilized without additional teacher computation.

</details>


### [60] [$\textit{BlockFormer}$ : Transformer-based inference from interaction maps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21617)
*Eloïse Touron,Pedro L. C. Rodrigues,Julyan Arbel,Nelle Varoquaux,Michael Arbel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种基于Transformer和合成数据训练的通用深度学习模型，有效解决了Hi-C交互图中因实体大小和数量变异导致的着丝粒定位难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基因组交互图（如Hi-C）分析中，识别特定结构（如着丝粒）通常被视为一个逆问题。然而，由于不同物种或样本中基因组实体的数量和尺寸存在高度可变性，传统的分析方法难以通用。因此，需要一种能够处理这种变异性并利用数据驱动方式解决此类逆问题的方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于Transformer架构的深度学习模型，该模型能够处理交互图中实体数量和大小的变化。同时，设计了一个自定义模拟器生成大量的合成数据，用于训练模型以学习地图间共享的结构和局部模式。

Result: 该方法成功应用于着丝粒定位任务，能够准确地在具有不同基因组大小的多种物种中恢复着丝粒的基因组位置。

Conclusion: 本研究证明了利用基于Transformer的数据驱动方法，通过模拟数据进行训练，可以有效且通用地解决基因组交互图中的逆问题，如跨物种的着丝粒定位。

Abstract: Inference from interaction maps, such as centromere identification from genome-wide chromosome conformation capture techniques -- notably Hi-C -- can be formulated as a generic inverse problem: infer a set of parameters given a map summarizing pairwise interactions between entities through blocks of variable numbers and sizes. In this work, we introduce a data-driven approach that leverages shared structure between these maps, such as global alignment between localized patterns, while handling the variability in number and size of entities arising in real-world data. Our approach relies on a transformer architecture capable of handling such variability and a custom simulator to generate abundant, yet computationally cheap synthetic data for training. Applied to the problem of centromere localization, the method accurately recovers their genomic positions across a wide range of species of various genome sizes.

</details>


### [61] [EntmaxKV: Support-Aware Decoding for Entmax Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21649)
*Gonçalo Duarte,Miguel Couceiro,Marcos V. Treviso*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 EntmaxKV 框架，通过利用 $\alpha$-entmax 的数学特性实现长上下文解码中的真正稀疏化，在加载 KV 缓存前即进行页面过滤，大幅降低内存访问开销，在保持推理精度的同时显著提升了长文本模型的运行速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型长上下文推理面临严重的 KV-cache 内存带宽瓶颈。传统的 Softmax 注意力因其长尾分布特性难以实现真正的稀疏化，导致即便采用了稀疏解码方法，仍需加载完整的 KV 缓存，无法从根本上解决内存读取压力。因此，作者希望利用 $\alpha$-entmax 产生的真实零值特性，实现真正意义上的稀疏解码。

Method: 1. 引入 EntmaxKV 框架，将 $\alpha$-entmax 的稀疏性整合至自回归解码中。
2. 设计查询感知（query-aware）页面评分机制，在加载 KV 页面前评估重要性。
3. 提出支持感知（support-aware）的候选选择策略，结合 Gaussian-aware 采样器动态估计 entmax 阈值。
4. 在计算注意力前直接根据预选的稀疏集过滤 KV 数据，从而减少内存带宽开销。

Result: 在 1M 上下文长度的基准测试中，EntmaxKV 在保持极低输出误差的前提下，实现了较全量注意力最高 5.43 倍的速度提升。相比于传统的 Softmax 稀疏方法，该方法在相同的 KV 缓存预算下，能够捕获更多的概率质量并保留更多关键 Token，表现出更高的计算效率。

Conclusion: EntmaxKV 证明了在长文本推理中，利用 $\alpha$-entmax 的稀疏特性可以有效突破 KV-cache 内存带宽限制。该框架通过提前预判稀疏支持集，在几乎不损失模型精度的情况下，实现了显著的推理速度提升，为长上下文大模型的高效部署提供了新路径。

Abstract: Long-context decoding is increasingly limited by KV-cache memory traffic since each generated token attends over a cache whose size grows linearly with context length. Existing sparse decoding methods reduce this cost by selecting subsets of tokens or pages, but are designed for softmax attention, whose dense tails make any truncation discard nonzero probability mass. In contrast, $α$-entmax produces exact zeros, turning sparse decoding from dense-tail approximation into support recovery: if the selected candidates contain the entmax support, sparse decoding remains exact. While recent entmax kernels enable efficient training, they do not address the autoregressive decoding bottleneck, where dense inference still streams the full KV cache before sparsity is known. In this work, we introduce EntmaxKV, an entmax-native sparse decoding framework that exploits sparsity before KV pages are loaded. EntmaxKV combines query-aware page scoring, support-aware candidate selection, and sparse entmax attention. We analyze truncation error through the dropped probability mass $δ$, showing that output error is controlled by $δ$ and vanishes when the entmax support is recovered. We further introduce a Gaussian-aware entmax selector that estimates the entmax threshold from lightweight page statistics, adapting the selected budget to the score distribution. Empirically, EntmaxKV drops less probability mass, retains more support tokens, and achieves lower output error than softmax-based sparse decoding at matched KV budgets. On long-context and language modeling benchmarks, it closely matches full-cache entmax while using a small fraction of the KV cache, achieving up to $3.36\times$ (softmax) and $5.43\times$ (entmax) speedup over full attention baselines at 1M context length. Code available at: https://github.com/deep-spin/entmaxkv.

</details>


### [62] [Amplifying, Not Learning: Fine-Tuned AI Text Detectors Amplify a Pretrained Direction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21653)
*Alexander Smirnov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AI文本检测器并非真的在分辨人机，而是在识别文本是否符合AI预训练模型的“典型分布”。研究揭示了检测器的核心在于典型性轴，并提出了一种基于雅可比矩阵的高效干预方法，同时指出当前主流的微调手段大多只是概率校准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的AI文本检测器往往被视为能够构建“人与AI”的决策边界，但其实际机制不明。本研究旨在验证AI文本检测器实际上是在放大预训练模型中的“典型性”轴，并探究这种机制对检测准确性、偏差表现及模型干预的影响。

Method: 1. 利用原始预训练编码器的向量空间，通过计算AI文本与人类文本的质心投影轴进行分类；2. 通过24样本的冻结探测（Frozen Probe）与全参数微调进行对比；3. 引入闭式雅可比预测器（Closed-form Jacobian Predictor）来解析并干预模型的判定轴；4. 使用三种操作上截然不同的探针（文本表面统计残留、几何符号-epsilon消融、文本对预测器）验证观测的一致性。

Result: 1. 在未经任务监督的原始编码器上，简单的质心投影即可达到甚至超过微调模型的判别性能（如RoBERTa-base上表现更优）；2. 该轴在非母语写作中会发生反转（AUROC极低）；3. 通过干预雅可比矩阵，可以将检测器的召回率（TPR）从0提升至0.9以上，且能有效减少误报率（FPR）；4. 验证了现有的偏差修正方法（如LoRA或校准）本质上大多是校准偏移而非学习到了新的特征表达。

Conclusion: AI文本检测器的本质是“典型性（Typicality）”度量，而非区分人机创作的分类边界。研究证明，这种基于典型性的检测器在处理非母语英语（ESL）文本时会出现失效，且现有的微调和偏差干预方法本质上仅是在进行概率校准，而非学习新的判别特征。

Abstract: AI text detectors amplify a pretrained typicality axis; they do not construct an AI-vs-human boundary. On raw encoders before any task supervision, projecting onto centroid(AI)-centroid(HC3) achieves NYT-vs-HC3 AUROC 0.806/0.944/0.834 across three architectures (86-106% of the fine-tuned discrimination ceiling: on RoBERTa-base, raw projection exceeds fine-tuning); on RoBERTa-base, full fine-tuning reduces discrimination below raw on both fluent-formal populations tested. The same axis inverts on non-native ESL writing (AUROC 0.06-0.20) -- a falsifiable prediction unique to the typicality reading. A 24-example frozen probe matches full fine-tuning (0.900 vs 0.895). A closed-form Jacobian predictor parameterises axis-manipulating interventions with R^2 = 1.000 universal, lifts ELECTRA-CE deployment TPR from 0.000 to 0.904 at FPR = 1%, and transfers to three independently-trained third-party RoBERTa detectors at 16/16 oracle-equivalence (57% NYT-FPR reduction on the OpenAI detector). Scope: encoder family; mechanism magnitude HC3-anchored; population-level shared axis with per-text mechanisms varying across architectures. Three operationally distinct probes -- text-surface caps_rate residualisation, geometric signed-epsilon ablation, closed-form text-pair predictor -- agree at cos 0.74/0.81/1.00 across three architectures, confirming observer-invariance. Under matched-TPR-0.90 evaluation, the published intervention zoo (CC, dealign-f2c) is calibration-equivalent across 27 cells (|Delta AUROC| <= 0.0081), and >= 97% of the LoRA->full-FT bias gap on ELECTRA is calibration shift, not learned representation -- the central claim's prediction confirmed.

### [63] [Value-Gradient Hypothesis of RL for LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21654)
*Arip Asadulaev,Daniil Ognev,Karim Salta,Martin Takac*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文从价值梯度的视角揭示了PPO/GRPO等无评论员强化学习算法在大模型后训练中为何有效，并提出了一种预测强化学习增益的理论评估标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管PPO、GRPO等无评论员强化学习方法在提升大模型性能方面表现显著，但其成功背后的理论依据尚不明确，且缺乏对该类方法在何种阶段或条件下能产生最大收益的系统性分析。

Method: 作者采用价值梯度视角（value-gradient perspective）进行理论推导。首先，利用可微分推出（differentiable rollout）和加性噪声参数化模型，证明了执行者（actor）的更新在期望上等价于价值梯度；其次，针对离散Transformer策略，分析了反向传播过程，指出自动微分产生的经验代价状态（empirical costates）近似于价值信号，并量化了其误差界限。

Result: 研究发现，在大模型后训练的无评论员强化学习中，反向传播传播的代价状态（costates）本质上是在估计价值梯度。研究还提出了一套将强化学习影响分解为“价值梯度信号”与“可达奖励空间（reward headroom）”的评估框架，能够有效判断强化学习在预训练路径的哪一阶段最能发挥作用。

Conclusion: 本文通过价值梯度视角揭示了无评论员（critic-free）强化学习算法在大型语言模型后训练中的底层机制，建立了策略梯度与价值梯度之间的理论联系，并提出了预测强化学习效能的量化判据。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning substantially improves pretrained language models, but it remains understudied why critic-free methods such as PPO and GRPO work as well as they do, and when they should provide the largest gains. We develop a value-gradient perspective of critic-free RL for LLM post-training. First, under a differentiable rollout and additive-noise parameterization, we show that the actor update is value-gradient-like in expectation: the backward pass propagates costates whose conditional expectation equals the value gradient. Second, for discrete transformer policies, we show that autodifferentiation through attention produces empirical costates that approximate this value signal, with an error controlled by the sampling gap and policy entropy. These results motivate a decomposition of RL impact into value gradient signal and reachable reward headroom, yielding a criterion for when RL should be most effective along a pretraining trajectory.

### [64] [Hierarchical Variational Policies for Reward-Guided Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21661)
*Kushagra Pandey,Farrin Marouf Sofian,Jan Niklas Groeneveld,Felix Draxler,Stephan Mandt*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分层变分推理的扩散模型摊销采样框架，通过学习轻量级随机策略取代昂贵的在线测试时优化，在大幅降低推理延迟的同时实现了高质量的奖励对齐生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练扩散模型在解决下游任务（如反问题）时，通常需要昂贵的测试时引导或迭代优化，导致推理成本极高。作者旨在寻找一种能够大幅降低推理成本，同时保持高质量奖励对齐采样效果的通用框架。

Method: 本文提出了一种将测试时自适应建模为“分层变分模型”的方法。具体而言，该方法将控制逻辑摊销为一个轻量级且具备表达能力的随机策略。该策略能够在扩散采样的每一步提供结构化的控制，从而支持大步长的少步采样，并在必要时结合少量的测试时优化（半摊销模式）以进一步提升生成质量。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在4倍超分辨率任务中，不仅实现了比现有最优基线更好的感知质量，而且推理速度提升了5倍以上。在多种具有挑战性的反问题中，该方法展现了卓越的质量-速度权衡，并在半摊销模式下达到了领域内最先进的性能水平。

Conclusion: 本文提出的分层变分框架成功将扩散模型的测试时自适应过程从昂贵的在线优化转化为高效的策略推断。该方法在保证高质量生成的同时，极大地降低了推理所需的计算成本，为奖励对齐的扩散采样提供了高效且可扩展的新方案。

Abstract: Adapting pretrained diffusion models to downstream objectives such as inverse problems often requires expensive test-time guidance or optimization. We propose a principled framework for generating high-quality reward-aligned samples at substantially reduced inference cost. Our approach formulates test-time adaptation as a hierarchical variational model, where control is amortized into a lightweight yet expressive stochastic policy. This formulation naturally supports few-step diffusion sampling: large step sizes enable fast inference, while the learned policy maintains sample quality by providing structured per-step control. The resulting fully amortized sampler achieves a strong quality--speed tradeoff, matching or exceeding recent test-time scaling baselines while requiring significantly less compute. For example, on 4x super-resolution, our method achieves better perceptual quality with more than 5x faster inference compared to the best-performing baseline. We further extend our approach to a semi-amortized regime that combines cheap amortized proposals with limited test-time optimization, achieving state-of-the-art perceptual quality across several challenging inverse problems.

### [65] [I-SAFE: Wasserstein Coherence Metrics for Structural Auditing of Scientific AI Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21731)
*Barbara Tarantino,Gennaro Auricchio,Paolo Giudici*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对科学AI模型可能存在预测捷径的问题，本研究提出了I-SAFE审计框架，通过结构化的输入扰动和多维相干度量，评估模型行为是否符合领域知识，从而超越了传统的准确率评估维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学预测中深度学习模型往往利用“捷径”而非领域知识，仅凭基准测试的高准确率难以保证模型行为的科学合理性，需要更深入的审计工具。

Method: 提出I-SAFE框架，利用Wasserstein相干度量（WCM）及基于领域结构先验的输入扰动，对黑盒模型进行事后分布审计。包含三种度量指标：QBM（位置相干性）、WCM（顺序相干性）和转换不变WCM（形状相干性）。

Result: 在药物-靶点相互作用（DTI）任务中，I-SAFE成功揭示了DeepConvDTI、DeepDTA和TAPB等模型在准确率相近的情况下存在显著不同的分布响应特征，证明了该框架能捕捉到基于准确率无法识别的潜在模型行为差异。

Conclusion: I-SAFE框架能够通过分布审计揭示模型在准确率指标之外的内在行为差异，为评估科学AI模型的可靠性提供了一种与模型无关、基于领域先验的通用方法。

Abstract: Deep learning models are increasingly used in scientific prediction tasks where strong benchmark performance is often interpreted as evidence of scientifically meaningful behavior. This interpretation is fragile, as models may exploit shortcut features, dataset-specific regularities, or distributional biases that are predictive on held-out data but not aligned with domain-relevant structure. To address this limitation, we introduce the \textsc{I-SAFE} (Interventional Secure, Accurate, Fair and Explainable) framework, a post-hoc distributional auditing framework for scientific AI models centered on the Wasserstein Coherence Metric (WCM). Given a trained black-box predictor and an external structural prior encoding domain knowledge about task-relevant input structure, \textsc{I-SAFE} evaluates raw model outputs under structurally guided perturbations of the input. The proposed audit measures output-distribution coherence through three complementary metrics: a Quantile-Based Metric (QBM) for location-level coherence, the WCM for ordinal coherence, and a translation-invariant WCM variant for shape coherence. We instantiate \textsc{I-SAFE} on drug--target interaction (DTI) prediction using the Davis kinase benchmark, KLIFS (Kinase--Ligand Interaction Fingerprints and Structures) binding-pocket annotations, and three sequence-based DTI models: DeepConvDTI, DeepDTA, and TAPB. Although the models operate in a comparable predictive regime, \textsc{I-SAFE} reveals substantially different distributional response profiles, a distinction invisible to accuracy-based evaluation. The framework is model-agnostic and applicable to any domain where inputs admit a structured decomposition and an external prior is available.

*Samuel McDowell,Nathan Stromberg,Lalitha Sankar*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Prior-data fitted networks (PFNs) have achieved exceptional performance on tabular classification tasks. We have adapted several classical techniques addressing class imbalance and analyzed their performance on PFN classification. We observe that thresholding performs exceptionally well because of the calibration characteristics of PFNs, and downsampling performs comparably because of PFNs exceptional limited-data performance, with the additional benefit of reduced computation cost for inference.

Among 987 patients, 89 (9%) were positive for myocardial ischemia. The final model incorporated the Agatston score, eight calcium-omics features, and age. The proposed model achieved a precision of 98.9+/-3.0%, sensitivity of 79.2+/-8.4, and F1 score of 87.7+/-5.3%. The addition of calcium-omics features significantly improved predictive performance compared with models using clinical variables alone or clinical variables with the Agatston score (p<0.05). Interestingly, the number of calcified arteries, despite being the lowest-ranked feature based on SHAP analysis, showed the strongest association with myocardial ischemia in logistic regression analysis (odds ratio: 3.63, 95% confidence interval: 2.80-4.77, p<0.00001). *Zhiqi Gao,Albert Ge,Alexander Berenbeim,Nathaniel D. Bastian,Frederic Sala*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了“有效绑定极限”概念，指出了大模型在文本到优化任务中处理大规模数据时的不足，并开发了BIND方法，通过将数据处理与建模逻辑解耦，显著提升了模型求解数学优化问题的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本到优化（Text-to-Optimization）任务涉及模型架构设计（建模）与数据绑定（绑定）两个核心能力。现有大模型在处理复杂或大规模实例数据时，尽管建模逻辑正确，但在将具体数据精确映射到变量的过程中往往表现欠佳（即“有效绑定极限”），导致整体准确率下降。研究旨在解决这一瓶颈。

Method: 作者提出了一种名为BIND（Binding-INference-based Data）的推理时策略，该方法通过将数值数据提取为结构化文件，迫使模型通过编程方式进行绑定，而非直接从提示词中转录数据。此外，作者还构建了Text2Opt-Bench基准测试，并验证了针对绑定任务进行微调的专项模型在处理复杂约束时的优越性。

Result: Text2Opt-Bench测试表明，数据规模增大时模型准确率显著下降。应用BIND方法后，GPT-5-Nano的准确率从59.1%提升至82.4%，GPT-5从86.2%提升至95.8%。专门针对绑定任务微调的1.5B参数模型在性能上优于7B参数的端到端基准模型。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了语言模型在解决数学优化问题时存在的“有效绑定极限”问题，并证明了将数值数据与模型逻辑解耦（通过BIND方法）是提升性能的关键。未来的优化问题求解应更侧重于将数据处理外部化，而非单纯依赖模型内部的参数化转换。

Abstract: Text-to-optimization requires two separable capabilities: modeling -- choosing the right optimization structure -- and binding -- grounding every coefficient, index, and parameter in the concrete problem data. We study this via Text2Opt-Bench, a scalable benchmark of solver-verified optimization problems spanning 12 categories, from textbook linear programs to stochastic and multi-objective formulations with up to thousands of variables. Across 10+ models, we find that accuracy collapses as instance data grows, even when the formulation itself is simple. We call this the effective binding limit. We address this via a simple inference-time approach, BIND, which externalizes numeric data to structured files so the model binds data programmatically rather than transcribing from the prompt. BIND improves GPT-5-Nano from 59.1% to 82.4% accuracy, matching pass@5 (82.0%) at lower token cost than pass@1, and GPT-5 from 86.2% to 95.8%. Furthermore, we validate our hypothesis by finetuning a model exclusively on binding and show that it outperforms end-to-end SFT and RL across three structurally distinct optimization categories, with a 1.5B binding specialist alone matching a 7B end-to-end baseline.

</details>


### [69] [PEARL: Unbiased Percentile Estimation via Contrastive Learning for Industrial-Scale Livestream Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21752)
*Blake Gella,Wei Wu,Yuhao Yin,Zexi Huang,Zikai Wang,Emily Liu,Junlin Zhang,Wentao Guo,Qinglei Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对推荐系统中因用户活跃度差异带来的偏差问题，本文提出了 PEARL 框架，通过对比分位数近似而非绝对数值来建模用户偏好，有效提升了推荐系统的准确性与公平性，并在大规模生产环境中取得了显著的性能收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决推荐系统中存在的“行为强度不平衡”问题。现有模型受用户参与度差异影响，导致对高活跃用户信号过度放大，而忽略了普通用户，从而降低了推荐系统的整体质量、公平性及在大规模数据下的鲁棒性。

Method: 提出了 PEARL（非参数化对比分位数近似框架）：1. 利用真实对比交互样本直接近似分位数关系，无需辅助分布估计模型；2. 引入基于预测的自举机制（bootstrapping）处理稀疏及离散反馈；3. 采用广义值加权公式与协同训练策略，提升建模灵活性与表示学习能力。

Result: 离线实验表明，PEARL 能有效缓解行为偏差，提升多项排名指标。在拥有数十亿用户的直播平台线上 A/B 测试中，观看时长提升 2.10%，消费金额提升 0.80%，交互率提升 1.49%，举报率下降 6.91%。

Conclusion: PEARL 通过引入非参数化对比分位数近似框架，成功解决了推荐系统中因用户行为强度差异导致的偏差问题。该方法在理论上具有无偏性，并在工业级场景下验证了其提升推荐质量与模型鲁棒性的实际价值，为处理大规模、高偏差的推荐数据提供了有效的范式。

Abstract: Recommender systems trained on user interaction data are susceptible to behavioral intensity imbalance--a systematic distortion arising from heterogeneous engagement patterns across users. This imbalance skews feedback signals such that observed interactions no longer faithfully reflect true preferences, causing models to disproportionately amplify signals from highly active users while underrepresenting others, which ultimately degrades recommendation quality and robustness at scale. To address this issue, we propose a nonparametric contrastive percentile approximation framework, PEARL, that models relative preference signals instead of absolute engagement magnitudes. Building upon relative advantage debiasing, PEARL leverages real contrastive interaction samples to approximate percentile relationships directly, without relying on auxiliary distribution estimation models. We provide theoretical justification demonstrating that such pairwise comparisons yield unbiased estimates of percentile-based preference signals. For broader applicability, we introduce a prediction-based bootstrapping mechanism for percentile smoothing to handle sparse and discrete feedback, alongside a generalized value-weighted formulation and a co-training strategy to enhance both modeling flexibility and representation learning. Extensive offline experiments demonstrate that PEARL effectively mitigates behavioral bias and consistently improves recommendation performance across multiple ranking targets. Deployed in a production livestream platform with a combined user base of billions, online A/B testing confirms substantial real-world gains: +2.10% Watch Duration, +0.80% Consumption Amount, +1.49% Interaction Rate, and -6.91% Report Rate.

</details>


### [70] [Machine learning prediction of obstructive coronary artery disease using opportunistic coronary calcium and epicardial fat assessments from CT calcium scoring scans](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21762)
*Juhwan Lee,Ammar Hoori,Tao Hu,Justin N. Kim,Mohamed H. E. Makhlouf,Michelle C. Williams,David E. Newby,Robert Gilkeson,Sanjay Rajagopalan,David L. Wilson*

TL;DR: 本研究利用机器学习整合非增强CT图像中的钙化组学和脂肪组学特征，实现了对阻塞性冠心病的高效精准预测，为改善低至中危患者的临床诊疗策略提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究基于SCOT-HEART试验的1,324名患者数据，利用非增强CT图像提取了424个临床及组学特征（钙化组学和脂肪组学）。采用CatBoost算法结合SHAP值进行特征选择，并构建CatBoost梯度提升模型，最终筛选出14个最具预测价值的特征进行建模。

Conclusion: 该研究开发的高级机器学习框架通过整合非增强CT图像中的冠脉钙化组学和心外膜脂肪组学特征，能有效预测阻塞性冠状动脉疾病。该方法有望减少对对比剂增强或侵入性检查的依赖，特别是在低至中危患者群体中具有显著的临床应用前景。

Abstract: Non-contrast computed tomography calcium scoring (CTCS) is a cost-effective imaging modality widely used to detect coronary artery calcifications. This study aimed to develop an advanced machine learning framework that utilizes quantitative analyses of coronary calcium and epicardial fat from CTCS images to predict obstructive coronary artery disease (CAD). The study population consisted of 1,324 patients from the SCOT-HEART clinical trial who underwent both CTCS and coronary CT angiography. We extracted and analyzed a broad range of features, including 24 clinical variables, 189 calcium-omics, and 211 epicardial fat-omics features from the CTCS images. Feature selection was conducted using the CatBoost algorithm combined with SHapley Additive exPlanation (SHAP) values. Predictive modeling utilized the CatBoost gradient boosting method, focusing on the most informative features. From an initial set of 424 candidate features, 14 were identified as most predictive through the CatBoost-SHAP method. The top two predictive features originated from fat-omics, with the remaining 12 features derived from calcium-omics. The optimized model achieved robust predictive capabilities, demonstrating a sensitivity of 83.1+/-4.6%, specificity of 93.8+/-1.7%, accuracy of 85.3+/-2.0%, and an F1 score of 73.9+/-3.3%. Inclusion of calcium-omics and fat-omics data significantly improved predictive performance. Notably, the model also showed reliable predictive accuracy in patients with diverse coronary calcium scores, including cases with obstructive CAD despite a zero-calcium score. This innovative approach holds promise for improving clinical decision-making and potentially reducing dependence on contrast-enhanced or invasive diagnostic procedures, particularly within low-to intermediate-risk patient groups.

### [71] [On the Sample Complexity of Discounted Reinforcement Learning with Optimized Certainty Equivalents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21763)
*Oliver Mortensen,Mohammad Sadegh Talebi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了有限折扣MDP中递归优化确定性等价（OCE）风险度量的PAC可学习性，刻画了效用函数的要求，推导了紧致的样本复杂度界，并显著提升了CVaR风险度量下的理论界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的风险敏感强化学习在处理广泛的风险度量（如OCE族，包含CVaR、熵风险等）时，缺乏统一的PAC可学习性特征刻画，且样本复杂度界限尚不紧致，需要建立更严谨的理论框架以指导算法设计。

Method: 采用基于模型的学习方法（Model-based approach），对递归OCE的目标函数进行数学分析，通过构建效用函数与PAC可学习性的映射关系，并结合信息论方法推导样本复杂度的上下界。

Result: 1. 明确了OCE定义的目标函数具有PAC可学习性的充要条件是效用函数定义域为全实数集；2. 给出了价值学习与策略学习的样本复杂度上下界；3. 改进了CVaR风险度量下的样本复杂度依赖关系（对τ的依赖优化至1/τ²）。

Conclusion: 研究确立了针对递归优化确定性等价（OCE）风险度量进行PAC学习的必要与充分条件，证明了当效用函数域非全域时问题不可学习，并为CVaR等特定风险度量提供了改进的样本复杂度下界，揭示了风险敏感强化学习的理论极限。

Abstract: We study risk-sensitive reinforcement learning in finite discounted MDPs, where a generative model of the MDP is assumed to be available. We consider a family or risk measures called the optimized certainty equivalent (OCE), which includes important risk measures such as entropic risk, CVaR, and mean-variance. Our focus is on the sample complexities of learning the optimal state-action value function (value learning) and an optimal policy (policy learning) under recursive OCE. We provide an exact characterization of utility functions $u$ for which the corresponding OCE defines an objective that is PAC-learnable. We analyze a simple model-based approach and derive PAC sample complexity bounds. We establish that whenever $u$ does not have full domain $\text{dom}(u)\neq \mathbb{R}$, the corresponding problem is not PAC-learnable. Finally, we establish corresponding lower bounds for both value and policy learning, demonstrating tightness in the size $SA$ of state-action space, and for a more restricted class of utilities, we derive lower bounds that makes the dependence on the effective horizon $\frac{1}{1-γ}$ explicit. Specifically, for $\text{CVaR}_τ$ we show that the correct dependence on $τ$ is $\frac{1}{τ^2}$, thus improving by a factor of $\frac{1}τ$ over state-of-the-art although our bound has a suboptimal dependence on $\frac{1}{1-γ}$.

### [72] [Memory-R2: Fair Credit Assignment for Long-Horizon Memory-Augmented LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21768)
*Sikuan Yan,Ahmed Bahloul,Ercong Nie,Susanna Schwarzmann,Riccardo Trivisonno,Volker Tresp,Yunpu Ma*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对记忆增强型 LLM 智能体在多会话训练中因记忆状态差异导致的归因偏差问题，该论文提出了 Memory-R2 框架，通过 LoGo-GRPO 算法和协同学习设计，实现了公平的策略比较与稳定的长跨度记忆优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于组相对（如 GRPO）的强化学习方法假设所有轨迹采样自同一环境，但记忆增强型智能体在多会话交互中会不断修改记忆状态，导致不同轨迹间的中间记忆状态不一致，使得轨迹级对比变得不公平，产生了严重的归因偏差，难以对长期记忆操作进行有效训练。

Method: 提出了 Memory-R2 训练框架，其核心算法为 LoGo-GRPO（结合局部与全局的组相对优化），利用局部重采样对比同一中间记忆状态下的不同操作，并结合全局奖励确保端到端学习；此外，引入了事实提取器与记忆管理器的共享参数协同学习设计，并采用从 8 到 32 个会话的渐进式课程学习来稳定训练。

Result: 该研究通过对比实验表明，Memory-R2 能够为长跨度记忆操作提供更精确的监督信号，有效提升了智能体在长期多会话交互环境中的记忆形成与进化能力。

Conclusion: Memory-R2 框架通过创新的分层优化策略和协同学习机制，有效解决了记忆增强型 LLM 智能体在长跨度、多会话场景下强化学习的归因偏差和训练不稳定问题，为构建长效记忆智能体提供了范式。

Abstract: Memory-augmented LLM agents enable interactions that extend beyond finite context windows by storing, updating, and reusing information across sessions. However, training such agents with reinforcement learning in multi-session environments is challenging because memory turns the agent's past actions into part of its future environment. Once different rollouts write, update, or delete different memories, they no longer share the same intermediate memory state, making trajectory-level comparisons fundamentally unfair. This violates a key assumption behind group-relative methods such as GRPO, where rollouts are compared as if they were sampled from the same effective environment. Consequently, trajectory-level rewards provide noisy or biased credit signals for long-horizon memory operations. To address this challenge, we introduce Memory-R2, a training framework for long-horizon memory-augmented LLM agents. Its core algorithm, LoGo-GRPO, combines local and global group-relative optimization. The global objective preserves end-to-end learning from long-horizon trajectory-level rewards, while local rerollouts compare different memory-operation outcomes from the same intermediate memory state, yielding fairer group comparisons and more precise supervision for memory construction. Beyond credit assignment, Memory-R2 jointly optimizes memory formation and memory evolution with a shared-parameter co-learning design, where a fact extractor and a memory manager are instantiated from the same LLM backbone through role-specific prompts. To stabilize multi-step RL over long memory horizons, we adopt a progressive curriculum that increases the training horizon from 8 to 16 to 32 sessions. Together, these components provide an effective training paradigm for memory-augmented LLM agents in long-horizon multi-session settings.

</details>


### [73] [Provable Robustness against Backdoor Attacks via the Primal-Dual Perspective on Differential Privacy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21780)
*Aman Saxena,Jan Schuchardt,Yan Scholten,Stephan Günnemann*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于差分隐私对偶性的通用框架，通过复合机制实现了针对后门攻击（即训练与推理时联合扰动）的端到端鲁棒性认证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的随机平滑方法主要针对单一攻击阶段（如仅训练时或仅推理时），难以同时处理训练时投毒攻击和推理时回避攻击共同构成的“后门攻击”威胁。需要一种能够将训练和推理阶段的随机机制统一在单一认证体系下的方法。

Method: 将随机平滑与差分隐私的对偶视角（隐私轮廓，Privacy Profiles）相结合，通过一种数值化流程实现对异构机制的复合，从而构建出端到端的鲁棒性认证框架。

Result: 通过将该框架应用于 DP-SGD 和深度分区聚合（Deep Partition Aggregation），成功推导出了针对训练和推理阶段联合攻击的鲁棒性保证，并在 MNIST 和 CIFAR-10 数据集上验证了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个基于差分隐私对偶视角的随机平滑统一框架，成功解决了同时处理训练时（投毒）和推理时（回避）攻击的认证难题。该框架具有高度的模块化和通用性，为复杂威胁模型下的鲁棒性认证提供了理论支持。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing is a powerful tool for certifying robustness to adversarial perturbations, including poisoning attacks via randomized training and evasion attacks via randomized inference. Extending these guarantees to backdoor attacks, where training and test data are jointly perturbed, remains challenging because training- and test-time randomized mechanisms must be analyzed within a single robustness certificate. We address this by connecting randomized smoothing to the dual view of differential privacy through privacy profiles, which provide a numerical procedure for composing heterogeneous mechanisms. The resulting framework enables tight, modular, end-to-end certification of complex, composed mechanisms while leveraging existing analyses of differentially private mechanisms. We instantiate the framework for DP-SGD and Deep Partition Aggregation with inference-time smoothing, deriving joint robustness guarantees against both training-time and inference-time attacks. Experiments on MNIST and CIFAR-10 demonstrate the effectiveness of our framework. Overall, we provide a principled and general framework for using composite mechanisms to certify robustness under complex threat models that better capture the capabilities of real-world adversaries.

### [74] [MMD-Balls as Credal Sets: A PAC-Bayesian Framework for Epistemic Uncertainty in Test-Time Adaptation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21783)
*Ahanaf Hasan Ariq*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文为测试时自适应（TTA）提出了一种基于PAC-Bayesian和非精确概率理论的框架，利用MMD量化分布偏移并构建置信集，从而实现了对认识论不确定性的量化及模型自适应可靠性的理论保障。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时自适应（TTA）方法在分布偏移下虽能提升模型性能，但缺乏将偏移程度与预测可靠性联系起来的形式化理论保证。该研究旨在填补这一空白，提供一种能够量化不确定性并解释自适应有效性的理论框架。

Method: 该研究构建了一个PAC-Bayesian框架，通过最大均值差异（MMD）显式参数化泛化界限。研究利用Walley的非精确概率理论，将源分布周围的MMD球解释为置信集（credal sets），并结合RKHS-Lipschitz损失假设和测地线保持特性，推导出了有限样本下的最坏情况风险界限。

Result: 研究导出了依赖于MMD偏移惩罚的PAC-Bayesian泛化界限；证明了有限样本下的MMD集中不等式；建立了置信集内一致最坏情况下的风险界限，实现了认识论与偶然不确定性的分离；并揭示了核引导自适应保护局部特征几何结构的内在机理。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将MMD球与Walley的非精确概率理论相结合，为测试时自适应（TTA）提供了一个理论上严谨的框架。该方法有效地量化了认识论不确定性，并为何时进行模型自适应提供了基于风险的决策准则。

Abstract: Test-time adaptation (TTA) methods improve model performance under distribution shift but lack formal guarantees connecting shift magnitude to prediction reliability. We develop a PAC-Bayesian framework yielding generalization bounds explicitly parameterized by the maximum mean discrepancy (MMD) between source and target distributions. Our principal contribution is interpreting MMD-balls around the source distribution as credal sets in Walley's imprecise probability theory, yielding natural epistemic uncertainty quantification. We establish: (i) a PAC-Bayesian bound with an MMD-dependent shift penalty under an RKHS-Lipschitz loss assumption; (ii) a finite-sample version via MMD concentration; (iii) a uniform worst-case risk bound over all distributions in the credal set, with a lower-upper risk decomposition; and (iv) geodesic preservation bounds explaining why kernel-guided adaptation protects local feature geometry. The credal set interpretation separates epistemic from aleatoric uncertainty and provides a principled decision criterion for when adaptation is warranted.

### [75] [Three Costs of Amortizing Gaussian Process Inference with Neural Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21798)
*Robin Young*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过理论证明，神经过程在近似高斯过程时存在三个主要误差来源（标签污染、信息瓶颈、摊销误差），并定量分析了维度与内核平滑度对误差的影响，最终为改进神经过程架构提供了针对性的设计建议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经过程（Neural Processes）虽然通过摊销推理将高斯过程的计算复杂度从 $O(n^3)$ 降低到 $O(n)$，但其本质是近似推理，缺乏对近似误差来源及其影响的系统性理论理解。因此，本研究旨在量化这种近似带来的性能成本，并为模型架构设计提供理论指导。

Method: 研究人员通过对潜变量神经过程类模型进行数学推导，将神经过程与精确高斯过程预测分布之间的KL散度分解为三个可解释项：标签污染、信息瓶颈及摊销误差。同时，利用数学分析刻画了瓶颈截断项随表示维度 $d$ 的衰减率，并根据核函数的平滑性（如平方指数核与Matérn核）建立了结构规模与近似误差之间的直接关联。

Result: 结果表明，信息瓶颈误差随表示维度 $d$ 呈指数或多项式衰减，这直接受核函数平滑度和输入维度的影响；标签污染项通常为 $O(1)$，表明通过依赖标签的表示来估算不确定性存在持续的系统性偏差；研究识别了摊销过程中的主要性能缺口，并提出了架构改进方案。

Conclusion: 本文通过理论分析量化了神经过程（Neural Processes）在近似高斯过程（GP）时的性能损失。研究指出，该近似误差源于标签污染、信息瓶颈和摊销误差。针对这些误差，作者提出了优化建议：在处理不确定性预测时应仅依赖上下文位置，并建议采用二阶池化（second-order pooling）替代均值聚合，以显著缩小性能差距。

Abstract: Neural processes amortize Gaussian process inference, replacing the exact $O(n^3)$ posterior with a learned $O(n)$ map from context sets to predictive distributions. For a class of latent neural processes, we bound the Kullback--Leibler (KL) divergence between the GP and LNP predictives, decomposing it into three interpretable sources, namely label contamination as the neural process uses label values to estimate a quantity that is label-independent in the exact GP, an information bottleneck because the finite-dimensional representation cannot resolve the full context geometry, and amortization error from a single encoder network shared across all contexts. The bottleneck truncation term decays in the representation dimension $d$ as $O(e^{-cd^{2/d_x}})$ for squared-exponential kernels on $\mathbb{R}^{d_x}$ where $c > 0$ is a kernel-dependent constant and as $O(d^{-2ν/d_x})$ for Matérn-$ν$ kernels, directly linking architecture sizing to kernel smoothness and input dimension. The label contamination term is $O(1)$ in general, with only the observation-noise component decaying as $O(1/n)$, identifying a persistent cost of routing uncertainty estimation through a label-dependent representation. These results characterize the costs of amortization within the analyzed class and yield architectural recommendations to predict variance from context locations alone in the GP-amortization regime, and replace mean aggregation with second-order pooling to close the dominant amortization gap.

</details>

It delivers (1) a high-performance Lance-based data layer with native support and conversion tools for MP4, HDF5, and LeRobot datasets, (2) clean, well-tested implementations of modern world model baselines and planning solvers, and (3) a broad suite of environments and tasks extended with controllable visual, geometric, and physical factors of variation for systematic in-silico evaluation of dynamics understanding, control performance, representation quality, and out-of-distribution generalization. By unifying the full pipeline under a single, scalable framework, \texttt{swm} dramatically reduces research overhead and accelerates trustworthy progress toward reliable world models.

Abstract: Post-training has become central to improving reasoning and alignment in large language models, where critic-free models enable scalable learning from model-generated outputs but lack principled mechanisms to distinguish informative from noisy signals. Recent approaches leverage response-level measures as uncertainty signals to regulate group-based optimization methods such as GRPO. In this paper, we provide, to our knowledge, the first principled formulation that interprets uncertainty signals as mechanisms for characterizing and regulating gradient variance and learning signal quality. Our results highlight the importance of designing uncertainty signals that are aligned with optimization dynamics, offering a principled perspective for robust post-training.

Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.

### [81] [Energy-Gated Attention: Spectral Salience as an Inductive Bias for Transformer Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21842)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种能量门控注意力（EGA）机制，通过计算Token嵌入的谱能量，让Transformer更聚焦于信息密集的核心内容，在几乎不增加计算成本的情况下显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的标准Transformer注意力机制将所有Token视为同等重要，忽略了像流体动力学中的“相干结构”一样，语言序列中存在信息密度极高的Token（如句法头、形态边界等），这些Token携带了绝大部分信息，而其余Token多为冗余填充。

Method: 作者提出了能量门控注意力（Energy-Gated Attention, EGA），通过一个单一的线性投影来学习嵌入空间中的主导谱模式，并以此作为门控机制，根据Key Token嵌入的谱能量来加权价值（Value）的聚合，从而实现对信息密集区域的重点关注。

Result: EGA在TinyShakespeare和Penn Treebank数据集上分别实现了0.103和0.101的验证损失改善，且仅增加了极少的参数量（<0.26%），几乎没有计算开销。研究还发现，数据自适应的能量门控优于固定的小波基。

Conclusion: 能量门控注意力（EGA）机制证明了通过数据自适应方式识别并聚焦信息高密度Token（即“相干结构”），能有效提升Transformer的性能。该研究揭示了语言数据中约36%的内容词携带了主要信息，证明了该方法与数据集的独立性以及对计算成本的极低影响。

Abstract: Standard transformer attention computes pairwise similarity between queries and keys, treating all tokens as equally salient regardless of their intrinsic informational content. In turbulent fluid dynamics, coherent structures -- the energetically dominant, spatially organized patterns that persist amid background chaos -- carry a disproportionate fraction of total energy and govern all transport. We propose that tokens play an analogous role in transformer attention: informationally dense positions (morphological boundaries, syntactic heads, discourse markers) concentrate spectral energy and should attract proportionally more attention than background tokens (function words, repeated patterns, low-information filler). We propose Energy-Gated Attention (EGA): a simple modification that gates value aggregation by the spectral energy of key token embeddings, computed by a single learned linear projection that discovers the dominant spectral mode of the embedding field. On TinyShakespeare, EGA achieves +0.103 validation loss improvement with only 12,480 additional parameters (<0.26% overhead) and no measurable computational cost. The result is consistent on Penn Treebank (+0.101), demonstrating dataset independence. A systematic ablation across three wavelet families (fixed Morlet, Daubechies db2/db4, and a parametric Morlet) establishes that fixed structured bases are suboptimal -- the optimal energy direction is data-adaptive and non-sinusoidal -- while identifying learned wavelet packets as a promising open direction. The learned energy threshold converges to tau ~= 0.35 independently of initialization, corresponding to the fraction (~36%) of tokens carrying above-average spectral energy in English text, a stable linguistic property consistent with the fraction of content words in running English text.

### [82] [Geometry-Adaptive Explainer for Faithful Dictionary-Based Interpretability under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21849)
*Sungjun Lim,Heedong Kim,Andrew Lee,Kyungwoo Song*

TL;DR: 该论文针对机械可解释性中稀疏字典在分布偏移（OOD）下失效的问题，提出了无需微调的几何自适应解释器（GAE），有效弥补了分布变化带来的解释忠实度下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于字典的可解释性工具（如稀疏自编码器）在分布外（OOD）数据下表现不稳定，作者旨在解决由于数据分布偏移导致的解释器“忠实度缺口”问题。

Method: 提出了“几何自适应解释器”（GAE），利用无标签的分布外（OOD）激活数据，通过几何重对齐方法，将解释器的字典与模型在OOD下的活跃子空间对齐，而无需进行梯度更新。

Result: 理论上证明了GAE的过量损失受限于二阶矩偏移；实验结果显示，GAE在多种模型和OOD设置下的因果忠实度指标上，达到甚至超过了现有的需训练基线模型。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过几何适应方法（GAE）解决字典学习中的分布偏移问题是提升机械可解释性模型忠实度的有效手段，无需重新训练即可实现性能优化。

Abstract: Mechanistic interpretability aims to explain a model's behavior by identifying causally responsible internal structures. Dictionary-based explainers such as sparse autoencoders and transcoders are a primary tool, but their faithfulness under out-of-distribution (OOD) shift has received little systematic attention. We show that distribution shift rotates the subspace that the model actively uses, misaligning the explainer's dictionary trained on in-distribution (ID) activations. We formalize this misalignment as the faithfulness gap, a geometric distance between the ID dictionary and the OOD-active subspace, and show that it controls OOD faithfulness degradation. To reduce this gap, we propose the Geometry-Adaptive Explainer (GAE), which realigns the explainer's dictionary with the OOD-active subspace while preserving the original feature structure. This requires only unlabeled OOD activations and no gradient updates. We prove that GAE improves over the unadapted ID explainer, with excess loss bounded quadratically by the second-moment shift. Empirically, GAE even matches or surpasses all training-based baselines in causal faithfulness across multiple models and OOD settings.
