*Yifan Lan,Yuanpu Cao,Hanyu Wang,Lu Lin,Jinghui Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型中隐蔽的数据污染问题，本文提出了Zero-CoT Probe（ZCP）检测方法。该方法通过截断思维链以剥离模型的掩饰，对比同构扰动数据来暴露模型的记忆捷径，从而有效检测各种形式的基准测试污染并量化污染程度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在基准测试中的推理能力评估正面临严重的数据污染威胁，特别是恶意发布者通过改写基准数据等隐蔽手段逃避检测，导致评估结果虚高。现有检测方法难以有效识别此类隐蔽污染，因此亟需一种能够揭示模型潜在记忆行为并量化污染程度的新型检测技术。

Method: 提出了一种名为Zero-CoT Probe（ZCP）的黑盒检测方法，核心思想是截断思维链（CoT）以暴露模型底层的捷径映射（shortcut mappings），并通过对比原基准测试与同构扰动数据集的Zero-CoT性能来区分真实推理能力与记忆行为，同时引入了“污染置信度”（Contamination Confidence）指标进行量化评估。

Result: 实验表明，ZCP能够稳健地检测出直接数据污染及隐蔽的改写数据污染。相比现有方法，ZCP通过截断思维链有效剥离了模型的掩饰行为，能够更准确地判断模型是在进行真实推理还是在调用记忆，并且提供的“污染置信度”指标比单一的二元分类具有更高的分析价值。

Conclusion: 本文提出的Zero-CoT Probe（ZCP）是一种有效且鲁棒的黑盒检测方法，能够识别大语言模型中通过各种策略（包括改写等隐蔽手段）实现的数据污染，揭示了思维链（CoT）在掩盖模型记忆行为中的关键作用，并为评估模型的真实推理能力提供了可靠指标。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated impressive reasoning abilities across a wide range of tasks, but data contamination undermines the objective evaluation of these capabilities. This problem is further exacerbated by malicious model publishers who use evasive, or indirect, contamination strategies, such as paraphrasing benchmark data to evade existing detection methods and artificially boost leaderboard performance. Current approaches struggle to reliably detect such stealthy contamination. In this work, we uncover a critical phenomenon: a model's generated reasoning steps actively mask its underlying memorization. Inspired by this, we propose the Zero-CoT Probe (ZCP), a novel black-box detection method that deliberately truncates the entire Chain-of-Thought (CoT) process to expose latent shortcut mappings. To further isolate memorization from the model's intrinsic problem-solving capabilities, ZCP compares the model's zero-CoT performance on the original benchmark against an isomorphically perturbed reference dataset. Furthermore, we introduce Contamination Confidence, a metric that quantifies both the likelihood and severity of contamination, moving beyond simple binary classifications. Extensive experiments on both previously identified contaminated models and specially fine-tuned contaminated models demonstrate that ZCP robustly detects both direct and evasive data contamination. The code for ZCP is accessible at https://github.com/Yifan-Lan/zero-cot-probe.

</details>


### [84] [When to Switch, Not Just What: Transition Quality Prediction in Clash Royale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21868)
*Heeyun Heo,Huy Kang Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对竞技游戏中玩家因连败而盲目更换策略导致胜率下降的问题，本文指出了现有推荐系统忽略“切换成本”的局限性，并提出了TQP模型，通过精确控制切换时机和个体化推荐，显著优化了策略调整的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有推荐系统通常基于“零切换成本假设”（Zero Switching Cost Assumption），仅关注策略的预期质量，而忽略了频繁切换带来的行为成本以及不同玩家在切换倾向上的个体差异，导致玩家在连败后盲目更换策略反而降低了胜率。

Method: 1. 提出了TQP（Transition Quality Predictor）三阶段流水线：PersonaGate（识别是否切换）、TimingGate（识别何时切换）、ScoreFusion（排名策略）；2. 提出了评估指标SwitchGap，该指标不依赖于玩家的实际选择作为最优基准，从而避免了推荐模型拟合次优决策；3. 利用92.6万条《皇室战争》对局数据进行验证。

Result: 1. 数据分析显示策略切换频率与胜率呈负相关；2. TQP框架在推荐覆盖率为5.4%时，SwitchGap指标提升了10.4个百分点；3. 对因连败而频繁切换策略的玩家群体，该模型提供了显著的优化引导。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，在竞技游戏中忽视策略切换的“行为成本”和玩家个体差异会导致推荐系统性能下降。通过将策略推荐重构为“过渡质量预测”问题并引入TQP框架，研究能够有效识别切换的最佳时机，从而显著提升玩家的胜率，特别是对于那些过度切换的低表现玩家群体。

Abstract: In competitive games, players frequently switch strategies after losing streaks, yet our analysis of 926,334 match records from 34,619 Clash Royale players reveals a counterintuitive pattern: switching frequency is inversely associated with the win rate, with effects that vary substantially across players and situational contexts. We attribute this to a limitation common in many prior recommendation systems, which evaluate strategies by expected quality while overlooking the behavioral cost of switching and individual differences in switching propensity. We refer to this implicit premise as the Zero Switching Cost Assumption. To address this, we reformulate strategy recommendation as a transition-level decision problem and instantiate it as TQP (Transition Quality Predictor), a three-stage pipeline structured as Who -> When -> What. PersonaGate suppresses recommendations for players whose strategic consistency is empirically associated with superior outcomes. TimingGate identifies moments when switching is likely to yield a net benefit over staying, using a subtype- and state-matched baseline to control for natural win-rate recovery. ScoreFusion ranks candidate strategies by combining an adoptability signal with predicted transition quality (delta WR). We further introduce SwitchGap, an evaluation metric that measures a policy's discriminative quality without treating observed player choices as optimal ground truth. This property is particularly important because the most frequent switchers record the lowest win rates. The full pipeline achieves a SwitchGap of +10.4 percentage points at a recommendation rate of 5.4%, and loss-triggered switchers, despite being the lowest-performing group, benefit the most from subtype-conditioned guidance.

</details>


### [85] [Noise Schedule Design for Diffusion Models: An Optimal Control Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21911)
*Seo Taek Kong,Weina Wang,R. Srikant*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于最优控制理论的扩散模型噪声调度设计框架，利用Fisher信息优化采样误差上界，在理论上实现了最优采样复杂度，并通过参数化广义调度方案提升了图像生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有扩散模型中常用的噪声调度多依赖于经验设定，缺乏系统的理论指导。虽然现有理论已证明存在能够实现最优采样误差（$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$）的调度，但这些调度方案往往与实际应用中常用的方案不符。因此，作者旨在建立一个原则性的框架，既能解释现有调度，又能引导出表现更优的新型调度。

Method: 1. 将扩散过程中的噪声调度设计重新表述为最优控制问题；2. 利用Fisher信息作为状态变量，通过ODE描述其演化；3. 定义基于Fisher信息的泛函作为目标函数（即KL散度采样误差的上界）；4. 通过求解该最优控制问题，推导出噪声调度的充分条件，并在特定数据分布假设下获得闭式解。

Result: 1. 推导出了实现$\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$采样误差的充分条件，涵盖了实践中常用的噪声调度；2. 提出了具有闭式解的广义噪声调度函数，引入了可调参数；3. 实验表明，系统地优化这些参数后，在图像生成任务中获得了更好的FID分数。

Conclusion: 通过将噪声调度设计建模为最优控制问题，本文提出了一种能够泛化现有经验性调度（如指数和Sigmoid调度）的理论框架。通过引入可调节参数，该方法在理论上保证了最优采样误差，并在图像生成基准测试中实现了性能提升。

Abstract: We develop a principled framework for analyzing and designing noise schedules in diffusion models. We show that one can recast this design problem as an optimal control problem, whose state is the Fisher information of the diffusion process which evolves according to an ODE and the control input is the noise schedule. The objective of the optimal control problem is a functional involving the Fisher information, which is shown to be an upper bound on the Kullback-Leibler sampling error. By solving this optimal control problem, we obtain sufficient conditions on noise schedules under which state-of-the-art $\tilde{\mathcal{O}} (d/n)$ sampling error is achievable, where $d$ is the data dimension and $n$ is the number of discretization steps. While existing theoretical work also prove that $\tilde{\mathcal{O}}(d/n)$ sampling error bounds are achievable, these results hold for specific noise schedules, which do not include the schedules used in practice. Under a further parametric assumption on the data distribution, we show that one can obtain closed-form expressions for the noise schedules. These noise schedules generalize standard empirical schedules such as exponential and sigmoid schedules by allowing additional parameters that can be tuned. Systematically tuning the parameters of these schedules yields new schedules that achieve superior FID scores on image generation benchmarks.

</details>


### [86] [CausalGuard: Conformal Inference under Graph Uncertainty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21928)
*Vikash Singh,Weicong Chen,Debargha Ganguly,Yanyan Zhang,Nengbo Wang,Sreehari Sankar,Mohsen Hariri,Alexander Nemecek,Chaoda Song,Shouren Wang,Biyao Zhang,Van Yang,Erman Ayday,Jing Ma,Vipin Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CausalGuard 是一种结合了大语言模型结构搜索与共形预测的因果推断框架，通过对多个候选因果图的伪结果进行加权聚合与校准，有效解决了因果图设定错误带来的覆盖偏差问题，在保证统计严谨性的同时提高了预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在观测数据中估计处理效应时，传统的调整集选择严重依赖因果图结构的准确性。若图结构设定错误，会导致统计覆盖率严重不足；而现有的“图无关”共形预测方法往往需要极大的覆盖范围（padding）来保证有效性，导致估计结果过于保守，缺乏实用价值。因此，研究旨在开发一种既能利用结构信息，又能在图结构不确定性下保持统计稳健性的新框架。

Method: CausalGuard 框架包括三个核心步骤：1. 利用大语言模型（LLM）获取边优先级，结合条件独立性测试和贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）筛选候选有向无环图（DAG）；2. 聚合基于这些图结构的双稳健（Doubly Robust）伪结果；3. 采用基于复合非一致性得分的共形预测方法进行校准，确保在有限样本下实现分布无关的边际覆盖。

Result: 在五个基准测试中，CausalGuard 的平均覆盖率超过了设定的 90% 水平，且在置信区间宽度上显著优于传统的“图无关”共形基线方法。压力测试表明，该方法能有效抑制对无效碰撞因子（collider）的调整，并在先验信息存在偏差但保留了数据支持的候选集时，表现出极强的稳定性。

Conclusion: CausalGuard 为处理观测数据中的因果推断不确定性提供了一种鲁棒的解决方案。通过整合 LLM 辅助的结构学习与共形预测（Conformal Prediction），该方法在有效控制覆盖误差的同时，显著提升了处理效果估计的精确度，有效应对了模型错误设定的风险。

Abstract: Estimating treatment effects from observational data requires choosing an adjustment set, but valid adjustment depends on an unknown causal graph. Graph misspecification can cause under-coverage, while graph-agnostic conformal wrappers may regain nominal coverage only through large padding. We introduce CausalGuard, a structure-weighted conformal framework that calibrates after aggregating graph-conditional doubly robust pseudo-outcomes. Candidate DAGs are proposed from an LLM-derived edge prior, pruned by conditional-independence tests, and reweighted by Bayesian Information Criterion. A composite nonconformity score then calibrates the posterior-weighted pseudo-outcome. CausalGuard provides distribution-free finite-sample marginal coverage for this aggregated pseudo-outcome; under causal identification, overlap, conditional-mean nuisance stability, and concentration on target-aligned valid adjustment strategies, its conditional mean converges to the true Conditional Average Treatment Effect. Across five benchmarks, CausalGuard attains mean coverage above the nominal 90% level for the directly evaluable target and reduces width when graph-agnostic conformal baselines require large padding. Stress tests show that CausalGuard suppresses invalid collider adjustment and remains stable under misspecified priors when the retained candidate set is data-supported.

</details>


### [87] [Optimal Guarantees for Auditing Rényi Differentially Private Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21938)
*Benjamin D. Kim,Lav R. Varshney,Daniel Alabi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于Donsker-Varadhan变分估计的RDP黑盒审计框架，在理论上实现了样本复杂度最优，并在实验中显著改进了对DP-SGD等算法的隐私泄露评估精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黑盒审计方法在评估声称具有Rényi差分隐私（RDP）的机器学习算法时往往不够精确，特别是在Rényi阶较小时难以准确估计隐私泄漏。研究者旨在建立一个理论支撑扎实、样本效率高且能有效界定RDP隐私下界的通用黑盒审计框架。

Method: 该研究构建了一个基于假设检验的审计框架，利用Donsker-Varadhan（DV）变分估计器直接估计相邻执行间的Rényi散度。通过引入类受限（class-restricted）的DV估计器，将统计估计误差与算法隐私泄露分离开来，并导出了非渐近置信区间。此外，作者证明了该方法在信息论意义下具有极小极大最优的样本复杂度。

Result: 理论上，该方法在对数因子范围内实现了信息论最优的样本复杂度保证。在实证方面，对MNIST和CIFAR-10数据集上的DP-SGD进行评估，结果表明该审计框架在广泛的隐私预算范围内，特别是在小到中等Rényi阶的情况下，能够提供比现有最先进黑盒方法更严格、更准确的RDP经验下界。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于Donsker-Varadhan变分估计的RDP黑盒审计框架。该方法不仅在理论上达到了样本复杂度的极小极大最优性，还在实验中显著提升了对DP-SGD等算法隐私保障的评估精度，为黑盒差分隐私审计提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: We study black-box auditing for machine learning algorithms that claim R \ 'enyi differential privacy (RDP) guarantees. We introduce an auditing framework, based on hypothesis testing, that directly estimates Rényi divergence between neighboring executions using the Donsker-Varadhan (DV) variational estimator. Our analysis yields explicit and non-asymptotic confidence intervals for RDP auditing via class-restricted DV estimators, separating statistical estimation error from algorithmic privacy leakage. We prove matching minimax lower bounds showing that, up to logarithmic factors, our sample-complexity guarantees are information-theoretically optimal, thereby establishing the first optimal guarantees for auditing RDP via DV estimators. Empirically, we instantiate our framework for auditing DP-SGD in a fully black-box setting. Across MNIST and CIFAR-10, and over a wide range of privacy regimes, our auditors produce a strong overall improvement on empirical RDP lower bounds compared to prior state-of-the-art black-box methods especially at small and moderate Rényi orders where accurate auditing is most challenging.

### [88] [SCI-Defense: Defending Manipulation Attacks from Generative Engine Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21948)
*Xucheng Yu,Haibo Jin,Huimin Zeng,Haohan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型检索系统易受生成引擎优化（GEO）攻击的问题，本文提出了SCI-Defense框架，通过多维度语义完整性评估有效识别并拦截了隐蔽的语义操纵，在实验中表现出色，并揭示了现有防御体系中的结构性盲点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于大模型（LLM）的检索系统容易受到“生成引擎优化（GEO）”攻击的影响。攻击者通过在产品描述中注入语义信号，人为提升其在检索结果中的排名。现有防御机制难以识别这种不改变文本困惑度但操纵排名的语义攻击，因此迫切需要更鲁棒的检测框架。

Method: 提出SCI-Defense防御框架，包含三个核心组件：1. 困惑度检测（PPL），用于识别生成式文本的异常分布；2. 语义完整性评分（SIS），从权威归属、叙述目的性、比较性声明和时效性声明四个维度评估内容操纵；3. 候选间检测（ICD），通过对比候选集内的语义特征识别异常增益。

Result: 在包含600个亚马逊产品描述的数据集上，SCI-Defense实现了1.000的精确率和0.000的误报率，针对不同类型攻击（String、Reasoning、Review）表现出了极高的召回率；在MS MARCO数据集上的实验也验证了其在识别操纵性内容方面的有效性，且显著优于现有的基线防御方法。

Conclusion: 本文证明了现有的防御手段（如困惑度过滤、安全分类器和改写）无法有效抵御语义操纵攻击，并提出了SCI-Defense框架作为一种高效的解决方案。同时，文章揭示了“规范放大”和“用例饱和”等新型攻击方式，表明语义相关性操纵仍是当前大模型检索系统的防御盲点，为未来研究指明了方向。

Abstract: LLM-based ranking systems are vulnerable to Generative Engine Optimization (GEO) attacks, where adversaries inject semantic signals into product descriptions to artificially boost rankings. We propose SCI-Defense, a three-component defense framework combining Perplexity detection (PPL), Semantic Integrity Scoring (SIS), and Inter-Candidate Detection (ICD). SIS evaluates four manipulation dimensions: Authority Attribution (AA), Narrative Purposiveness (NP), Comparative Claims (CA), and Temporal Claims (TC). Evaluated on 600 Amazon product descriptions across 6 categories, SCI-Defense achieves Precision=1.000 and FPR=0.000, with Recall of 1.000, 0.952, and 0.830 against String, Reasoning, and Review attacks respectively. On 600 MS MARCO web passages, String attacks are blocked with perfect recall while Review attacks yield near-zero recall, as web passages lack the persuasion-oriented signals that SIS targets in product descriptions. We demonstrate that existing defenses -- PPL-only filters, SafetyClf content classifiers, and paraphrasing -- achieve zero recall against semantic manipulation attacks. We further demonstrate new attacks such as Specification Amplification and Use-Case Saturation can expose semantic relevance manipulation as a structural defense blind spot that suggests directions for future research.

### [89] [Dynamic Mixture of Latent Memories for Self-Evolving Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21951)
*Dianzhi Yu,Vireo Zhang,Hongru Wang,Yanyu Chen,Minda Hu,Wanghan Xu,Siki Chen,Philip Torr,Zhenfei Yin,Irwin King*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决智能体在多任务持续学习中面临的“灾难性遗忘”与“知识无法有效内化”之间的矛盾，即在不更新基础模型参数的前提下，实现知识的有效累积与能力的自我进化。

Method: 提出了一种基于动态专家混合（MoE）的生成式潜记忆框架（MoLEM）。该方法将多个专家作为独立的知识载体，通过键值匹配路由来聚合潜记忆，并将其注入推理过程；保持基础模型冻结以防止灾难性遗忘，同时利用轻量级自动编码器处理不同训练阶段的知识归档。

Result: 在数学、科学和代码领域的持续学习任务中，MoLEM相较于原始预训练基线模型，平均准确率提升了10.40%，且在不同训练顺序下表现出比现有对比方法更优的一致性和稳定性。

Conclusion: MoLEM框架有效地解决了持续学习中的灾难性遗忘问题，通过模块化架构实现了知识的累积与内化，为构建具备自我进化能力的智能体提供了一种鲁棒且高效的解决方案。

Abstract: Achieving self-evolution in intelligent agents requires the continual accumulation of new knowledge across changing task sequences without forgetting previously acquired abilities. Existing approaches either internalize knowledge by updating model parameters, which induces catastrophic forgetting, or rely on external memory, which fails to genuinely enhance the model's intrinsic capabilities. We propose MoLEM, a generative mixture of latent memory framework based on a dynamic mixture-of-experts (MoE). We treat multiple experts as independent carriers to generate memory. A router selects and weights experts through key-query matching, and the aggregated latent memory is injected into the reasoning process. The base model for reasoning remains entirely frozen, with all experiential knowledge internalized into the additional modules, avoiding catastrophic forgetting. For continual learning, each training stage is paired with a lightweight autoencoder that selects the appropriate routing group at inference, and inputs that match no stage fall back to the pretrained model. Experiments train the framework on continual-learning sequences spanning math, science, and code domains. After training, we evaluate the framework on the corresponding test sets to measure task learning and competence preservation across continual adaptation stages. After the full continual-learning sequence, our method improves the average accuracy by 10.40% over the Vanilla pretrained baseline, while none of the competing methods consistently exceed this baseline across different training orders.

### [90] [Teaching Language Models to Forecast Research Success Through Comparative Idea Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21491)
*Srujan P Mule,Aniketh Garikaparthi,Manasi Patwardhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了语言模型预测科研假设成功率的能力。通过构建大规模实验结果数据集，证明了经过训练的小型语言模型（SFT/RLVR）能作为高效、客观的“验证器”，在实验前筛选出更有潜力的科学研究思路，从而打破自动化科学研究的评估瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语言模型加速科学研究中假设的生成，评估和筛选这些海量AI生成想法的效率成为新的瓶颈。研究者旨在探讨语言模型是否能够在实验开始前，通过对比预测来判断研究想法的经验成功率，从而实现更高效的科学探索。

Method: 1. 数据集构建：利用PapersWithCode构建了包含11,488对基于客观实验结果的想法对比数据集。2. 模型训练：采用监督微调（SFT）显著提升预测准确率；引入带可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），使模型能够探索潜在的推理路径并提供可解释的论证。3. 评估与测试：进行了消融实验、分布外（OOD）测试、跨领域时间分割测试以及独立构建的数据集测试。

Result: 经过监督微调（SFT）后的模型在对比预测任务中达到了77.1%的准确率，超越了GPT-4（文中提及GPT-5类比）；基于RLVR的方法达到了71.35%的准确率，并能提供具有解释性的论证；模型在各类稳健性测试中表现出良好的泛化能力和抗干扰性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，小型语言模型通过特定的监督微调（SFT）和强化学习（RLVR），能够有效地作为科学假设的客观验证器。这为实现自主科学发现提供了一条可扩展且高效的路径，克服了评估AI生成想法的高成本瓶颈。

Abstract: As language models accelerate scientific research by automating hypothesis generation and implementation, a new bottleneck emerges: evaluating and filtering hundreds of AI-generated ideas without exhaustive experimentation. We ask whether LMs can learn to forecast the empirical success of research ideas before any experiments are run. We study comparative empirical forecasting: given a benchmark-specific research goal and two candidate ideas, predict which will achieve better benchmark performance. We construct a dataset of 11,488 idea pairs grounded in objective outcomes from PapersWithCode. While off-the-shelf 8B-parameter models struggle (30% acc.), SFT dramatically boosts performance to 77.1%, outperforming GPT-5 (61.1%). By framing evaluation as a reasoning task via Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), we train models to discover latent reasoning paths, achieving 71.35% acc. with interpretable justifications. Through additional ablations and out-of-distribution tests, we show robustness to surface-level heuristics and transfer to both a cross-domain time-split test set and an independently constructed test set. Our results demonstrate that compute-efficient small language models can serve as effective, objective verifiers, offering a scalable path for autonomous scientific discovery.

### [91] [ChronoMedicalWorld: A Medical World Model for Learning Patient Trajectories from Longitudinal Care Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21963)
*Jiangyuan Wang,Xuyong Chen,Junwei He,Xu Xu,Shasha Xie,Fuman Han*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对慢性病长期生理演变预测难题，作者提出了CMWM世界模型框架，通过整合临床结构化数据与对话文本，利用闭环训练策略，在CKD患者预测任务中实现了比大模型更优的精度，为复杂临床长周期模拟提供了有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的电子健康记录（EHR）模型多为判别式模型，难以处理长周期预测；而通用大模型在面对重复干预时容易出现模型漂移。针对慢性病护理中对长周期生理演变预测的需求，需要构建一个能够理解干预措施与患者状态演变关系的生成式世界模型。

Method: 提出了ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)框架：1. 联合嵌入状态编码器与广义动作编码器（处理结构化指标及自由文本）；2. 循环潜在转移模块；3. 采用包含六项损失函数的复合目标（观测监督、潜在预测、正则化及生理形态先验）；4. 引入闭环滚动前缀协议（Closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol）以优化多步预测表现。

Result: 在慢性肾脏病（CKD）患者的年度估算肾小球滤过率（eGFR）预测任务中，CMWM表现优于基准模型（GPT-5.5），MAE降低了7.28%，RMSE降低了7.35%，且证明了患者与健康教练之间的对话信息对提升预测精度具有显著贡献。

Conclusion: CMWM提供了一个通用的、基于动作条件下的潜在世界模型框架，通过整合结构化干预和自然语言对话，能够有效模拟慢性病患者的长周期生理演变，其架构和训练策略具有广泛的临床应用前景。

Abstract: Long-horizon clinical simulation -- predicting how a patient's physiology evolves over years under specified interventions -- is central to chronic-disease care, yet existing electronic health record (EHR) models are predominantly discriminative, and general-purpose large language models drift under repeated interventions. We propose the \textbf{ChronoMedicalWorld Model (CMWM)}, an action-conditioned latent world-model framework for learning patient trajectories from longitudinal care data. CMWM couples a joint-embedding state encoder with a wide action encoder that admits both structured intervention indicators and free-text communication embeddings, and trains a recurrent latent transition module under a six-term objective: next-observation supervision, next-latent prediction, SIGReg latent regularisation, and three physiology-aware shape priors (slope, continuity, large-jump penalty). A closed-loop rollout-prefix protocol matches training to deployment, so the model is optimised against the same multi-step error it exhibits at inference. As a concrete case study, we instantiate CMWM for annual estimated glomerular filtration rate (eGFR) trajectory forecasting in chronic kidney disease (CKD). On a 2{,}232-patient nephrology cohort, the CKD instantiation achieves a dynamic-50\% history rollout test mean absolute error (MAE) of 7.384 and root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 10.256, against 7.964 and 11.069 for a tuned GPT-5.5 structured-prompting baseline ($-7.28\%$ MAE, $-7.35\%$ RMSE), with the gain dominated by the dialogue portion of patient--health-coach communication. The framework is not CKD-specific: its architecture, loss design, and training protocol apply to any chronic condition that can be cast as periodic clinical state interleaved with structured and conversational interventions.

</details>


### [92] [HealthCraft: A Reinforcement Learning Safety Environment for Emergency Medicine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21496)
*Brandon Dent*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: HealthCraft 是首个针对急诊医疗场景的轨迹级安全性强化学习评估环境，揭示了当前前沿大模型在多步临床工作流中存在严重的性能崩溃和安全风险，并强调了评估基础设施保真度的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前沿大模型在临床工作流中的部署速度超过了安全评估基础设施的发展速度。传统的静态医疗问答（QA）基准无法捕捉急诊医疗中关键的故障模式，如轨迹级安全崩溃、工具误用以及在持续临床压力下的表现失效。因此，需要一个能够评估轨迹级安全性的动态环境。

Method: 研究团队开发了 HealthCraft，这是一个基于 FHIR R4 标准的强化学习环境，模拟真实急诊医疗条件。该环境包含 14 种实体类型、3,987 个种子实体和 24 个工具调用（MCP），并定义了双层评估准则，其中安全关键准则的违规会导致奖励归零。研究共包含 205 项任务，并利用确定性 LLM 评判器来降低评估噪声。

Result: 实验测试了两种前沿模型：Claude Opus 和 GPT-5.4。结果显示，模型在处理多步工作流时性能几乎崩溃（Claude 为 1.0%，GPT 为 0.0%），且存在高达 27.5% 至 34.0% 的安全故障率。研究还发现，基础设施的微小调整会显著改变模型表现的排名，证明了评估基础设施本身是测量过程中的关键变量。

Conclusion: 现有的前沿大模型在模拟急诊医疗的多步工作流中表现出严重的性能衰退和安全风险。评估基础设施的保真度对测量结果至关重要，HealthCraft 提供了一个必要且严谨的基准环境，用以推动医疗大模型在安全性与临床可靠性方面的进步。

Abstract: Frontier language models are being deployed into clinical workflows faster than the infrastructure to evaluate them safely. Static medical-QA benchmarks miss the failure modes that matter in emergency medicine: trajectory-level safety collapse, tool misuse, and capitulation under sustained clinical pressure. We present HealthCraft, the first public reinforcement-learning environment that rewards trajectory-level safety under realistic emergency-medicine conditions, adapted from Corecraft. It is built on a FHIR R4 world state with 14 entity types and 3,987 seed entities, exposes 24 MCP tools, and defines a dual-layer rubric that zeroes reward whenever any safety-critical criterion is violated. We release 195 tasks across six categories, graded against 2,255 binary criteria (515 safety-critical); a post-hoc 10-task negative-class slate extends this to 205 tasks and 2,337 criteria. V8 results on two frontier models show Claude Opus 4.6 at Pass@1 24.8% [21.5-28.4] and GPT-5.4 at 12.6% [10.2-15.6], with safety-failure rates of 27.5% and 34.0%. On multi-step workflows - the closest proxy to real emergency care - performance collapses to near zero (Claude 1.0%, GPT-5.4 0.0%) despite partial competence on individual steps. Six infrastructure bugs fixed between pilots v2 and v8 re-ordered which model "looks stronger," evidence that infrastructure fidelity is part of the measurement. A deterministic LLM-judge overlay bounds evaluator noise, and a 60-run negative-class smoke pilot shows the reward signal is not drop-in training-safe: restraint criteria pass at 0.929 prevalence, a gameability an eval harness can tolerate but a training reward cannot. We scaffold coupling to a Megatron+SGLang+GRPO loop per Corecraft Section 5.2 and leave training-reward ablations as future work. Environment, tasks, rubrics, and harness are released under Apache 2.0.

### [93] [An Improved Adaptive PID Optimizer with Enhanced Convergence and Stability for Deep Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21968)
*Saurabh Saini,Kapil Ahuja,Thomas Wick,Saurav Kumar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 IAdaPID-ADG 优化器，通过整合非递增有效学习率和梯度差调制机制，解决了 AdaPID 在收敛与稳定性上的不足，并在多个数据集上验证了其卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的动量随机梯度下降存在梯度噪声和过冲现象。虽然 Adam 和 PID 优化器分别解决了部分问题，而后续的 AdaPID 尝试结合两者，但仍存在严重的收敛性和稳定性挑战。本研究旨在通过改进 AdaPID 克服这些局限性。

Method: 提出了一种新型优化器 IAdaPID-ADG。该方法在现有的 AdaPID 框架基础上，引入了 AMSGrad 的“非递增有效学习率”机制以改善收敛性，并结合 DiffGrad 的“基于梯度差的调制因子”来增强训练的稳定性。

Result: 在 MNIST、CIFAR10 等基准数据集以及 IARC 和 AnnoCerv 等现实数据集上的实验表明，IAdaPID-ADG 在性能上显著优于现有的竞争优化器，且消融实验证明了所引入的各项改进组件均对性能提升有实质性贡献。

Conclusion: 通过整合非递增有效学习率和基于梯度差的调制因子，IAdaPID-ADG 成功解决了传统自适应 PID 优化器在收敛性和稳定性方面的固有缺陷，为深度学习优化提供了一种更稳健、高效的方案。

Abstract: Optimization is essential in deep learning. The foundational method upon which most optimizers are built is momentum-based stochastic gradient descent. However, it suffers from two key drawbacks. First, it has noisy and varying gradients, and second, it has an overshoot phenomenon. To address noisy gradients, Adam was proposed, which remains the most widely used adaptive optimizer. To address the overshoot phenomenon, a control-theory-based PID optimizer was proposed. To tackle both the limitations within a single framework, several variants of Adaptive PID (AdaPID) have recently been proposed.
  Although AdaPID performs well, it still inherits two critical drawbacks from Adam, namely convergence and stability issues. In this work, we address both these limitations. To fix the convergence issue, we uniquely integrate the idea of using a non-increasing effective learning rate into AdaPID (originally proposed in AMSGrad, an extension of Adam). To fix the stability issue, we innovatively integrate a gradient difference based modulation factor into AdaPID (originally proposed in DiffGrad, another extension of Adam). Combining both these ideas in AdaPID, results in our novel IAdaPID-ADG optimizer.
  We evaluate our proposed optimizer on multiple datasets, including benchmark datasets (MNIST and CIFAR10) and real-world datasets (IARC and AnnoCerv). The IAdaPID-ADG substantially outperforms all competing optimizers. Additionally, we perform an ablation study on the MNIST dataset to demonstrate the contribution of each added component.

### [94] [Reasoning through Verifiable Forecast Actions: Consistency-Grounded RL for Financial LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21975)
*Jialin Chen,Aosong Feng,Harshit Verma,Siyi Gu,Haiwen Wang,Ali Maatouk,Yixuan He,Yifeng Gao,Leandros Tassiulas,Rex Ying*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: StockR1 是一种将金融推理与时间序列预测相统一的 LLM。它通过结构化的“预测动作”连接定性分析与定量预测，并结合不确定性感知的强化学习进行优化，有效解决了金融数据预测中的非平稳性和推理脱节问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的金融预测方法通常将时间序列文本化或将定性推理与定量预测割裂，无法有效处理金融市场的高非平稳性、低信噪比以及对外部信息的高度依赖，导致定性推理与量化结果之间存在根本性的不匹配。因此，需要一种能够统一金融推理与预测的方法。

Method: 1. 提出 StockR1 模型：一种时间序列增强的 LLM，通过工具调用（tool-call）机制将预测动作作为定性市场观点的结构化表征。
2. 双阶段流程：先由模型生成预测动作，再由条件时间序列解码器基于该动作生成未来分布路径。
3. 强化学习优化：通过联合奖励函数（涵盖答案有效性、预测准确性及动作-时间序列一致性）对全流程进行优化。
4. 不确定性感知：利用样本级的不确定性标量对奖励进行加权，以增强模型对市场动态波动性的适应能力。

Result: StockR1 在 10 年的大规模基准测试中表现卓越，显著优于现有的时间序列基线模型和通用大模型。在金融问答与股价预测任务中，4B 和 8B 参数版本的模型推理准确性分别提升了 17.7% 和 25.9%，验证了该框架在数值化归因和推理方面的有效性。

Conclusion: StockR1 通过建立预测动作（forecast action）这一中间结构，成功将大语言模型的定性推理与定量金融预测紧密结合。研究表明，这种结构化的协同机制显著提升了模型处理金融市场非平稳性数据的能力，证明了通过可验证的预测动作实现推理与预测闭环是金融领域人工智能的重要发展方向。

Abstract: Financial markets are characterized by extreme non-stationarity, low signal-to-noise ratios, and strong dependence on external information such as news, company fundamentals, and macroeconomic signals. Yet, existing approaches either abstract time-series into text or decouple forecasting from language-based reasoning, leading to a fundamental mismatch between qualitative reasoning and quantitative outcomes. To address this, we introduce StockR1, a time-series-enhanced LLM that unifies stock forecasting and financial reasoning through a verifiable forecast action. Based on a tool-call design, the model first emits a forecast action, which is a structured and interpretable representation of its qualitative market outlook. It then invokes a time-series decoder conditioned on this action to generate distributional future trajectories, leading to more informed question answering and financial reasoning. We optimize the full pipeline with reinforcement learning, where rewards jointly reflect answer validity, forecast accuracy, and consistency between generated actions and observed time-series dynamics. In addition, rewards are reweighted by a sample-level uncertainty scalar, encouraging the model to accommodate varying uncertainty in market dynamics. We evaluate StockR1 on financial question answering and stock forecasting over a large-scale 10-year benchmark. Our method consistently outperforms time-series baselines and general-purpose LLMs, improving reasoning accuracy by 17.7% (4B) and 25.9% (8B). These findings demonstrate that structuring the forecast actions establishes a powerful synergy between language reasoning and temporal prediction, enabling LLMs to reason through verifiable, interpretable, and numerically grounded decisions.

### [95] [Check Your LLM's Secret Dictionary! Five Lines of Code Reveal What Your LLM Learned (Including What It Shouldn't Have)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22005)
*Hisashi Miyashita*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种仅需对模型输出层（lm_head）权重进行奇异值分解（SVD）的轻量级分析方法，无需运行推理即可直接从模型权重中揭示语义子空间，从而有效地审计模型预训练数据的构成、识别敏感内容及异常词汇，并能指导后续的模型设计与优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在无需昂贵模型推理的情况下，通过分析模型权重本身，深入理解大模型的训练数据构成、潜在安全隐患（如不当词汇）以及模型设计理念。

Method: 对Transformer模型中的lm_head权重矩阵进行奇异值分解（SVD）。无需模型推理，仅需少量代码即可通过左奇异向量识别词汇表聚类，并利用新提出的词汇聚类得分（VCS）和加权投影得分（WPS）进行量化分析与异常检测。

Result: 研究发现不同模型的权重结构存在显著差异，且通过该方法能直接发现模型在预训练阶段引入的不当词汇子空间（且无法通过对齐消除）。此外，该方法成功识别了著名的“glitch token”（如shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu），证明了其在审计及异常检测中的有效性。

Conclusion: 通过对lm_head权重矩阵进行SVD分析，可以无推理地揭示大模型中可解释的语义子空间及其潜在问题。该方法应被采纳为大模型发布前的标准化安全审计步骤，并对未来的分词器优化及模型设计具有指导意义。

Abstract: We show that singular value decomposition of the lm_head} weight matrix of a transformer-based large language model -- requiring only five lines of PyTorch and no model inference -- reveals interpretable semantic subspaces directly from the model weights. Each left singular vector identifies the vocabulary tokens most readily selected when the hidden state aligns with the corresponding singular direction; inspecting these clusters exposes the model's training data composition and curation philosophy.
  Analysing GPT-OSS-120B, Gemma-2-2B, and Qwen2.5-1.5B, we find that singular value spectra and vocabulary cluster structures differ systematically across models: GPT exhibits a graduated hierarchy of functionally differentiated subspaces; Gemma is dominated by pre-nineteenth-century English orthography, forming a stepwise clustering structure that may contribute to high output controllability; and Qwen exhibits broad multilingual coverage alongside subspaces whose vocabulary the authors have determined to be ethically inappropriate for direct publication.
  Base-instruct comparison reveals that ethically concerning subspaces originate in pretraining and are not removed by post-training alignment. We introduce the Vocabulary Cluster Score (VCS) to quantify subspace coherence, and the Weighted Projection Score (WPS) as a static glitch token detector; applying WPS to GPT-OSS-120B recovers shokubutsu-hyakka-tsu (ID 137606), a well-known glitch token widely reported in the CJK language community, without any model inference. We propose a taxonomy of root causes for problematic vocabulary content and call for lm_head} SVD analysis to be adopted as a standard pre-release safety auditing step. Our findings further suggest directions toward SVD-guided tokenizer optimisation and more controllable LLM design.

### [96] [LABO: LLM-Accelerated Bayesian Optimization through Broad Exploration and Selective Experimentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22054)
*Zhuo Chen,Xinzhe Yuan,Jianshu Zhang,Jinzong Dong,Ruichen Zhou,Yingchun Niu,Tianhang Zhou,Yu Yang Fredrik Liu,Yuqiang Li,Nanyang Ye,Qinying Gu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 LABO 的框架，通过门控机制动态利用大语言模型的低成本预测与少量高成本的真实实验数据，显著提高了科学探索中贝叶斯优化的样本效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学探索中存在实验成本高昂和数据稀缺的问题。尽管现有研究已尝试将大语言模型引入贝叶斯优化，但未能充分利用大语言模型评估成本极低的优势，因此需要一种更高效的策略来整合这两种信息源。

Method: 提出 LLM-Accelerated Bayesian Optimization (LABO) 框架，该方法将大语言模型的预测与真实实验观测整合在同一个贝叶斯优化闭环中，并引入一个门控准则（gating criterion）来动态平衡大语言模型预测与真实实验数据的使用，以实现在大空间探索与高精度实验验证之间的权衡。

Result: 理论上给出了累积遗憾界（cumulative regret bound）证明了其效率增益，实验结果表明，在相同的实验预算下，LABO 在多个科学任务中表现均优于现有的贝叶斯优化方法。

Conclusion: LABO 提供了一种将大语言模型与贝叶斯优化有机结合的实用且具有理论依据的框架，通过动态决策机制显著提升了科学发现流程的样本效率。

Abstract: The high cost and data scarcity in scientific exploration have motivated the use of large language models (LLMs) as knowledge-driven components in Bayesian optimization (BO). However, existing approaches typically embed LLMs directly into the sampling or surrogate modeling pipeline, without fully leveraging their significantly lower evaluation cost compared to real-world experiments. To address this limitation, we propose LLM-Accelerated Bayesian Optimization (LABO), a framework that combines LLM predictions with experimental observations within a single BO loop. LABO employs a gating criterion to dynamically balance the reliance on LLM predictions versus actual experiments. By leveraging inexpensive LLM evaluations to broadly explore the search space and reserving costly real experiments only for regions with high uncertainty, LABO achieves more sample-efficient optimization. We provide a theoretical analysis with a cumulative regret bound that formalizes this efficiency gain. Empirical results across diverse scientific tasks demonstrate that LABO consistently outperforms existing methods under identical experimental budgets. Our results suggest that LABO offers a practical and theoretically grounded approach for integrating LLMs into scientific discovery workflows.

### [97] [Prototype-Guided Classification Sub-Task Decoupling Framework: Enhancing Generalization and Interpretability for Multivariate Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22055)
*Xianhao Song,Yuang Zhang,Yuqi She,Liping Wang,Xuemin Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PDFTime 是一种新型原型引导的时间序列分类框架，通过将直接的分类映射转化为基于原型的多阶段相似度推理，显著提升了分类性能并赋予了模型更好的可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的时间序列分类（TSC）方法多采用直接的特征到标签（feature-to-label）分类范式，通过全局池化和线性投影将时间嵌入转换为类别逻辑，导致特征提取与决策逻辑混淆，形成难以解释的“黑盒”，限制了模型的准确性与可解释性。

Method: 提出了一种名为 PDFTime 的原型引导框架。该方法将时间序列分类重新定义为一个多阶段的决策过程：首先利用学习到的原型（Prototypes）近似潜在空间中的类条件特征分布，随后通过不同粒度的分类子任务实现逐步判别，而非简单的直接特征到标签映射。

Result: 在 UEA 和 UCR 基准测试上达到了当前的最高水平（SOTA）。特别是在 UCR 档案的 128 个数据集中，PDFTime 在 80 个数据集上取得了第一名的准确率，在一致性和泛化能力上均显著优于现有主流方法。

Conclusion: PDFTime 成功打破了传统时间序列分类（TSC）中直接映射的“黑盒”范式，证明了通过解耦特征提取与决策逻辑，采用基于原型的多阶段推理过程，不仅能提升分类的准确性，还能显著增强模型的透明度和可解释性。

Abstract: Time Series Classification (TSC) is a long-standing research problem that has gained increasing attention in recent years with the rapid growth of large-scale temporal data. Despite substantial progress enabled by deep learning, designing TSC models that are both accurate and interpretable remains a challenging task. Many existing approaches adopt a direct feature-to-label classification paradigm, by collapsing high-dimensional temporal embeddings into class logits via a single linear projection (often after global pooling), the paradigm conflates feature extraction and decision logic into an inseparable mapping.
  To address these limitations, we propose PDFTime, a prototype-guided framework that reformulates time series classification as a multi-stage decision process. Instead of direct feature-to-label mapping, PDFTime leverages learned prototypes to approximate class-conditional feature distributions in the latent space, enabling progressive discrimination through classification sub-tasks of varying granularity. To our knowledge, PDFTime is the first framework to reformulate time series classification as a decoupled, multi-stage similarity-based reasoning process, breaking the long-standing paradigm of direct, black-box feature-to-label mapping. Extensive evaluations demonstrate that PDFTime achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance across UEA and UCR benchmarks. Notably, it secures the top-$1$ accuracy on 80 out of 128 datasets in the UCR archive, significantly outperforming recent strong baselines in both consistency and generalization.

### [98] [From Reasoning Chains to Verifiable Subproblems: Curriculum Reinforcement Learning Enables Credit Assignment for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22074)
*Xitai Jiang,Zihan Tang,Wenze Lin,Yang Yue,Shenzhi Wang,Gao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SCRL通过将复杂数学问题分解为可验证的子问题课程，解决了强化学习中稀疏奖励和信用分配困难的问题，有效提升了大模型的复杂推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于结果的强化学习（RLVR）在大语言模型处理高难度推理任务时效率较低，原因是正确的最终答案样本稀少，且模型难以从失败路径中提取有效的部分进展信息（即缺乏细粒度的信用分配）。

Method: SCRL（子问题课程强化学习）：1. 从参考推理链中自动派生出可验证的子问题序列；2. 采用子问题级归一化方法，独立对每个子位置进行奖励归一化，从而实现细粒度的信用分配；3. 通过固化最终子问题为原问题，逐步引导模型从简单推理过渡到复杂推理。

Result: 在七个数学推理基准测试中，SCRL的表现优于基准方法（如GRPO）。在Qwen3-4B-Base模型上平均准确率提升4.1个百分点，在Qwen3-14B-Base上提升1.9个百分点；在AIME24、AIME25和IMO-Bench等高难度数据集上，pass@1和pass@64指标均有显著提升。

Conclusion: SCRL通过将复杂的推理问题拆解为可验证的子问题序列，构建了有效的课程学习框架。这种方法不仅解决了稀疏奖励带来的梯度死区问题，还实现了无需外部奖励模型的细粒度信用分配，显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂数学推理任务中的表现。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown strong promise for LLM reasoning, but outcome-based RLVR remains inefficient on hard problems because correct final-answer rollouts are rare and sample-level credit assignment cannot use partial progress in failed attempts. We introduce SCRL (Subproblem Curriculum Reinforcement Learning), a curriculum RL framework that derives verifiable subproblems from reference reasoning chains and fixes the final subproblem as the original problem. This turns partial progress on hard problems into verifiable learning signals. Algorithmically, SCRL uses subproblem-level normalization, which normalizes rewards independently at each subproblem position and assigns the resulting advantages to the corresponding answer spans, enabling finer-grained credit assignment without external rubrics or reward models. Our analysis shows that subproblem curricula lift hard problems out of gradient dead zones, with larger relative gains as the original problem becomes harder. Across seven mathematical reasoning benchmarks, SCRL outperforms strong curriculum-learning baselines, improving average accuracy over GRPO by +4.1 points on Qwen3-4B-Base and +1.9 points on Qwen3-14B-Base. On AIME24, AIME25, and IMO-Bench, SCRL further improves pass@1 by +3.7 points and pass@64 by +4.6 points on Qwen3-4B-Base, indicating better exploration on hard reasoning problems.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Accurate modeling of aerodynamic loads is essential for understanding and predicting the responses of complex structural systems. However, these models often rely on simplifications of the true physical forces, introducing assumptions that can limit their accuracy. Validating such models becomes particularly challenging in the presence of noisy or incomplete data. To address this, we introduce a probabilistic physics-informed machine learning approach designed to reconstruct the underlying aerodynamic loads from noisy measurements of structural dynamic responses. The model avoids overfitting, eliminates the need for regularization schemes, and allows for the use of heterogeneous and multi-fidelity data during the training process. The efficacy of the approach is demonstrated through the reconstruction of aerodynamic loads on the Great Belt East Bridge, simulated under a linear unsteady assumption. Results show a strong agreement between true and predicted loads, particularly related to root mean squared errors, magnitude, phase angle and peak values of the signals. ### [101] [The Attribution Impossibility: No Feature Ranking Is Faithful, Stable, and Complete Under Collinearity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21492)
*Drake Caraker,Bryan Arnold,David Rhoads*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了特征共线性导致特征排序无法同时达到忠实、稳定和完整的根本性困境，并通过形式化方法验证了该局限性，提出了帕累托最优的集成方法DASH以提升归因稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决可解释人工智能（XAI）中长期存在的一个根本性缺陷：当输入特征存在共线性时，现有的特征排序方法无法同时满足“忠实性”、“稳定性和“完整性”这三个基本准则。研究者希望通过理论证明和形式化验证，揭示这一 impossibility（不可能定理）的本质，并寻找改进方案。

Method: 1. 数学建模：量化了在四种不同模型类中，共线性如何导致归因不稳定性；2. 理论推导：证明了特征排序在共线性下的“二分法”困境；3. 提出算法：设计了DASH（Diversified Aggregation of SHAP）以实现帕累托最优；4. 形式化验证：使用Lean 4定理证明器完成了305个定理的机械化验证，确保结论的严谨性；5. 实证分析：通过77个公共数据集验证了不稳定性问题的普遍性。

Result: 1. 证明了在共线性条件下，特征排序不可避免地存在不稳定性；2. 将所有归因方法划分为“忠实-完整型”（不稳定）和“集成型”（如DASH，稳定且能处理共线性对称特征）两大类；3. 发现68%的公共数据集存在显著的归因不稳定性；4. 证明了SHAP在特定条件下的不稳定性，且指出其在公平性审计中可能产生的误导性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过形式化验证揭示了特征重要性排序在共线性条件下的本质局限性。研究明确了“忠实且完整”与“稳定”之间的权衡不可避免，并提出DASH作为一种理论上最优的集成解决方案，为可解释人工智能（XAI）的可靠性提供了严谨的数学基础。

Abstract: No feature ranking can be simultaneously faithful, stable, and complete when features are collinear. For collinear pairs, ranking reduces to a coin flip. We prove this impossibility, quantify it for four model classes, resolve it via ensemble averaging (DASH), and machine-verify it with 305 Lean 4 theorems. We characterize the complete attribution design space: exactly two families of methods exist -- faithful-complete methods (unstable, with rankings that flip up to 50% of the time) and ensemble methods like DASH (stable, reporting ties for symmetric features) -- and no method lies outside this dichotomy. The impossibility is quantitative: the attribution ratio diverges as 1/(1-rho^2) for gradient boosting, is infinite for Lasso, and converges for random forests. DASH (Diversified Aggregation of SHAP) is provably Pareto-optimal among unbiased aggregations, achieving the Cramer-Rao variance bound with a tight ensemble size formula. In a survey of 77 public datasets, 68% exhibit attribution instability. Switching to conditional SHAP does not escape the impossibility when features have equal causal effects. The framework includes practical diagnostics -- a Z-test workflow and single-model screening tool -- and has direct consequences for fairness auditing: SHAP-based proxy discrimination audits are provably unreliable under collinearity. The design space theorem, diagnostics, and impossibility are mechanically verified in Lean 4 (305 theorems from 16 axioms, 0 sorry) -- to our knowledge, the first formally verified impossibility in explainable AI.

</details>


### [102] [Short-Term-to-Long-Term Memory Transfer for Knowledge Graphs under Partial Observability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22142)
*Taewoon Kim,Vincent François-Lavet,Michael Cochez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种神经符号化的强化学习方法，通过让智能体显式地决定哪些观测事实应存入长期记忆，有效解决了部分可观测环境下有限内存的管理问题，并在导航任务中取得了优于传统序列模型的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于记忆的强化学习方法通常缺乏对短期记忆向长期记忆转移过程的显式建模，且在处理部分可观测环境时，难以在有限的内存空间内高效地筛选和保留关键的符号化观测信息。

Method: 提出了一种神经符号化的基于价值（value-based）的决策框架，将短期缓冲区内的观测三元组视为待处理对象。智能体通过共享参数的逐项（per-item）Q学习来决定保留或丢弃哪些信息，并结合时间差分（TD）更新机制处理变长的短期缓冲区，最终实现向长期记忆的有效转移。

Result: 在RoomKG基准测试中，该方法在长期记忆容量为128的情况下，超越了包括带有时间标注的符号化基线以及基于LSTM/Transformer的序列基线。分析显示，智能体能有效保留导航和查询相关的关键事实，同时剔除低价值信息。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在部分可观测的强化学习场景中，通过神经符号化的决策机制对观测到的知识进行显式的“存/弃”筛选，能显著提升有限内存下的智能体表现。这种方法不仅优于传统的序列建模方法，还增强了决策的可解释性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning under partial observability requires deciding what information to retain, yet most memory-based approaches do not explicitly model short-term-to-long-term transfer of symbolic observations. We study this transfer process in a temporal knowledge-graph memory setting and cast it as a neuro-symbolic value-based decision problem: for each observed triple, the agent chooses whether to keep or drop it before long-term insertion. To handle variable-sized short-term buffers, we use a per-item Q-learning design with shared parameters and a practical temporal-difference update over matched items across consecutive steps. On the RoomKG benchmark at long-term memory capacity 128, learned transfer decisions outperform symbolic and neural baselines, including symbolic baselines with temporal annotations and history-based LSTM/Transformer baselines. Across transfer-policy ablations, a lightweight local short-term-only variant performs best, and step-level behavior shows that the policy keeps navigation- and query-relevant facts while discarding lower-value candidate facts, supporting explicit and interpretable memory decisions under memory constraints.

### [103] [Algebraic Machine Learning for Small-to-Medium Datasets Is Competitive against Strong Standard Baselines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22155)
*David Mendez,Fernando Martin-Maroto,Gonzalo G. de Polavieja*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出并评估了代数机器学习（AML），证明了该基于代数结构分解的方法无需超参数调优和交叉验证，即可在小样本图像和表格数据上达到甚至超越现代主流学习模型的性能，展示了其通用的归纳偏差优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 符号学习方法通常被认为在现实的监督学习任务中难以与现代统计机器学习模型竞争。本文旨在挑战这一观点，通过评估代数机器学习（AML）框架，探究其在无需数值优化和交叉验证的情况下，是否能在不同规模的图像和表格数据分类任务中实现具有竞争力的性能。

Method: AML 摒弃了基于数值优化的传统学习范式，转而采用代数结构的亚直积分解（subdirect decomposition）进行学习。该方法通过通用的代数归纳偏差建模，无需针对特定任务进行超参数调优，也不依赖于交叉验证过程。

Result: 在 50 到 2000 个训练样本的小中型图像数据集上，AML 优于包括 CNN 在内的多种交叉验证基准模型；在同规模的表格数据集上，虽然 XGBoost 表现最优，但 AML 的性能与 LightGBM 和随机森林等包含任务特定偏差的方法相当。

Conclusion: 代数机器学习（AML）作为一种无需超参数调整和交叉验证的符号学习框架，在小样本数据集上展现出了与深度学习和传统集成学习模型竞争的潜力，证明了代数归纳偏差在处理多样化数据任务中的有效性和通用性。

Abstract: Symbolic methods are generally not considered competitive with strong modern learners on realistic supervised tasks. We evaluate Algebraic Machine Learning (AML), a framework that learns through subdirect decomposition of algebraic structure rather than numerical optimization, against standard baselines on image and tabular classification across varying training-set sizes. We find that AML trained only on training data without using validation or cross-validation outperforms a family of cross-validated baseline methods including CNNs on small to medium image datasets (50--2000 training examples). On tabular datasets in the same size range, XGBoost is overall the best performing method, but AML is nonetheless comparable to methods incorporating task-specific biases such as LightGBM and random forests. AML achieves this competitive performance across two very different types of datasets using a generic algebraic inductive bias, rather than the modality-specific biases built into standard baselines like CNNs for images or XGBoost for tabular data, and requires no cross validation because it has no task-dependent hyperparameters to tune.

### [104] [One-Way Policy Optimization for Self-Evolving LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22156)
*Shuo Yang,Jinda Lu,Kexin Huang,Chiyu Ma,Shaohang Wei,Yuyang Liu,Guoyin Wang,Jingren Zhou,Li Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对RLVR中参考策略约束抑制性能提升的问题，提出了单向策略优化（OWPO）。通过解耦优化方向与更新幅度，并结合不对称重加权与“棘轮效应”，实现了大语言模型推理能力的持续、稳定提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于验证器的强化学习（RLVR）在扩展大语言模型推理能力方面表现出色，但奖励的稀疏性导致训练不稳定。现有方法常通过基于参考策略的Token级约束来稳定训练，但这会无差别地惩罚策略的所有偏离，导致当模型尝试超越参考策略时，其性能增益被错误地抑制。

Method: 提出了单向策略优化（OWPO）方法，核心是解耦优化方向与更新幅度。具体包括：1. 不对称重加权：对落后于参考策略的偏差执行“加速对齐”，对超越参考策略的偏差执行“增益锁定”；2. 迭代式参考更新：通过迭代更新参考策略，引入“棘轮效应”以巩固性能增益。

Result: 实验结果表明，OWPO方法在各项任务中均优于强基线模型（如DAPO、OPD和MOPD），有效打破了固定先验的瓶颈，使模型能够摆脱对外部参考模型的依赖，实现持续的性能自我演进。

Conclusion: OWPO通过将验证器奖励的优化方向与参考策略的调节作用解耦，成功解决了RLVR中传统约束方法抑制模型性能提升的问题。该方法通过不对称重加权机制和“棘轮效应”，实现了大语言模型推理能力的持续自演进，打破了对外部参考模型的依赖，在多项基准测试中表现优于现有的DAPO、OPD和MOPD等方法。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a promising paradigm for scaling reasoning capabilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the sparsity of binary verifier rewards often leads to low efficiency and optimization instability. To stabilize training, existing methods typically impose token-level constraints relative to a reference policy. We identify that such constraints penalize deviations indiscriminately; this can flip verifier-determined direction when the policy attempts to outperform the reference, thereby suppressing gains. To resolve this, we propose One-Way Policy Optimization (OWPO), a method based on the principle of decoupling optimization direction from update magnitude. In OWPO, the verifier dictates the update direction, while the reference policy serves only to adjust the magnitude. Specifically, OWPO applies asymmetric reweighting: it performs Accelerated Alignment for inferior deviations (where the policy lags behind the reference) and Gain Locking for superior deviations (where the policy surpasses the reference). Furthermore, by incorporating iterative reference updates, OWPO creates a ``Ratchet Effect'' that continuously consolidates gains. Experimental results demonstrate that OWPO outperforms strong baselines, including DAPO, OPD, and MOPD, breaking the bottleneck of fixed priors to enable continuous self-evolution without reliance on external reference models.

</details>


### [105] [Maestro: Reinforcement Learning to Orchestrate Hierarchical Model-Skill Ensembles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22177)
*Jinyang Wu,Guocheng Zhai,Ruihan Jin,Yuhao Shen,Zhengxi Lu,Fan Zhang,Haoran Luo,Zheng Lian,Zhengqi Wen,Jianhua Tao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Maestro 是一种基于强化学习的智能体编排框架，它通过一个轻量级协调器动态调度多种专家模型和技能，无需单一超大规模模型即可在复杂多模态任务上实现性能超越，并具有优秀的泛化性与计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的智能体框架多依赖于单一的大语言模型，难以充分利用不同模型和技能在特定领域的优势，导致在处理复杂多模态任务时存在性能瓶颈。因此，作者旨在设计一种能协同调用异构专家模型与技能库的框架，以优化任务执行效率和准确性。

Method: 提出 Maestro 框架，将多模态任务建模为基于层级模型-技能注册表的序列决策过程。采用强化学习（RL）训练一个轻量级（4B）协调器，该协调器能够动态决定何时调用外部专家、选择哪种模型-技能组合以及何时终止任务，无需步骤级监督。

Result: 在十个多模态基准测试中，仅使用 4B 参数的 Maestro 达到 70.1% 的平均准确率，超过了 GPT-5 (69.3%) 和 Gemini-2.5-Pro (68.7%)。此外，该协调策略表现出极佳的泛化能力，在不重新训练的情况下，通过扩展外部专家库即可在未见过的任务中超越所有闭源基线模型，且保持了高计算效率和低延迟。

Conclusion: Maestro 通过将异构模型和技能的编排转化为强化学习决策过程，有效突破了单一模型的性能瓶颈。该研究证明，通过轻量级协调器动态调度专家模型和技能库，不仅能实现超越顶级闭源模型的性能，还具备极强的可扩展性和泛化能力，为构建高效、灵活的智能体系统提供了新范式。

Abstract: The proliferation of large language models (LLMs) and modular skills has endowed autonomous agents with increasingly powerful capabilities. Existing frameworks typically rely on monolithic LLMs and fixed logic to interface with these skills. This gives rise to a critical bottleneck: different LLMs offer distinct advantages across diverse domains, yet current frameworks fail to exploit the complementary strengths of models and skills, thereby limiting their performance on downstream tasks. In this paper, we present Maestro (Multimodal Agent for Expert-Skill Targeted Reinforced Orchestration), a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-driven orchestration framework that reframes heterogeneous multimodal tasks as a sequential decision-making process over a hierarchical model-skill registry. Rather than consolidating all knowledge into a single model, Maestro trains a lightweight policy to dynamically compose ensembles of frozen expert models and a two-tier skill library, deciding at each step whether to invoke an external expert, which model-skill pair to select, and when to terminate. The policy is optimized via outcome-based RL, requiring no step-level supervision. We evaluate Maestro across ten representative multimodal benchmarks spanning mathematical reasoning, chart understanding, high-resolution perception, and domain-specific analysis. With only a 4B orchestrator, Maestro achieves an average accuracy of 70.1%, surpassing both GPT-5 (69.3%) and Gemini-2.5-Pro (68.7%). Crucially, the learned coordination policy generalizes to unseen models and skills without retraining: augmenting the registry with out-of-domain experts yields a 59.5% average on four challenging benchmarks, outperforming all closed-source baselines. Maestro further maintains high computational efficiency with low latency. The source code is available at https://github.com/jinyangwu/Maestro.

### [106] [Beyond Euclidean Proximity: Repairing Latent World Models with Horizon-Matched Trajectory Reachability Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22164)
*Liangyu Li,Shengzhi Wang,Qingwen Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了轨迹可达性度量（TRM），这是一种通过成对头部监督学习修复潜在世界模型终端排名偏差的方法，显著提升了模型在复杂长程规划任务中的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在当前的潜在模型预测控制（Latent MPC）中，通常使用潜在空间中终端状态与目标状态之间的欧几里得距离来对候选序列进行排名。研究发现，这种原始距离假设往往无法正确捕捉与可达性相关的变量，导致规划器在决策时选择了错误的路径，尤其在复杂环境下表现不佳。

Method: 提出了一种轨迹可达性度量（TRM）方法，作为固定潜在世界模型的后处理终端排名器。该方法通过训练一个小型成对头部（pairwise head），利用已有的轨迹结构进行监督学习。其关键创新在于“水平感知监督”（horizon-aware supervision），即在广泛且平衡的时间间隔上进行训练，以匹配长程规划的需求。TRM可以完全替代或与原有的潜在MSE距离成本混合使用。

Result: 在TwoRoom基准测试中，使用TRM使LeWorldModel的成功率从7.0%提升至97.0%，并将PLDM基准从32.7%提升至84.0%。分析表明，原始潜在MSE往往因包含大量无关信息而导致排序偏差，而TRM通过过滤无关特征并聚焦于关键可达性信息，显著改善了规划器的排序效果。在PushT任务中，TRM同样展现了在连续操作任务中提升性能的潜力。

Conclusion: 轨迹可达性度量（TRM）为现有潜在世界模型提供了一种有效的“事后修复”机制。它证明了在潜在空间中，单纯的欧几里得距离往往无法正确反映到达目标的可达性，而引入基于时域监督的成对度量可以显著修正规划器的决策质量，为解决长距离任务规划提供了一种低成本且高性能的方案。

Abstract: Latent world models can contain the state needed for control, yet their terminal-cost interface can expose the planner to the wrong decision-relevant information. In common latent MPC, candidate sequences are ranked by Euclidean distance between predicted terminal and goal latent states; this assumes that raw latent distance weights reachability-relevant variables correctly. We propose trajectory reachability metrics (TRM), a post-hoc terminal-ranking method for fixed latent world models. TRM trains a small pairwise head from logged trajectory structure and uses it as a replacement or hybrid cost; the encoder, dynamics, sampler, optimizer, and evaluation manifests remain fixed. The key design choice is horizon-aware supervision: the metric is trained on broad, balanced temporal separations to match the long-horizon terminal candidate ranking problem. On a hard TwoRoom benchmark, raw latent planning with LeWorldModel (LeWM) reaches 7.0% success, while full-horizon TRM reaches 97.0%; shuffled temporal-label controls stay at 0.0%. The same recipe improves a PLDM baseline from 32.7% to 84.0% across three seeds, and a short-horizon TRM variant reaches only 35.0% with the 100,000 pair budget. In TwoRoom, we provide mechanistic evidence for why TRM works: XY position is linearly decodable (R^2=0.998), yet raw latent MSE misranks candidates; the XY-probe rowspace accounts for less than 1% of terminal-goal latent MSE but carries most candidate-quality signal; and SCSA audits show that TRM improves the ordering and selected endpoint seen by the planner. On PushT go50/go75, TRM-style task-state metrics improve SCSA ranking and selected final distance more cleanly than closed-loop success, motivating auxiliary hybrid costs in continuous manipulation. TRM is the planner-facing repair, and audits explain when terminal reachability metrics should replace or augment raw latent proximity.

### [107] [Survive or Collapse: The Asymmetric Roles of Data Gating and Reward Grounding in Self-Play RL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22217)
*Sophia Xiao Pu,Zhaotian Weng,Chengzhi Liu,Jayanth Srinivasa,Gaowen Liu,William Yang Wang,Xin Eric Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出，大模型自我博弈强化学习的训练崩溃主要源于数据筛选机制的缺失而非奖励函数设计不当。研究表明，通过严格的数据筛选门控，即便在缺乏真值反馈的情况下也能实现稳定的模型训练，并揭示了过早引入真值反馈可能反而导致模型陷入虚假自洽的“接地气的提议者悖论”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我博弈强化学习在提升语言模型推理能力方面表现出色，但普遍面临训练崩溃和不稳定性问题。现有研究多聚焦于奖励设计，而本文旨在探索自我博弈稳定性的底层逻辑，并揭示了数据筛选与奖励机制在其中的非对称作用。

Method: 研究团队通过受控实验（Python输出预测任务和确定性DSL孪生任务）构建了基准，并引入了“筛选门（gate）”作为核心变量。研究者系统地对比了不同筛选严格程度与多种奖励函数（包括无真值访问的自洽性奖励）的组合，通过连续严格度参数 $\varepsilon$ 分析了训练过程的相变现象，并解构了提议者（Proposer）与求解者（Solver）的协同演化机制。

Result: 实验证明筛选机制与奖励机制存在非对称性：严格的筛选足以保证稳定性，即使缺乏真值奖励；反之，若移除筛选机制，任何奖励变体都无法防止崩溃。研究还观察到了两阶段相变现象，并指出数据门控是制约自我博弈稳定性的关键瓶颈。

Conclusion: 自我博弈学习的稳定性主要取决于数据层面的筛选机制（Data-level Gate），而非奖励函数的校准。严格的筛选机制是实现自我博弈长期稳定的关键，同时也揭示了“接地气的提议者悖论”，即过早接触真值反而可能加速模型陷入虚假的自洽吸引子中。

Abstract: Self-play reinforcement learning trains language models on their own generated tasks, co-evolving a proposer and solver without human labels. Recent systems report strong reasoning gains, but collapse and instability are widely observed and poorly understood. The dominant response treats this as a reward-design problem. We argue instead that self-play stability is governed by two distinct levers: a data-level gate that decides which proposer-generated tasks enter the training pool, and the reward signal that updates the policy on tasks already admitted. Through controlled experiments on a Python output-prediction task and a deterministic-DSL twin task that strips pretraining priors, output ambiguity, and executor noise, we find the two levers are asymmetric. A strict gate is sufficient for stability under every reward variant we test, including a self-consistency reward with no access to ground truth; while no reward variant is sufficient once the gate is removed. This asymmetry exposes a counter-intuitive coupling we call the Grounded Proposer Paradox: a proposer with ground-truth access accelerates collapse faster than an ungrounded one when paired with a self-consistency solver, by concentrating training on clean tasks that form the fastest path to a spurious self-consistent attractor. Replacing the binary gate with a continuous strictness parameter $\varepsilon$ further reveals a two-stage phase transition: training-side metrics decouple at low $\varepsilon$, while validation accuracy holds until $\varepsilon$ is much higher. Data-level gating, not reward calibration, is the binding constraint on self-play stability.

TL;DR: 该研究发现，针对AI安全分类器的成员推理攻击可以通过识别模型置信度最低的“边界样本”来大幅提升效率，成功恢复敏感的训练数据，并提出通过噪声注入来增强模型隐私保护。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了一种“边界目标选择策略”（boundary-targeted selection strategy），专门识别模型置信度最低的训练样本。这种策略利用了模型在处理模糊训练数据时产生记忆化现象的特性，从而放大攻击者推断样本是否属于训练集的信号。

Result: 实验结果表明，该攻击方法在检测需要情感支持用户的分类器上，能够以5%的假阳性率恢复19%的训练对话。这一攻击效果是现有最先进成员推理攻击方法的3.5倍，证明了边界样本是隐私泄露的关键突破口。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了安全分类器在训练数据隐私方面的脆弱性，证明了基于模型置信度的边界样本对于成员推理攻击具有极高的信息价值，并指出简单的内容过滤不足以抵御此类攻击，但适当的噪声注入策略可以有效减轻隐私泄露风险。

Abstract: Safety classifiers are essential safeguards within generative AI systems, filtering harmful content or identifying at-risk users when interacting with large language models. Despite their necessity, these models are trained on sensitive datasets including discussions of self-harm and mental health, raising important, yet poorly understood, privacy concerns. Membership inference attacks (MIAs) allow adversaries to infer membership of examples used to train models. In this work, we hypothesize that identifying the examples on which the classifier is least confident are informative for an adversary to infer membership. This reflects a localized failure of generalization, where the model relies on memorization to resolve ambiguity in the training set. To investigate this, we introduce a new boundary-targeted selection strategy that identifies low confidence examples that amplify the signal of an examples membership within a training set. Our experimental results show that an adversary can recover 19\% of the conversations a safety classifier flagged as indicating user distress, at a 5\% false-positive rate, on a classifier fine-tuned for detecting a user who may require emotional support. This is $3.5$ times more than attacking using state-of-the-art MIA methods alone. Finally, we characterize the boundary laying examples and show that content-based filtering is ineffective for protection, and existing noise strategies can effectively mitigate susceptibility of these examples.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然GPU在连续优化领域取得了巨大成功，但其在处理包含离散变量、组合结构和非线性目标的优化问题（如带基数约束的广义线性模型）时仍面临挑战，主要痛点在于分支定界算法中节点处理的顺序性以及CPU与GPU之间频繁的数据交换导致效率低下。

Result: 实验表明，该框架在具有挑战性的实例上实现了1到2个数量级的速度提升，并能达到零最优性间隙。此外，该框架还能有效收集Rashomon集，支持变量重要性分析及模型选择等下游统计任务。

Abstract: GPUs have significantly accelerated first-order methods for large-scale optimization, especially in continuous optimization. However, this success has not transferred cleanly to problems with discrete variables, combinatorial structure, and nonlinear objectives, such as certifying optimal solutions for cardinality-constrained generalized linear models. Major challenges include the sequential processing of heterogeneous nodes in branch and bound (BnB) and frequent data movement between the CPU and GPU. We propose a simple, generic, and modular CPU--GPU framework that processes multiple BnB nodes in batches on GPUs. The framework is built around a small set of GPU-efficient routines and uses padding together with lightweight custom kernels to handle irregular node data structures. Experiments show one to two orders of magnitude speedups and zero optimality gap on challenging instances. The framework can also be extended to collect the entire Rashomon set, enabling downstream statistical analysis such as variable-importance analysis and model selection under secondary user-specific measures (e.g., AUC in classification).

### [110] [Structured-Sparse Attention for Entity Tracking with Subquadratic Sequence Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22476)
*Hangyue Zhao,Paul Caillon,Erwan Fagnou,Alexandre Allauzen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用注意力权重局部稀疏性的分块评估策略，有效将Transformer中多跳注意力算子的复杂度从二次方降低至次二次方，在保证准确率的同时大幅提升了长序列追踪任务的推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在实体追踪任务中，Transformer等模型虽然能够通过多跳状态传播压缩层数，但其全量注意力计算在大序列上代价昂贵，难以满足高效推理的需求。因此，迫切需要一种在保持精度的同时降低注意力机制计算复杂度的方法。

Method: 研究观察到学习得到的注意力权重具有强结构性，主要集中在局部对角块区域，存在少量块间残差。基于此，作者推导了一种分块评估的解析式算子（resolvent-style operator），在保持块内交互精确性的同时，通过缩减系统处理块间交互。该方法的计算复杂度降至 O(n^4/3 d)。

Result: 在受控的追踪基准测试中，该方法在匹配全量算子精度的前提下，标准化测量下的实际运行时间减少了12%至29%；相比于紧凑型全量Transformer，在相同准确率下速度提升高达2.4倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种基于分块评估的注意力优化方法，成功降低了复杂序列建模任务中的计算复杂度。实验表明，当同时演化的属性数量超过注意力头数时，模型性能会显著下降，这为未来研究跨头信息交互及扩展性提供了方向。

Abstract: Entity tracking requires maintaining and updating latent states for entities and attributes over long sequences. Recent task-specific attention operators can compress deep Transformer stacks into a few layers by performing multi-hop state propagation within a single layer, but their dense evaluation remains expensive. We show that in this setting, learned attention is strongly structured: most mass concentrates in local block-diagonal neighborhoods with a light cross-block residue. Exploiting this, we derive a blockwise evaluation of a resolvent-style operator that keeps within-block interactions exact and routes cross-block interactions through a reduced system. The resulting evaluation is subquadratic in sequence length $O(n^{4/3}d)$ (and $O(n^{7/3})$ when $d\approx n$). On controlled tracking benchmarks, our method matches the dense operator's accuracy while reducing wall-clock time by $12-29\%$ under a standardized measurement protocol, and is up to $2.4 \times$ faster than a compact dense Transformer at comparable exact-match accuracy. We further provide ablations over block size and model capacity, and identify a limitation: performance collapses when the number of simultaneously evolving properties exceeds the number of attention heads.

### [111] [Bandit Convex Optimization with Gradient Prediction Adaptivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22191)
*Shuche Wang,Adarsh Barik,Vincent Y. F. Tan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了带宽凸优化（BCO）中梯度预测对提升学习效果的作用。研究指出，单点反馈下预测无效；但在双点反馈下，通过提出的 TP-VR-OPT 算法，实现了遗憾界与预测误差的主动对齐，达到了理论最优的预测自适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探究在带宽凸优化（BCO）中，利用外部梯度预测信息是否能在最坏情况下提升遗憾（regret）界限。特别是针对单点反馈下预测收益受限的理论瓶颈，寻求改进方案以实现预测自适应性。

Method: 1. 提出了“双点方差缩减乐观梯度下降”（TP-VR-OPT）算法，该算法使用一种新的梯度估计器，其方差直接与预测误差相关而非梯度范数。2. 建立了单点与双点反馈下的信息论下界。3. 开发了无需先验知识（如预测误差或时间跨度）的自适应变体。4. 将框架扩展至非平稳环境，实现了对预测误差和比较器路径长度的双重自适应。

Result: 1. 证明了在单点反馈协议下，即使预测误差极小，也无法避免 Ω(√T) 的遗憾下界。2. 在双点反馈下，证明了 TP-VR-OPT 算法的遗憾界为 O(√(d·E[ST]))。3. 建立了 Ω(√E[ST]) 的信息论下界，证明了该算法在维度因子 d 的差距内是最优的。4. 实现了对非平稳环境下的动态遗憾控制。

Conclusion: 本文通过引入方差缩减技术，成功克服了单点反馈下梯度预测无法提升遗憾界限的限制。在双点反馈协议下，TP-VR-OPT 算法达到了预测自适应性的最优遗憾界限，并进一步证明了该算法在非平稳环境下的有效性，为带宽凸优化提供了鲁棒且高效的学习框架。

Abstract: Bandit convex optimization (BCO) is a fundamental online learning framework with partial feedback, where the learner observes only the loss incurred at the chosen decision point in each round. In this work, we investigate whether optimistic gradient predictions can improve worst-case regret guarantees in a prediction-adaptive manner. Specifically, given gradient predictions $m_t$, we seek regret bounds that scale with the cumulative prediction error $S_T=\sum_{t=1}^T \|\nabla f_t(x_t)-m_t\|^2.$ We first establish a negative result: under the single-point feedback protocol, an unavoidable $Ω(\sqrt{T})$ regret lower bound persists even when $S_T=o(T)$, showing that the variance of gradient estimation fundamentally obscures the benefit of accurate predictions. To overcome this barrier, we propose \emph{Two-Point Variance-Reduced Optimistic Gradient Descent} (TP-VR-OPT) for the two-point feedback setting. The key idea is a novel variance-reduced gradient estimator whose variance scales with the prediction error rather than the gradient norm. This yields a regret bound of $O\big(\sqrt{d\,\mathbb{E}[S_T]}\big),$ where $d$ is the decision dimension. Complementing this result, we establish an information-theoretic lower bound that scales as $Ω(\sqrt{\mathbb{E}[S_T]})$, providing a fundamental characterization of the best achievable prediction-adaptive regret and showing that TP-VR-OPT is optimal up to a factor of $\sqrt d$. We further develop adaptive variants that eliminate the need for prior knowledge of $\mathbb{E}[S_T]$ or the horizon $T$, and extend our framework to non-stationary environments, establishing dynamic regret guarantees that adapt simultaneously to the cumulative prediction error and the comparator path length.

</details>

*Manuel Noah Riesen,Peter Alfred von Niederhäusern*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为了解决思维图（GoT）依赖人工预设结构且灵活性不足的问题，本文提出了强化思维图（RGoT），通过强化学习自动生成适应任务复杂度的推理路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的思维图（GoT）范式虽然能提升复杂问题的求解能力，但其思维图结构通常需要人工预先定义，缺乏针对不同问题复杂度的自适应性，且需要极高的领域知识，限制了其实际应用。

Method: 提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的框架RGoT，其核心逻辑是在预定义的思维操作集基础上，利用RL智能体动态地决定执行哪些思维操作以及它们的组合方式，从而自动构建适应特定问题的“思维图”。

Result: 实验结果表明，在受限环境下，RGoT能够成功地针对任务复杂度自动构建出最优的思维图结构，实现了推理过程的自动化与自适应化。

Conclusion: RGoT通过强化学习实现了推理路径（即思维图）的自动化构建，证明了LLM能够根据任务复杂度自适应地调整思维结构，克服了传统GoT框架依赖人工预设固定思维图的僵化问题，是迈向自主推理系统的重要一步。

Abstract: Graph of Thoughts (GoT), a generalized form of recent prompting paradigms for large language models (LLMs), has been shown to be useful for elaborate problem solving. By executing a graph of operations, thoughts of the LLM are structured as an arbitrary graph, forming the actual graph of thoughts. Originally, the graph of operations is defined manually, which requires in-depth knowledge about the solution of the problem to solve. Such a static graph of operations is rigid and therefore lacks adaptability. We propose Reinforced Graph of Thoughts (RGoT), an automated approach to the GoT prompting paradigm that leverages reinforcement learning (RL) to adaptively generate a graph of operations from a human-defined set. Results indicate that, under certain constraints, it is possible to construct graphs of operations adaptively to the task's complexity in an automated way.

### [113] [A Tutorial on Diffusion Theory: From Differential Equations to Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22586)
*Jiayi Fu,Yuxia Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过微分方程（ODE/SDE）的视角，为扩散模型构建了统一的理论框架，证明了现有模型训练目标的等价性，并深入剖析了反向生成过程与采样算法的数学本质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前扩散模型的研究领域存在多种视角和术语（如DDPM、DDIM等），缺乏一个统一的理论框架。本文旨在通过微分方程（SDE/ODE）的视角，将这些看似不同的方法和技术归纳在同一个数学体系下，以揭示其内在联系与本质。

Method: 本文采用基于微分方程的分析方法，从条件高斯前向过程出发，通过边缘化处理推导扩散模型的正向与反向SDE及概率流ODE；建立了分数函数（Score function）与训练目标之间的等价性；并分析了多种采样策略（如DPM-Solver及分类器引导）的数学原理。

Result: 论文证明了标准噪声预测目标与分数匹配目标等价；阐明了DDPM采样本质上是离散化的反向SDE过程，而DDIM采样对应于反向概率流ODE过程，并系统梳理了引导采样和高效求解器在这一框架下的运作机制。

Conclusion: 通过微分方程的统一视角，本文确立了扩散模型在分数匹配、概率流ODE和随机微分方程（SDE）框架下的理论基础，明确了现有流行模型（DDPM/DDIM）的数学实质，为扩散模型的研究与应用提供了严谨的理论指导。

Abstract: This tutorial develops diffusion models from the viewpoint of differential equations. We begin with the conditional Gaussian forward process and show that this path admits both an ordinary differential equation (ODE) representation and a stochastic differential equation (SDE) representation. Averaging the conditional process over the data distribution then yields marginalized forward ODE and SDE formulations that transport the data distribution $p_0=p_{\mathrm{data}}$ to a Gaussian prior $p_1=\mathcal{N}(0,I)$. We next derive the corresponding reverse-time dynamics, namely the reverse SDE and the reverse probability-flow ODE, both of which are governed by the marginal score $\grad\log p_t(x)$. This leads to a training objective for score estimation and shows that the standard noise-prediction objective is equivalent to score matching up to an additive constant independent of the model parameters. We then discuss sampling methods for the learned reverse dynamics, including DPM-Solver, as well as guided sampling through classifier guidance and classifier-free guidance. Finally, we compare DDPM and DDIM with the reverse SDE/ODE framework and show that they share the same training objective, while DDPM sampling corresponds to discrete reverse-SDE sampling and DDIM sampling corresponds to reverse-ODE sampling.

### [114] [Two is better than one: A Collapse-free Multi-Reward RLIF Training Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22620)
*Shourov Joarder,Diganta Sikdar,Ahsan Habib Akash,Binod Bhattarai,Prashnna Gyawali*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有无监督大模型强化学习（RLIF）单一奖励导致的训练不稳定问题，本文提出了一种包含多重互补奖励、奖励归一化及新型正则化机制的框架，实现了无需外部人工监督即可达到接近监督学习水平的稳健推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的无监督RLIF方法通常依赖单一内部奖励，容易引发奖励破解（reward hacking）、熵崩塌及推理结构退化的问题。研究旨在寻找一种更稳健、无需人工标注的强化学习训练方案。

Method: 提出了一种多重奖励RLIF框架，包含两个互补组件：基于聚类投票的答案级奖励和基于token级自置信度的完成级奖励。同时引入GDPO归一化以解决奖励尺度不平衡问题，以及KL-Cov正则化以防止熵崩塌并维持探索能力。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成基准测试中，该方法显著提升了无监督RL训练的稳定性和鲁棒性，性能接近有监督的RLVR方法。

Conclusion: 多重内部奖励结合针对性正则化（KL-Cov），能够有效支撑大模型在无需外部监督的情况下的长程推理，在保持模型探索能力的同时，实现了接近有监督强化学习（RLVR）的性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has substantially improved the reasoning ability of LLMs, but often depends on external supervision from human annotations or gold-standard solutions. Reinforcement learning from internal feedback (RLIF) has recently emerged as a scalable unsupervised alternative, using signals extracted from the model itself. However, existing RLIF methods typically rely on a single internal reward, which can lead to reward hacking, entropy collapse, and degraded reasoning structure. We propose a multi-reward RLIF framework that decomposes the training signal into two complementary components: an answer-level reward based on cluster voting and a completion-level reward based on token-wise self-certainty. To combine these signals robustly, we apply GDPO-based normalization to reduce reward-scale imbalance. We further introduce KL-Cov regularization, which targets low-entropy token distributions responsible for disproportionate entropy reduction, preserving exploration and preventing late-stage collapse. Across mathematical reasoning and code-generation benchmarks, our method improves stability and robustness over prior unsupervised RL approaches, while achieving performance close to supervised RLVR methods. These results show that complementary internal rewards, combined with targeted regularization, can support stable long-horizon reasoning without relying on external ground-truth supervision. Code will be released soon.

### [115] [Can Transformers Learn to Verify During Backtracking Search?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22221)
*Yin Jun Phua,Tony Ribeiro,Tuan Nguyen,Katsumi Inoue*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文指出Transformer在学习回溯搜索时会错误地依赖历史路径而非当前状态，并提出了SSA机制和局部化技术，强制模型基于状态做出一致决策，从而提升了逻辑推理的稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前基于Transformer的推理系统通常采用在离线回溯搜索轨迹上进行自回归训练的方法。然而，这种基于累积轨迹的训练方式忽略了搜索任务的核心原则：最优决策应当仅依赖于当前的搜索状态，而与达到该状态的历史路径无关。作者旨在解决现有模型在处理序列化搜索轨迹时未能有效隔离状态与历史，导致决策不一致的问题。

Method: 1. 诊断：指出模型在累积轨迹上训练存在“状态特征分散”和“历史纠缠”缺陷。
2. 局部化（Localization）：重写决策块，将状态特征局部化，解决分散检索问题。
3. 选择性状态注意力（Selective State Attention, SSA）：通过设计特定的固定注意力掩码（Attention Mask），在结构上强制模型仅关注当前搜索状态，消除历史轨迹对决策的干扰。

Result: 在3-SAT、图着色、Blocks World和回溯解析等任务的测试中，SSA机制成功使模型在面对相同状态但不同历史路径时做出了一致的决策。相比之下，传统的因果语言模型基线无法达到这一要求。研究表明，该方法有效实现了搜索状态的隔离，并提出了推理阶段清理上下文的可能性。

Conclusion: 本文诊断出基于累积轨迹训练的Transformer模型在处理回溯搜索任务时存在“分散检索”和“历史纠缠”问题。通过局部化技术（Localization）和选择性状态注意力（SSA）机制，能够在无需修改训练目标或参数的情况下，迫使模型仅依赖当前搜索状态做出决策，从而显著提升了模型在逻辑推理任务中的鲁棒性和一致性。

Abstract: Backtracking search underlies classical constraint solvers, planners, and theorem provers. Recent transformer-based reasoning systems explore search trees over their own intermediate steps. A common training recipe fits an autoregressive next-token loss on offline solver traces. The model's input at each step is a cumulative trace of all prior decisions. The optimal continue-or-backtrack predictor depends only on the current search state, since two trajectories reaching the same state admit the same viable continuations. We show that decoder-only transformers trained on cumulative traces fail this requirement in two ways: the trace can scatter state features across many positions (scattered retrieval), and the predictor can condition on the trajectory rather than the state (history entanglement). We address scattered retrieval with localization, a trace-level fix that rewrites each decision block to expose state features locally. We address history entanglement with Selective State Attention (SSA), a fixed attention mask that enforces state-based decisions structurally without modifying training data, objective, or parameters. We focus on reactive verification, after propagation has exposed a contradiction. We test SSA on 3-SAT, graph coloring, Blocks World, and backtracking parsing. On same-state pairs that differ only in prior history, SSA emits identical decisions while a cumulative-trained causal baseline does not. Our contribution is a diagnostic of transformer behavior on serialized trajectory data, paired with a structural fix. Pretrained language models that search over their own reasoning steps may face the same failure. Our analysis opens up inference-time context clearing as a candidate way to apply the same isolation without retraining.

</details>


### [116] [ARC-STAR: Auditable Post-Hoc Correction for PDE Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22222)
*Chengze Li,Lingwei Wei,Li Sun,Hongbo Lv,Jie Yang,Hongrong Zhang,Kening Zheng,Wei-Chieh Huang,Enze Ma,Philip S. Yu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ARC-STAR是一种针对PDE基础模型的后处理框架，通过分层的全局偏差消除与局部动态精炼，在不修改预训练模型权重的情况下，显著提升了物理场模拟的精度与计算鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 预训练的PDE基础模型在处理未见流场时会产生逐步骤的误差漂移，且误差往往集中在特定空间区域，现有的全模型微调方法易导致模型稳定性下降，且简单的均匀后处理忽略了误差的空间异质性。

Method: 提出了一种名为ARC-STAR的后处理修正框架，包含三个阶段：1. 全局矫正器（Global corrector）消除基础模型的大范围偏差；2. 分块局部精炼器（Blockwise local refiner）处理残留误差；3. 部署阶段的无标签评分系统（Label-free score），根据计算预算动态路由高风险区域的精炼。该方法无需对原预训练模型进行微调。

Result: 在五个流体基准测试的十个实验场景中，ARC-STAR在所有场景下均将速度推演误差降低了至少36倍。其中，全局阶段减少了原始模型91%-99%的误差，局部阶段进一步减少了剩余残差的94.4%。

Conclusion: ARC-STAR通过模块化的修正架构，有效解决了PDE基础模型在处理未见流体数据时的累积误差问题，证明了在保持预训练模型“冷冻”状态下，通过分层矫正实现高精度与计算效率的平衡是可行的。

Abstract: Partial differential equation (PDE) foundation models are pretrained networks that forecast how physical fields like velocity and pressure evolve from a single reusable solver. On unfamiliar flows their predictions drift step by step, errors concentrate in a few regions, yet retraining destabilizes the network and uniform post-hoc correction overlooks this spatial concentration. To address this, we propose a frozen-solver post-hoc correction framework, Adaptive Risk-Calibrated Spatial Triage for Auditable Refinement (ARC-STAR). ARC-STAR organizes correction into three stages: a global corrector removes broad solver bias, a blockwise local refiner cleans the post-global residual, and, at deployment, a label-free score routes refinement to high-risk blocks under a compute budget. The framework is designed to be (i) frozen-host, preserving the pretrained solver without fine-tuning; (ii) auditable, with global and local stages trained and evaluated separately for measurable contributions; and (iii) budget-aware, using a blockwise interface that either refines the full field or routes limited compute to high-risk regions. Across five flow benchmarks spanning ten regime cells, ARC-STAR is the only method that cuts velocity rollout error by at least 36x over raw Poseidon on every cell. The global stage reduces raw host error by 91-99%, and the local stage further reduces the remaining post-global residual by up to 94.4%. Our code implementation is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/arc_star.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 本文从理论上证明了Transformer模型在生成序列时存在本质限制，即其可访问的序列空间随提示词长度线性增长，且在超过临界阈值后呈指数级衰减。这些发现解释了Transformer在处理复制或填充等简单序列任务时的表现缺陷，并为理解Transformer的生成能力边界提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study how we can leverage only a handful of characteristics of a transformer's architecture to closely predict the number of different sequences it can output, both qualitatively and quantitatively. We provide an upper bound depending on the length of the prompt, which we show empirically to be tight up to a factor less than 10, across architectures and model sizes. Our analysis also provides a theoretical explanation for previously observed empirical failures of transformers on simple sequence tasks, such as copying and cramming. Formally, we prove that (i) the maximal length of accessible sequences (those that the transformer can output for some prompt) grows linearly with the prompt length, (ii) beyond a critical threshold, the proportion of accessible sequences decays exponentially with sequence length, and (iii) the linear coefficient relating prompt length to accessible sequence length admits a theoretical upper bound. Notably, these results hold even with unbounded context and computation time.
