### [160] [Ternary Decision Trees with Locally-Adaptive Uncertainty Zones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22740)
*William Smits*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三元决策树模型，通过在决策边界处引入加权不确定区域，成功解决了标准决策树对边界样本分类置信度不足的问题，显著提升了模型在各类数据集上的预测准确度与实用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统决策树利用硬二元阈值划分特征空间，无法区分决策边界附近的实例与远离边界的实例，导致在边界附近的预测置信度缺失，难以应对不确定性，限制了模型在需要风险评估场景中的应用。

Method: 本文引入了“三元决策树”（Ternary Decision Trees），在每个划分节点处设置一个以最优阈值为中心、半宽为 delta 的不确定区域。当实例落入该区域时，模型通过加权融合两个子树的预测结果，并标记为“边界不确定”。文章提出了五种无需外部噪声设定的 delta 局部估算方法：质量平台法（quality-plateau）、类别重叠法（class-overlap）、增益比法（gain-ratio）、节点引导法（node-bootstrap）和边缘法（margin）。

Result: 在 OpenML-CC18 的 72 个数据集上进行验证，五种 delta 估算方法在分类准确性上均显著优于传统 CART 算法。其中，margin（边缘法）在效率和性能平衡上表现最优（在 42 个数据集上胜出），且无需额外超参数。在医疗案例中，该方法通过标记部分不确定样本，显著提升了整体分类的准确性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的三元决策树通过引入“不确定区域”机制，有效弥补了传统决策树在决策边界处硬划分的缺陷。实验证明，该方法在不增加额外超参数的情况下，显著提升了分类的准确性与鲁棒性，特别是在医疗和金融等对决策风险敏感的领域具有重要的应用价值。

Abstract: Decision trees partition the feature space using hard binary thresholds, assigning identical confidence to instances far from a decision boundary and to those directly on it. We introduce ternary decision trees, which augment each split node with an uncertainty zone of half-width delta centered on the optimal threshold. Instances in this zone receive predictions formed by weighted blending of both child subtrees and are flagged as boundary-uncertain, signaling that downstream applications may treat these predictions differently. Crucially, delta is computed locally at each node from statistics already available during standard CART split finding, requiring no external noise specification. We propose and evaluate five delta-estimation methods: quality-plateau (plateau width of the split criterion curve), class-overlap (empirical class-distribution overlap), gain-ratio (split quality relative to split entropy), node-bootstrap (threshold variance under node-level resampling), and margin (SVM-inspired distance to the nearest cross-class training example). Evaluated across 72 OpenML-CC18 datasets with 5-fold cross-validation, all five methods with probabilistic routing significantly outperform standard CART on decided accuracy (Wilcoxon signed-rank, p < 0.001). The margin method achieves the best efficiency (0.104 accuracy gain per unit of boundary-uncertain flagging rate), wins on 42 of 72 datasets, and requires zero additional hyperparameters. Analysis on three Breiman synthetic benchmarks reveals that margin is self-calibrating on clean data while node-bootstrap and quality-plateau best track theoretical irreducible error. Experiments on four medical and financial datasets demonstrate practical value: on mammography, node-bootstrap achieves +0.71% decided accuracy by flagging 10.8% of screening cases as boundary-uncertain.

### [161] [Lumberjack: Better Differentially Private Random Forests through Heavy Hitter Detection in Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22756)
*Christian Janos Lebeda,David Erb,Tudor Cebere,Aurélien Bellet*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Lumberjack 是一种新型差分隐私随机森林算法，通过构建深度更大的决策树并结合创新的分层数据隐私剪枝技术，显著提升了模型在隐私保护下的性能，达到行业领先水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的差分隐私（DP）随机森林算法在保护隐私的同时，通常会导致模型性能（实用性）大幅下降，使其难以在实际场景中应用。研究旨在解决这一隐私与实用性之间的权衡难题，提升模型在隐私约束下的表达能力。

Method: Lumberjack算法：首先构建大型随机决策树，随后利用一种创新的、针对分层数据的 (ε, δ)-差分隐私“重击手”（Heavy Hitter）检测算法，对树进行激进的隐私保护剪枝，仅保留样本量充足的节点。该检测算法在高度为 h 的树上具有 O(sqrt(log h)) 的错误率，允许构建比现有方法更深的树。

Result: 在基准数据集上的实验评估表明，Lumberjack 在实际隐私预算范围内，在隐私-实用性权衡方面表现优于现有的所有差分隐私随机森林方法，树立了该领域的新技术标杆。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过精心设计的差分隐私算法（如Lumberjack），可以在很大程度上弥合隐私保护与模型实用性之间的差距，证明了差分隐私随机森林在处理敏感表格数据方面具有广阔的应用前景。

Abstract: Random forests are widely used in fields involving sensitive tabular data, but existing approaches to enforcing differential privacy (DP) typically degrade performance to the point of impracticality. In this paper, we introduce Lumberjack, a differentially private random forest algorithm that achieves substantially higher utility by constructing large random decision trees and then applying aggressive, privacy-preserving pruning to retain only sufficiently populated nodes. A key component of our approach is a novel $(\varepsilon,δ)$-DP heavy hitter detection algorithm for hierarchical data, whose error is $O_{\varepsilon,δ}(\sqrt{\log h})$ for trees of height $h$ and may be of independent interest. This favorable scaling enables the use of significantly deeper trees than in prior work, leading to improved expressiveness under privacy constraints. Our empirical evaluation on benchmark datasets shows that Lumberjack consistently outperforms prior DP random forest methods, establishing a new state of the art. In particular, our approach yields substantial improvements in the privacy-utility trade-off for practical privacy budgets. Our findings suggest that carefully designed DP random forests can close much of the utility gap, highlighting a promising and underexplored direction for future research.

### [162] [Uniform Diffusion Models Revisited: Leave-One-Out Denoiser and Absorbing State Reformulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22765)
*Samson Gourevitch,Yazid Janati,Dario Shariatian,Umut Simsekli,Eric Moulines,Eric P. Xing,Alain Durmus*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了均匀扩散模型（UDM）中训练目标与后验预测存在的不匹配问题，通过提出“留一法”参数化、吸收态重构及改进的采样算法，有效提升了UDM在语言建模任务中的生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离散扩散模型（如掩码扩散模型MDM与均匀扩散模型UDM）在训练和反向动力学定义上存在差异，UDM的标准插件参数化与最优去噪后验之间存在不匹配，限制了模型的性能，需要从理论上厘清并改进参数化与采样策略。

Method: 1. 识别并分析了均匀扩散模型（UDM）中标准插件ELBO目标函数与交叉熵去噪目标之间的不匹配问题。
2. 提出了“留一法”（leave-one-out）后验参数化方法，用于优化预测目标。
3. 推导了去噪器、留一法后验与得分函数之间的精确转换关系，从而解耦了参数化与训练目标。
4. 引入了一种吸收态重构方法，将UDM分解为类掩码扩散的采样操作。
5. 设计了改进的预测-校正采样器及温度采样策略，无需额外训练即可提升推理性能。

Result: 实验结果显示，采用“留一法”参数化能够稳定提升UDM的生成效果；所提出的吸收态重构方法使得UDM在语言建模任务中匹配甚至超过了MDM的表现，证明了参数化与采样设计对离散扩散模型性能的关键影响。

Conclusion: 研究表明，离散扩散模型性能的差异主要源于参数化和采样设计，而非边际分布选择。通过改进参数化（如留一法）和采样机制（如预测-校正采样），可以显著提升均匀扩散模型的性能，并使其达到或超越掩码扩散模型的水平。

Abstract: Discrete diffusion models are often trained through clean-data prediction, but the prediction can be used in different ways to define the reverse dynamics. In Masked Diffusion Models (MDM) these choices largely coincide, whereas in Uniform Diffusion Models (UDM) they do not. We show that the standard plug-in bridge parameterization for UDM is not optimized by the denoising posterior, but by a leave-one-out posterior that predicts each clean token without using its own noisy observation. This identifies a mismatch between the plug-in ELBO and the usual cross-entropy denoising objective. We characterize the leave-one-out target and derive exact conversions between the denoiser, the leave-one-out posterior, and the score. These conversions allow us to disentangle parameterization and training objective. Our results also lead to inference improvements without any additional training through an informed predictor-corrector sampler and improved temperature sampling based on the leave-one-out predictor.
  We further introduce an absorbing-state reformulation of uniform diffusion that preserves the UDM joint law while decomposing it into masked-diffusion-like sampling operations, with simpler denoising posteriors, carry-over unmasking, and a natural remasking mechanism. On language modeling, leave-one-out parameterizations consistently improve UDM generation, while the absorbing construction matches or surpasses masked diffusion. These results suggest that the empirical gap between masked and uniform diffusion is driven less by the choice of marginals themselves than by parameterization and sampling design. The code and models can be found at https://github.com/samsongourevitch/rev_udm.

</details>


### [163] [Remember to be Curious: Episodic Context and Persistent Worlds for 3D Exploration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22814)
*Lily Goli,Justin Kerr,Daniele Reda,Alec Jacobson,Andrea Tagliasacchi,Angjoo Kanazawa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对复杂3D环境中好奇心驱动探索的局限性，本文提出了一种结合持久化在线3D重建与边缘序列模型的方法，有效解决了智能体因缺乏空间记忆而陷入局部循环的问题，实现了高效的自主探索与任务泛化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的好奇心驱动强化学习在复杂的真实感3D环境中表现不佳，智能体容易陷入局部循环，并因“遗忘”而重复获取内在奖励。作者旨在解决这一缺乏空间持久性和情境上下文的问题，以实现高效的自主探索。

Method: 提出了一种新的好奇心驱动强化学习框架，核心包括两部分：1. 使用在线3D重建技术构建持久的全局世界模型；2. 采用序列模型（Sequence Model）处理RGB观测，以维护边缘情境（Episodic Context）记忆。该架构使智能体能够识别新区域并避免重复访问旧状态。

Result: 在HM3D环境中的纯好奇心训练证明，该方法优于基于强化学习的主动建图基准，并在Gibson和AI生成的世界中表现出色的零样本泛化能力。此外，该策略在下游任务（如苹果采摘和图像目标导航）中展现了极高的适应效率。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了将在线3D重建作为持久世界模型，结合基于序列模型的边缘情境记忆，是解决复杂3D环境中探索难题的关键。这种方法无需外部奖励即可学习到可迁移的导航策略。

Abstract: Exploration is a prerequisite for learning useful behaviors in sparse-reward, long-horizon tasks, particularly within 3D environments. Curiosity-driven reinforcement learning addresses this via intrinsic rewards derived from the mismatch between the agent's predictive model of the world and reality. However, translating this intrinsic motivation to complex, photorealistic environments remains difficult, as agents can become trapped in local loops and receive fresh rewards for revisiting forgotten states. In this work, we demonstrate that this failure stems from a lack of spatial persistence and episodic context. We show that effective curiosity requires a model of the world that is persistent and continuously updated, paired with an agent that maintains an episodic trajectory history to navigate toward novel regions. We achieve this using an online 3D reconstruction as a persistent model of the world, while the agent policy is parameterized as a sequence model over RGB observations to maintain episodic context. This design enables effective exploration during training while allowing the agent to navigate using solely RGB frames at deployment. Trained purely via curiosity on HM3D, our agent outperforms RL-based active mapping baselines and generalizes zero-shot to Gibson and AI-generated worlds. Our end-to-end policy enables efficient adaptation to downstream tasks, such as apple picking and image-goal navigation, outperforming from-scratch baselines. Please see video results at https://recuriosity.github.io/.

</details>

### [164] [Bridging the Cold-Start Gap: LLM-Powered Synthetic Data Generation for Natural Language Search at Airbnb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21812)
*Wendy Ran Wei,Hao Li,Weiwei Guo,Xiaowei Liu,Xueyin Chen,Dillon Davis,Malay Haldar,Soumyadip Banerjee,Kedar Bellare,Huiji Gao,Stephanie Moyerman,Sanjeev Katariya*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对自然语言搜索系统的冷启动难题，本文提出了一种利用大语言模型生成高质量合成查询与标签的框架，实现了训练与评估数据的自动化，显著提升了检索模型的性能，并在Airbnb生产环境中得到了成功应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在部署自然语言搜索系统时面临严重的“冷启动”问题：缺乏真实的用户查询数据来学习语言模式，且缺乏相关性标注数据来训练排名模型。因此，需要一种能够利用大语言模型自动生成高质量合成数据的方法，以支持系统的训练与评估。

Method: 提出了一套利用大语言模型（LLM）生成合成查询与相关性标签的框架。具体包括：1. 查询生成：结合预订会话中的对比房源对与用户调研种子查询，以平衡真实性与多样性；2. 标签生成：引入“对比生成”技术（contrastive generation）构建主题相关性标签，并使用“虚拟评审员”（Virtual Judge）进行大规模标签覆盖。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在查询长度分布上取得了优异表现（KL散度仅为0.66，远优于InPars基线的12.03）；在属性分布上以0.04的KL散度优于种子查询（0.09）。此外，生成的评估样本更具挑战性（Pairwise准确率为79%），能够有效提升模型的判别能力，目前已在Airbnb生产环境中部署。

Conclusion: 本研究通过结合领域特定的种子数据与大语言模型，成功构建了一套冷启动检索系统的训练与评估框架。该方法不仅解决了数据匮乏问题，还通过提供高质量的合成数据，显著提升了检索模型的准确性与泛化能力，证明了利用LLM进行数据增强在实际工业级搜索场景中的有效性。

Abstract: Deploying natural language search systems presents a critical cold-start challenge: no real user queries to learn linguistic patterns, and no relevance labels to train ranking models. We present a framework for generating synthetic queries and labels using large language models (LLMs), powering model training and evaluation for Airbnb's natural language search.
  For query generation, we combine contrastive listing pairs from booking sessions with seed queries from user research to balance realism and diversity, enabling a cold-to-warm start transition as real user data becomes available. For label generation, we introduce contrastive generation that produces topicality labels by construction, and Virtual Judge (VJ) labeling for broader coverage.
  We compare our approach against a no-seed contrastive baseline and an InPars-style baseline. For query length, the InPars baseline produces verbose queries with KL divergence of 12.03 vs. real users; our seed-guided approach achieves 0.66, a 7.5x improvement. For attribute type distributions, our approach achieves the lowest KL divergence (0.04), outperforming even seed queries (0.09). Experiments show our approach produces harder evaluation examples than the no-seed baseline (79% vs. 97% pairwise accuracy), providing discriminative signal for model improvement. We deploy production pipelines generating synthetic examples daily for embedding-based retrieval and ranking evaluation.

### [165] [Generative Conversational Recommender System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21987)
*Sixiao Zhang,Mingrui Liu,Cheng Long*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的端到端生成式对话推荐系统，通过将商品语义 ID 化并采用结构化决策的自回归生成框架，显著提升了对话式推荐的精准度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对话式推荐系统通常将推荐与对话生成模块分离，或依赖基于检索的流水线，导致两部分难以深度集成，且难以精准建模用户意图。因此，作者旨在构建一个统一的、端到端的生成式框架，以解决上述集成度不足的问题。

Method: 提出了一种全生成式对话推荐系统，将推荐任务与对话生成统一在单一自回归框架内。核心方法包括：1. 将商品表示为离散语义ID，通过下一个标记预测联合生成商品与回复；2. 引入结构化生成范式，将对话推荐分解为“预测意图与推荐目标 -> 条件生成回复”的顺序决策过程；3. 利用约束解码技术确保商品生成的准确性。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在保持对话质量的同时，推荐性能显著提升，在 Recall@1 指标上相比强基线模型实现了高达 29% 的性能增长。

Conclusion: 通过将对话式推荐统一在一个自回归生成框架下，本研究证明了端到端建模能够显著提升推荐的准确性与对话的连贯性，为构建更智能的对话式推荐系统提供了有效的技术范式。

Abstract: Conversational recommender systems aim to provide personalized recommendations via natural language interactions. However, existing approaches either decouple recommendation from dialog generation or rely on retrieval-based pipelines, limiting the integration between recommendation and response generation and leading to suboptimal modeling of user intent. In this paper, we propose a fully generative conversational recommender system that unifies recommendation and dialog generation within a single autoregressive framework. Our approach represents items as discrete semantic IDs and integrates them directly into the generation process, enabling joint prediction of items and responses via next-token modeling. We further introduce a structured generation paradigm that factorizes conversational recommendation into a sequence of interdependent decisions, where the model first predicts the response intent and the recommendation target, and then generates the response conditioned on them. This design enables end-to-end optimization, enforces a more coherent dependency structure, and supports faithful item generation via constrained decoding. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method consistently improves recommendation performance, achieving gains of up to 29% on Recall@1 over strong baselines, while maintaining competitive dialog quality.

### [166] [Diversed Model Discovery via Structured Table Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22766)
*Zhengyuan Dong,Renée J. Miller*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为StructuredSemanticSearch的模型检索框架，通过挖掘模型卡片中的结构化表格数据而非仅依赖文本，实现了更精准、更多样化的模型对比检索，并通过新的评估协议验证了其在证据覆盖率方面的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型检索系统主要依赖文本语义相似度，导致检索结果同质化，难以满足用户对模型在特定性能指标或配置上进行差异化比较的需求。研究者认为，模型检索本质上是比较性的，需要从模型卡片中提取简洁、高质量的结构化证据。

Method: 提出了StructuredSemanticSearch框架，该框架结合了语义基线与结构感知管线。其核心包括：1. 利用联合（unionability）、可连接性（joinability）和关键词搜索等算子发现模型卡片中的结构化表格；2. 实施定向感知整合（orientation-aware integration）以处理异构表格；3. 建立基于“数据碎片”（nugget）的评估协议，以量化证据覆盖率和多样性。

Result: 在包含597个模型推荐查询的实验中，StructuredSemanticSearch展示了比纯语义基线更高的“数据碎片”（nugget）覆盖率，证明了结构感知检索能更有效地定位符合特定意图的模型。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入StructuredSemanticSearch框架，证明了在模型检索中结合结构化表格数据能够显著优于仅依赖文本语义的方法。这种基于证据的方法不仅提升了模型检索的相关性，还通过可审计的评估协议促进了模型卡片生态系统的透明度和可解释性。

Abstract: Model cards describe model behavior through a mixture of textual descriptions and structured artifacts, including performance, configuration, and dataset tables. Existing model search systems rely predominantly on semantic similarity over text, which can produce homogeneous result sets and limit exploration of alternatives. We argue that model search is inherently comparative: users want models that are task-aligned yet differentiated in measurable ways. We hypothesize that this balance requires retrieval over condensed, high-quality evidence rather than verbose descriptions, and much of that evidence is concentrated in structured tables. We present StructuredSemanticSearch, a table-driven model search framework built on the ModelTables benchmark. Given a query, StructuredSemanticSearch combines a semantic baseline for task alignment with a structure-aware pipeline that discovers query-related model-card tables using table discovery operators such as unionability, joinability, and keyword search. Retrieved tables are mapped back to model cards under a controlled top-k budget, enabling fair comparison between text-based and table-based retrieval. Beyond retrieval, StructuredSemanticSearch adapts table integration to the model-table domain through orientation-aware integration, producing compact integrated views of tables from partially overlapping and sometimes transposed evidence tables. For evaluation, we introduce a nugget-based, auditable protocol that extracts compact evidence items from model cards, matches queries to condition- or intent-specific nuggets, and measures evidence coverage and diversity over retrieved model-card candidate sets. This protocol also provides a scalable path toward approximate, evidence-based labeling in dynamic model lakes. Experiments on 597 model-recommendation queries show improved nugget coverage for the structure-aware pipeline than semantic baseline

</details>


### [167] [LLM Retrieval for Stable and Predictable Ad Recommendations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21969)
*Vinodh Kumar Sunkara,Satheeshkumar Karuppusamy,Hangjun Xu,Sai Deepika Regani,Kshitij Gupta,Gaby Nahum,Sneha Iyer,Jean-Baptiste Fiot,Yinglong Guo,Xiaowen Guo,Atul Jangra,Yucheng Liu,Jinghao Yan,Vijay Pappu,Benjamin Schulte,Deepak Chandra*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对广告推荐系统在面对素材微小扰动时表现不稳定的问题，本文提出了一种基于大语言模型的语义化候选检索框架，通过增强系统的语义感知能力，在提升推荐精准度的同时，有效改善了系统的预测稳定性与可预测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该研究证明，通过引入基于大语言模型的语义化候选生成框架，不仅能够显著提升广告推荐系统的预测稳定性与可预测性，还能在保持甚至优化传统指标（如点击率、转化率）的同时，解决广告变体引发的冷启动和分发不一致问题，为大规模推荐系统提供了一种通用的稳健性优化方案。

Abstract: Traditional ads recommendation systems have primarily focused on optimizing for prediction accuracy of click or conversion events using canonical metrics such as recall or normalized discounted cumulative gain (NDCG). With the hyper-growth of ads inventory and liquidity with generative AI technologies, the prediction stability and predictability is becoming increasingly critical. Intuitively, prediction stability and predictability can be defined to quantify system robustness with respect to minor/noisy input (ads, creatives) perturbations, the lack of which could lead to advertiser perceivable problems such as repeatability, cold start and under-exploration. In this paper, we introduce a new evaluation framework for quantifying stability and predictability of an ads recommender system, and present an online validated semantic candidate generation framework powered by fine-tuned Large Language Models (LLMs) that showed significant improvement along these metrics by fundamentally improving the semantic-awareness of the system. The approach extracts hierarchical semantic attributes from ad creatives to obtain LLM representations, which serve as the foundation for graph-based expansion, ensuring the retrieved candidates encapsulate semantic variants of an ad, guaranteeing that small creative variants from the advertiser yield consistent and explainable delivery results to the user. We tested this LLM ads retrieval framework in a large-scale industrial ads recommendation system, demonstrating significant improvements across offline and online A/B experiments, showcasing gains in both predictability and traditional performance metrics. Although evaluated in the ads stack, this is a general framework that can be applied broadly to any large-scale recommendation and retrieval systems facing similar scaling and predictability challenges.

### [168] [Benchmarking and Improving Monitors for Out-Of-Distribution Alignment Failure in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21602)
*Dylan Feng,Pragya Srivastava,Cassidy Laidlaw*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对大模型在分布外（OOD）场景下的安全失效问题，本文提出了MOOD基准，并证明了通过将OOD检测器与防护模型结合，能够以极小的计算成本显著提升模型对未知安全问题的识别召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大模型在面对超出训练分布（OOD）的提示词或异常响应时，往往会出现安全对齐失效。现有的安全防护手段通常难以泛化到这些未知场景，因此需要研究如何有效监测并识别这些未预见的对齐失败。

Method: 作者提出了名为MOOD（Misalignment Out Of Distribution）的基准测试，通过限制训练数据集来模拟真实场景下的OOD偏差。研究对比了四种不同类型的OOD检测器，并提出了一种将安全防护模型与基于马氏距离（Mahalanobis distance）及困惑度（Perplexity）的OOD检测器结合的监控方案。

Result: 实验结果表明，单一的防护模型在处理OOD问题时泛化能力较差。引入OOD检测器后，安全失效的召回率从39%提升至45%。此外，研究发现结合OOD检测器的监控方案在扩展性上表现优异，其性能增益甚至超过了增加20倍模型参数的单纯防护模型。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在大型语言模型（LLM）的监控体系中，将专门的分布外（OOD）检测器与现有的安全防护模型（Guard Models）相结合，是提升模型对未知偏差和安全失效检测能力的有效途径。研究强调了OOD检测应作为LLM安全防护的核心组成部分。

Abstract: Many safety and alignment failures of large language models (LLMs) occur due to out-of-distribution (OOD) situations: unusual prompt or response patterns that are unforeseen by model developers. We systematically study whether LLM monitoring pipelines can detect these OOD alignment failures by introducing a benchmark called Misalignment Out Of Distribution (MOOD). It is difficult to find failures that are truly OOD for off-the-shelf models trained on vast safety datasets. We sidestep this by including a restricted training set in MOOD that we use to train our own monitors, as well as seven test sets with diverse alignment failures that are outside the training distribution. Using MOOD, we find that guard models (safety classifiers) often fail to generalize OOD. To fix this, we propose combining guard models with OOD detectors. We test four types of OOD detectors and find that a combination of a guard model with Mahalanobis distance and perplexity-based OOD detectors can improve recall from 39% to 45%. We also establish positive scaling trends across model scales for monitors that combine a guard model and OOD detector; we find that incorporating OOD detection into monitoring achieves a higher recall gain than using a guard model with 20 times more parameters. Our work suggests that OOD detection should be a crucial component of LLM monitoring and provides a foundation for further work on this important problem.

</details>


### [169] [The Shape of Testimony: A Scalable Framework for Oral History Archive Comparison](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21623)
*Itamar Trainin,Renana Keydar,Amit Pinchevski*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过计算手段分析了1600多份大屠杀幸存者证词，验证并修正了学术界关于两个主要档案库在访谈风格上存在简单二分法的传统认识，并建立了一套新的数字口述历史分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大屠杀研究中长期存在一种观点，认为南加州大学大屠杀基金会（USC Shoah Foundation）的访谈倾向于结构化引导，而耶鲁大学福图诺夫视频档案（Yale Fortunoff Video Archive）倾向于自由叙事。本研究旨在通过实证数据验证这一区分，并探索这一分类的准确性。

Method: 研究人员对来自两个档案库的1600多份口述证词进行了大规模计算分析。具体方法包括：语篇分割（Discourse segmentation）、主题建模（Topic modeling）以及基于大语言模型（LLM）的分析，旨在量化证词的“结构化”水平，包括评估主题连贯性、访谈者与幸存者的互动动力学以及问题类型的分布。

Result: 结果总体上证实了早前研究中指出的结构性差异，但同时也发现这两个档案库在个别访谈和叙事模式上存在显著的重合与共性，挑战了二者截然对立的定论。

Conclusion: 本研究通过计算分析证实了两个档案库在访谈结构上存在差异，但同时也揭示了它们之间的大量重合与复杂交互，从而反驳了以往简单的“结构化 vs 自由叙事”二分法。此外，该研究提供了一套可扩展且可复制的数字口述历史分析框架。

Abstract: Researchers in Holocaust studies have often distinguished between two styles of oral survivor testimony: the USC Shoah Foundation's interviews tend to follow a structured, interviewer-guided format, whereas the Yale Fortunoff Video Archive generally favors a more free-form, open-ended style. This distinction has influenced both scholarly research and the development of later archives. In this study, we critically examine that claim by conducting a large-scale computational analysis of more than 1,600 testimonies from both collections. Leveraging discourse segmentation, topic modeling, and large language model (LLM) based analysis, we quantify the "structuredness" level of testimonies through topic coherence, interviewer-survivor dynamics, and the distribution of question types. Our results generally corroborate the structural differences identified in earlier research, while also revealing significant overlaps between the collections, both within individual interviews and across common narrative patterns. This complicates the simple "structured vs. free-form" dichotomy often applied to these oral histories. Beyond revisiting a foundational claim in Holocaust studies, our work provides a scalable, replicable framework for comparative corpus analysis. As a proof of concept, it suggests broader applications for digital oral history, narrative analysis, and the design of citizen-science annotation platforms.

</details>


### [170] [MindLoom: Composing Thought Modes for Frontier-Level Reasoning Data Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21630)
*Haiyang Shen,Taian Guo,Xuanzhong Chen,Mugeng Liu,Weichen Bi,Wenchun Jing,Sixiong Xie,Zhuofan Shi,Yudong Han,Chongyang Pan,Siqi Zhong,Jinsheng Huang,Ming Zhang,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MindLoom通过将推理逻辑分解为“思维模式”并进行组合式合成，有效解决了大语言模型推理数据生成中难度不可控和多样性不足的问题，显著提升了模型在STEM领域的推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型推理数据合成方法缺乏对任务结构和难度的系统性把控，导致生成数据的多样性不足且难度难以稳定控制。研究者旨在通过拆解推理逻辑来解决这些局限。

Method: 1. 思维模式解构：将复杂推理任务分解为原子级的知识-推理转换，称为“思维模式”。2. 检索模型训练：训练模型以根据当前问题状态匹配合适的思维模式。3. 组合式生成：基于种子问题，迭代应用思维模式构建新任务。4. 分布对齐采样：确保生成数据的多样性覆盖。5. 滚出（rollout）评估与筛选：通过多轮模拟推理验证生成问题的难度并生成标准答案，用于监督微调。

Result: 在涵盖5个STEM学科和4个数学推理任务的9个基准测试中，基于MindLoom生成数据微调的模型表现优于基准模型、蒸馏方法及外部数据基准；消融实验证实了各组件的有效性，并证明了该框架在保持难度可控的同时，具备广泛的推理模式覆盖能力。

Conclusion: MindLoom通过将推理过程解构为“思维模式”（thought modes），成功实现了对推理任务难度的系统性控制和多样化生成。该方法验证了组合式推理工程在提升大语言模型STEM和数学推理能力方面的有效性，为高质量推理数据的自动合成提供了稳健的框架。

Abstract: Although LLMs have made substantial progress in reasoning, systematically producing frontier-level reasoning data remains difficult. Existing synthesis methods often have limited visibility into the structural factors that govern problem difficulty, which can result in narrow diversity and unstable difficulty control. In this work, we view the difficulty of a reasoning problem as arising from the accumulation of atomic knowledge-reasoning transformations, which we term thought modes. Building on this perspective, we propose MindLoom, a framework for synthesizing frontier-level reasoning data through compositional thought mode engineering. Given a collection of hard problems with verified solutions, MindLoom first decomposes those solutions into thought mode chains that reveal each problem's construction logic. It then trains a retrieval model that matches problem states to compatible thought modes, providing guidance on which reasoning challenges to introduce during synthesis. New problems are composed by iteratively applying retrieved thought modes to seed questions, with distribution-aligned sampling to encourage diverse reasoning coverage. Finally, a rollout-based judging stage labels generated questions by difficulty and supplies judged-correct responses for supervised fine-tuning. We evaluate MindLoom on nine benchmarks covering five STEM disciplines and four mathematical reasoning tasks across multiple model families and sizes. Models fine-tuned on MindLoom-generated data achieves favorable performances over base models, distillation, and external-data baselines across the reported benchmarks. Ablation studies indicate the contribution of each component, and further analysis suggests that MindLoom covers a broad range of reasoning patterns while maintaining useful difficulty control. We have open-sourced our implementation at https://github.com/EachSheep/MindLoom.

</details>


### [171] [Search-E1: Self-Distillation Drives Self-Evolution in Search-Augmented Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22511)
*Zihan Liang,Yufei Ma,Ben Chen,Zhipeng Qian,Xuxin Zhang,Huangyu Dai,Lingtao Mao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为Search-E1的简洁自我演化方法，证明了通过简单的GRPO与离线自我蒸馏相结合，无需复杂的辅助模块即可训练出高性能的搜索增强推理智能体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主流的搜索增强推理智能体研究倾向于引入复杂的辅助机制（如外部监督、过程奖励模型、树搜索、多阶段课程学习等），这不仅导致训练流程臃肿，还增加了对特定资源和设计的依赖。作者旨在探究这些复杂机制是否必要，并寻求一种更简洁、高效的优化路径。

Method: 提出了Search-E1方法，该方法通过GRPO（组相对策略优化）与离线自我蒸馏（OFSD）交替进行。在每一轮GRPO后，策略模型在自身问题集上进行推理，并通过基于token层面的前向KL散度目标函数，将推理时的分布与在该 privileged 上下文（利用更高效的兄弟路径）下的分布进行对齐，从而实现密集的逐步监督。

Result: Search-E1在七个问答基准测试中，使用Qwen2.5-3B模型达到了0.440的平均准确率（EM），超越了所有同等规模及更大规模的开源基线模型。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，在搜索增强推理智能体的训练中，复杂的辅助机制并非必要。通过简单的自我演化方法（Search-E1），仅利用基础的GRPO和离线自我蒸馏（OFSD），即可实现与复杂方法相当甚至更优的性能，从而简化了训练流程并提高了可扩展性。

Abstract: Post-training has become the dominant recipe for turning a language model into a competent search-augmented reasoning agent. A line of recent work pushes its performance further by adding elaborate machinery on top of this standard pipeline. These augmentations import external supervision from stronger external systems, attach auxiliary modules such as process reward models or retrospective critics, restructure the rollout itself with tree search or multi-stage curricula, or shape the reward with hand-crafted bonuses and penalties. Each addition delivers a measurable gain, but each also inflates the training pipeline and ties the recipe to resources or designs that may not always be available. We take a step back and ask whether any of this machinery is actually necessary, and propose Search-E1, a self-evolution method that lets a search-augmented agent improve through only vanilla GRPO interleaved with offline self-distillation (OFSD). After each GRPO round, the policy rolls out on its own training questions. A token-level forward KL objective then aligns the policy's inference-time distribution to its own distribution under a privileged context that exposes a more efficient sibling trajectory. Despite this simplicity, the procedure naturally provides dense per-step supervision. On seven QA benchmarks, Search-E1 reaches $0.440$ average EM with Qwen2.5-3B, surpassing all open-source baselines at both scales. Code and complete version will be made public soon.

</details>


### [172] [The Impact of AI Usage and Informativeness on Skill Development in Logical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21695)
*Shang Wu,Hongyu Yao,Catarina Belem,Shuyuan Fu,Mark Steyvers,Padhraic Smyth*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了 AI 辅助对人类技能学习的影响：过度依赖 AI 会削弱技能习得，而 AI 提供的信息质量决定了它是促进还是阻碍学习；研究建议通过规范 AI 使用来平衡即时绩效与长期技能培养。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管人工智能在人类解决问题中的应用日益广泛，但它对个人技能习得的具体影响尚不明确。本研究旨在探讨 AI 的使用频率和 AI 提供的信息量如何影响学习过程。

Method: 研究人员通过一项受控的逻辑推理任务进行实验，观察受试者在有需求时使用 AI 辅助的情况，并分析 AI 使用频率及 AI 的信息量（informativeness）对受试者技能发展的影响。通过对比实验组（使用 AI）与对照组（不使用或轻度使用 AI）的表现，评估短期绩效及移除 AI 后的持续表现。

Result: 研究发现：1. 频繁使用 AI 与较弱的技能习得相关，重度 AI 用户表现不如同等水平的轻度用户；2. AI 的“信息量”起关键中介作用，低信息量 AI 既无法提升即时绩效，也无法在撤去辅助后维持表现，反而阻碍学习；3. 高信息量 AI 可在不显著降低撤离 AI 后表现的情况下提升短期绩效，但存在个体差异。

Conclusion: AI 对人类技能发展的影响取决于 AI 的使用方式和信息量。AI 既可能通过增强独立思考来补充技能，也可能因作为替代品而削弱技能。因此，在 AI 辅助环境下，对 AI 的访问和使用进行调节对于促进技能习得至关重要。

Abstract: Artificial intelligence (AI) is being increasingly integrated into human problem-solving, yet its effects on individual skill development remain unclear. We examine how both AI usage and informativeness can shape learning in the context of a controlled logical reasoning task with on-demand access to AI assistance. We find that greater AI usage is associated with weaker skill development: heavy AI users underperform relative to comparable peers, whereas light AI users perform similarly to matched users who do not use AI. We also find in our study that these patterns are mediated by AI informativeness. Low-information AI neither improves immediate performance nor preserves performance after AI assistance is removed, and is linked to weaker learning overall. On the other hand, high-information AI was found to improve short-run performance without reducing post-AI outcomes on average in our experiments, but with heterogeneous effects. Our findings in general suggest that AI can, depending on context, either complement human skill development by amplifying independent reasoning or can act as a substitute that undermines such reasoning, with the implication that regulating AI access and usage will be important for promoting skill development in the presence of AI assistance.

</details>


### [173] [Latent-space Attacks for Refusal Evasion in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21706)
*Giorgio Piras,Raffaele Mura,Fabio Brau,Maura Pintor,Luca Oneto,Fabio Roli,Battista Biggio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文将拒绝抑制重新诠释为一种针对线性探测器的潜在空间规避攻击，提出了一种通过强制将模型状态推入“合规区域”的受控攻击方法，在多种主流模型上实现了比现有技术更强大的攻击效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的安全性对齐模型虽然能拒绝有害请求，但其拒绝行为可以通过操纵内部表示来被抑制。以往的研究虽然通过消融“拒绝方向”取得了实效，但缺乏对潜在空间变换背后的数学原理及有效机制的理论解释，且其抑制效果存在局限。

Method: 本文将拒绝抑制视为一种针对线性探测器的潜在空间规避攻击。作者分析了以往基于差分均值的消融方法本质上是向决策边界的投影。在此基础上，提出了一种受控潜在空间规避（Controlled Latent-space Evasion, CLE）攻击，通过将模型表示以优化后的置信度进一步推入“合规”区域，从而更有效地绕过安全防御。

Result: 实验证明，CLE 攻击在 15 种涵盖指令微调、多模态及推理的模型上均达到了最先进的攻击成功率，显著优于现有的拒绝消融基准方法和专门的越狱攻击手段。

Conclusion: 本文通过将拒绝抑制重构为潜在空间规避攻击，成功解释了现有消融方法的机制及其局限性。所提出的受控潜在空间规避攻击（CLE）通过将模型表示推向决策边界之外，在多种模型上实现了最优的攻击成功率，证明了这一视角在分析和绕过语言模型安全性方面的有效性。

Abstract: Safety-aligned language models are trained to refuse harmful requests, yet refusal behavior can be suppressed by steering their internal representations. Existing methods do so by ablating a refusal direction from model activations, aiming to remove refusal from the model's residual stream. Despite their empirical success, these methods lack a principled account of the latent-space transformation they induce and why it suppresses refusal. In this work, we recast refusal suppression as a latent-space evasion attack against linear probes trained to separate refused from answered prompts. Under this view, prior work's difference-in-means direction naturally defines such a probe, and its ablation is exactly a projection onto its decision boundary, i.e., a minimum-confidence evasion attack. This perspective not only explains the empirical success of prior work but also admits a key limitation: evasion stops at the decision boundary, motivating the need to push representations further into the compliant region, i.e., where the model answers. We leverage this by proposing a Controlled Latent-space Evasion attack that projects representations past the boundary with an optimized confidence. We achieve state-of-the-art attack success rate across 15 instruction-tuned, multimodal, and reasoning models, outperforming existing refusal-ablation baselines and specialized jailbreak attacks.

</details>


### [174] [AttuneBench: A Conversation-Based Benchmark for LLM Emotional Intelligence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21739)
*Kate M. Lubrano,Faisal Sayed,Ankita Rathod,Akshansh,Craver Corbyn Thomas-Smith,Mark E. Whiting,Karina Nguyen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 AttuneBench，这是首个基于 200 场真实多轮人机对话的基准测试，用于评估大模型在动态交互中的情商表现，研究发现情商由多个可拆解的能力组成，且单一的聚合指标无法全面反映模型处理情感对话的真实水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的情商评估基准多依赖合成提示词或单轮对话，难以真实反映大模型在实际多轮交互中感知、理解并响应人类情感状态的能力，缺乏对动态对话情境的考察。

Method: 构建了名为 AttuneBench 的基准测试集，包含 200 场真实的、带有人类用户逐轮标注（情感状态、模型行为、偏好响应）的多轮人机对话数据，并对 11 个主流大语言模型在情感识别、行为分类、偏好预测和响应质量四个维度进行了评估。

Result: 研究发现 11 个模型在情商各子任务上的排名缺乏相关性，证明情商由多个独立能力构成。此外，在偏好对齐和响应质量评估上，模型间的表现差距显著大于情感标签识别任务，说明模型在识别情感与满足用户情感诉求之间存在鸿沟。

Conclusion: 情商行为包含多个可分离的能力维度，且模型在这些维度上的表现并不一致。该研究强调，在多轮对话中预测用户特定的情感需求比单纯的情感标签分类更能体现真正的情商。AttuneBench 为评估和诊断大模型在情感对话中的能力提供了更为细致的框架。

Abstract: Emotional intelligence (EI), the ability to perceive, understand, and respond appropriately to others' emotional states, is central to human communication, and increasingly important to assess as LLMs assume conversational roles in everyday life. Existing EI benchmarks rely on synthetic prompts, single-turn cases, or third-party annotation. These approaches do not directly measure how models infer and respond to a participant's emotional state over the course of a real conversation. We introduce AttuneBench, a benchmark grounded in 200 genuine multi-turn human-model conversations in which participants conversed with anonymized LLMs and provided turn-by-turn annotations of their emotional state, the model's behavior, and their preferred responses. Across 11 evaluated models, we find that model rankings on emotion recognition, behavioral classification, preference prediction, and judged response quality are largely independent, indicating that emotionally intelligent behavior decomposes into separable capabilities. Preference alignment and response-quality judgments are substantially more model-discriminating than emotion-label accuracy. These results indicate that emotionally intelligent behavior requires predicting what kind of response a specific user wants in context, a distinction that aggregate scoring can obscure and that single-turn or synthetic formats cannot directly capture across turns. AttuneBench provides a framework for assessing each of these capabilities and for diagnosing model-specific strengths and failure modes in emotionally salient conversation.

### [175] [Who Uses AI? Platforms, Workforce, and AI Exposure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21743)
*Michelle Yin,Burhan Ogut*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文指出，利用AI对话日志评估职业暴露存在“样本偏差”，其结果更多反映了平台用户构成而非劳动力市场本身。修正该测量偏差后，现有关于AI对就业影响的估计值大幅衰减，且方向性存在争议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的研究倾向于利用AI平台（如ChatGPT）的对话日志来评估各职业受AI技术影响的程度，但作者怀疑这些分数反映的是平台用户群体的特征，而非真实劳动力市场的分布，导致测量结果不可靠。

Method: 通过固定结果变量、样本、控制变量和估计器，仅改变AI平台输入数据，对比不同平台下的职业暴露评分差异；通过重加权（reweighting）方法将平台用户基础调整为美国劳工统计局（BLS）的劳动力份额；形式化描述非经典测量误差，推导就业弹性的概率极限与部分识别界限。

Result: 研究发现，更换平台输入会导致就业系数发生1.9倍的变化，且不同渠道（消费者端对比企业端）的估计值符号甚至相反；通过劳动力份额加权后，估计值减小了42%至93%；现有研究方法在低估了替代效应的同时，也未能准确评估增强效应。

Conclusion: 使用AI平台对话日志来衡量职业对AI的暴露程度存在严重的测量误差，且往往受到平台用户基础特征的干扰。若不进行人口统计学加权校准，研究结论将存在显著偏差，无法准确反映AI对劳动力市场的真实替代或增强效应。

Abstract: A growing literature uses artificial intelligence platform conversation logs to measure occupation exposure. We show that these scores partly measure platform user base rather than the workforce. Holding outcome, sample, controls, and estimator fixed while varying only the platform input changes the post-ChatGPT employment coefficient by a factor of 1.9, and within-vendor consumer-versus-enterprise channels produce estimates that disagree in sign. Reweighting to Bureau of Labor Statistics workforce shares attenuates estimates by 42 to 93 percent. We formalize the non-classical measurement error, derive probability limits and partial-identification bounds for employment elasticities. The bias understates substitution more than augmentation.

### [176] [A Causal Argumentation Method for Explainability of Machine Learning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21758)
*Henry Salgado,Meagan R. Kendall,Martine Ceberio*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合因果发现与双极论证框架（BAF）的创新XAI方法，通过对模型预测过程中的因果逻辑进行显式建模，有效地解释了模型做出特定决策的底层逻辑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的可解释AI（XAI）方法多局限于识别与预测相关的特征（Feature Relevance），缺乏对“为什么”做出特定决策的因果逻辑解释。为了弥补这一短板，研究者试图通过引入因果关系和论证推理来提升AI决策的可理解性。

Method: 本文提出了一种融合因果分析与双极论证框架（BAF）的解释方法：首先通过因果发现算法梳理变量间的因果关系，随后将其转化为双极论证框架以表示特征间的支持与冲突关系，最后利用半稳定语义（semi-stable semantics）提取论证扩展，从而解释预测背后的逻辑机制。

Result: 通过在两个基准数据集上的实验，结果表明该方法能成功提取出揭示预测原因的特征组合，且在提供决策逻辑解释方面优于传统的后置可解释性（post-hoc）方法。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了结合因果关系与论证推理的框架能为XAI提供更具解释力和逻辑性的决策依据，超越了传统仅关注特征相关性的方法，为理解黑盒模型行为提供了有效的理论与实践工具。

Abstract: Explainable AI (XAI) methods identify which features are relevant to a model's predictions but often fail to clarify why certain decisions are made. In this work, we present a novel method that integrates causality with argument-based reasoning to explain why models may be making predictions. Our approach first identifies causal relationships among variables using causal discovery methods and then translates these into a Bipolar Argumentation Framework (BAF) to represent supportive and opposing interactions among features. By using semi-stable semantics, we find extensions of features that explain why certain outcomes may have been chosen. We demonstrate our method on two benchmark datasets and compare its results against standard post-hoc explainability approaches.

### [177] [What Counts as AI Sycophancy? A Taxonomy and Expert Survey of a Fragmented Construct](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21778)
*Meryl Ye,Lujain Ibrahim,Jessica Y. Bo,Myra Cheng,Ida Mattsson,Daniel Vennemeyer,Robert Kraut,Steve Rathje*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对 AI 谄媚（sycophancy）定义模糊的问题，通过文献综述构建了分类体系，并调研了专家意见，指出 AI 谄媚是一类复杂的行为集合，需要更精细化的评估与应对策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前学术界和工业界对“AI 谄媚”缺乏统一且一致的定义，导致不同研究间难以比较评估结果、缓解策略难以迁移，且系统往往在防御某种谄媚的同时仍表现出其他形式的谄媚。为此，需要建立一个明确的定义框架。

Method: 1. 文献综述：系统梳理了 70 篇关于 AI 谄媚的研究论文，构建了一个多维度的分类体系（按目标对象分为观点/信念与个人特质/情绪；按表现形式分为显性直接语言与隐性微妙行为）。2. 专家调查：对 106 名相关领域的专家进行了问卷调查，探讨其对 AI 谄媚定义的共识程度及对相关行为的界定。

Result: 1. 研究发现现有的学术研究主要集中在针对用户信念的显性谄媚，而对针对个人特质以及更微妙的谄媚行为研究不足。2. 专家调查显示，尽管 94.3% 的专家认同 AI 谄媚是一个重大问题，但对于哪些具体行为属于“谄媚”存在显著分歧。

Conclusion: AI 谄媚（sycophancy）是一个涵盖多种行为的复杂概念，当前研究缺乏统一的定义与度量标准。本文提出的分类体系为学术界、工业界和政策制定者提供了一个共享的词汇表，有助于未来更精准地识别、研究和缓解各类 AI 谄媚行为。

Abstract: AI sycophancy has become a prominent concern in large language model (LLM) research. Yet the term lacks a consistent definition and has been applied to behaviors ranging from agreeing with a user's false claim to excessively praising the user to withholding corrective feedback. When researchers, companies, and policymakers use the same term to describe different behaviors, evaluation results become difficult to compare, mitigation strategies fail to transfer, and systems that are resistant to one form of sycophancy continue exhibiting other forms. To address this, we make two contributions. First, we reviewed 70 papers on AI sycophancy to develop a taxonomy of how the behavior has been defined and measured. The taxonomy distinguishes (1) whether a model is sycophantic toward a user's positions and beliefs, or toward the user's broader personal traits and emotions, and (2) whether this occurs through explicit, direct language or more implicit, subtle behaviors such as framing, omission, or tone. Mapping existing literature to our taxonomy reveals that current research has focused on overt forms of sycophancy toward users' beliefs, leaving more subtle and person-directed behaviors relatively understudied. Second, we surveyed 106 experts in AI sycophancy and related fields to examine whether researchers agree on which model behaviors are sycophantic. While experts are nearly unanimous in believing that sycophancy is a significant problem in current AI systems (94.3% agree), they disagree substantially on which specific behaviors qualify. Together, these findings demonstrate that AI sycophancy is a broad family of behaviors with different measurement challenges, intervention requirements, and governance implications. Our taxonomy provides a shared vocabulary for understanding and addressing these behaviors.

</details>


### [178] [Implicit Safety Alignment from Crowd Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21822)
*Qian Lin,Daniel S. Brown*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种从众包偏好中提取共享安全准则并迁移至下游任务的分层强化学习框架，无需显式安全奖励即可实现安全与性能的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的RLHF方法在利用人群偏好进行安全约束方面存在局限性（如直接组合奖励函数效果不佳）。研究旨在从不同用户可能具有不同目标但遵循共同安全原则的偏好数据集中，发现并提取这些共享的安全准则，从而引导强化学习智能体在下游任务中实现安全行为。

Method: 提出了一种基于“安全人群偏好”的强化学习（Safe Crowd Preference-based RL）分层框架：首先通过人群偏好数据学习并提取出符合安全要求的技能（skills），随后利用高层策略（high-level policy）对这些技能进行组合，以在实现下游任务目标的同时满足安全约束。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在多个安全强化学习环境以及类LLM任务中，能够有效规避风险，显著降低安全成本，同时在任务性能上达到了与拥有显式安全奖励信号的基准方法相当的水平。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的分层框架成功实现了从多样化人群偏好中提取通用安全准则，并将其有效迁移至下游任务。该方法在无需显式安全奖励的情况下，既能显著降低安全违规成本，又能保持与基于真实安全信号的预言机（oracle）方法相当的性能。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) can reveal implicit objectives such as safety considerations that go beyond task completion. In this work, we focus on the common safety criteria embedded in crowd preference datasets, where different users may express distinct preferences or objectives, yet follow similar safety principles. Our aim is to discover shared safety criteria from crowd preferences and then transfer them to downstream RL tasks to regularize agent behavior and enforce safety. We first show that direct reward combination-optimizing a preference-learned reward model together with downstream task rewards-has inherent limitations. Motivated by this, we propose Safe Crowd Preference-based RL, a hierarchical framework that extracts safety-aligned skills from crowd preferences and composes them via a high-level policy to safely solve downstream tasks. Experiments across safe RL environments and a preliminary LLM-style task with diverse user goals and shared safety constraints demonstrate that our approach substantially lowers safety costs without access to explicit safety rewards, while achieving task performance comparable to oracle methods trained with ground-truth safety signals.

### [179] [FLUID: From Ephemeral IDs to Multimodal Semantic Codes for Industrial-Scale Livestreaming Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21832)
*Xinhang Yuan,Zexi Huang,Anjia Cao,Xudong Lu,Zikai Wang,Penghao Zhou,Chang Liu,Wentao Guo,Qinglei Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对直播场景下物品ID冷启动严重的问题，本文提出了FLUID框架，通过跨模态预训练的层级离散码（LUCID）替代传统ID，在工业级推荐系统中实现了无需候选侧ID的排序，显著提升了冷启动内容的推荐效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在直播推荐场景中，直播间生命周期极短（通常仅几十分钟），导致传统的ID-based协同过滤方法无法积累足够的交互数据，使得物品ID长期处于冷启动状态，严重限制了排序模型的泛化能力。因此，研究人员寻求一种摆脱物品ID依赖的推荐范式。

Method: 1. 提出了LUCID框架：通过跨领域多模态编码器（联合训练短视频和直播数据），将物品映射为离散的层级编码；2. 采用ID-free架构：在后端排序模型中彻底移除候选侧物品ID，改为将片级（slice-level）和房间级（room-level）的LUCID作为独立Token注入；3. 优化训练策略：通过分阶段预热（staged warmup）结合在线增量训练，确保系统的稳定性与持续学习能力。

Result: 在覆盖全球超过十亿用户的工业级直播推荐系统中部署后，FLUID带来了显著的线上指标提升：优质观看时长（Quality Watch Duration）增加+0.55%，冷启动直播间播放量（Cold-Start Room Views）提升+2.05%，活跃时长（Active Hours）增加+0.05%。

Conclusion: FLUID框架成功证明了在生产级直播推荐系统中，完全摒弃物品ID（ID-free）是可行的且有效的。通过使用跨模态编码器生成的层级离散码（LUCID）替代传统的ID嵌入，FLUID有效解决了直播间生命周期短导致的冷启动和泛化难题，为超大规模推荐系统提供了一种新的架构范式。

Abstract: Modern recommender systems rely heavily on ID-based collaborative filtering: each item is represented by a unique ID embedding that accumulates collaborative signals from user interactions. Livestreaming recommendation, however, faces a unique challenge in this paradigm: a live room typically broadcasts for only tens of minutes, so its item ID remains poorly learned in a persistent cold-start state and ID-centric ranking models fail to generalize. We present FLUID, the first framework to fully retire the candidate-side item ID from a production-scale livestreaming ranker. FLUID couples a cross-domain multimodal encoder, jointly trained on short videos and livestreams to produce discrete hierarchical codes (LUCID), with a late-fusion, ID-free design that injects slice-level and room-level LUCID as independent tokens, stabilized by a staged warmup under online incremental training. Deployed on our industrial livestreaming recommenders with a cross-platform combined user base of over one billion globally, FLUID delivers significant online gains of +0.55% Quality Watch Duration, +2.05% Cold-Start Room Views, and +0.05% Active Hours.

Result: 研究表明，将LLM从“执行规划”的角色转向“生成符号求解器”的角色，能够显著降低系统对模型推理的依赖，同时增强求解过程的可验证性和效率。论文明确了当前规划生成方法在泛化能力和可靠性上的瓶颈。

Conclusion: 本文指出，LLM在规划领域的应用正经历范式转移：从直接推理转向生成可验证的符号求解器。这不仅提高了规划的可靠性和资源效率，也为开发可维护、低推理成本的智能体规划系统指明了方向。未来研究应聚焦于提升规划生成器的稳健性与通用性。

Abstract: Growing attention to intelligent agents has put a spotlight on one of their central capabilities: planning. Early attempts to leverage large language models (LLMs) for planning relied on single-shot plan generation, followed by hybrid approaches that coupled LLMs with limited external search. These methods, unsound and incomplete by their very nature, often require substantial resources without yielding better solutions on unseen problems. As the limitations of LLMs become clearer, recent work has shifted toward using them at solution construction time -- generating symbolic solvers for a family of problems that can be verified and then used efficiently at inference time. This trend reflects the growing need for agents that are both reliable and resource-efficient. It also offers a path towards generating maintainable planners with minimal dependence on language models at inference time. In this paper, we argue that this shift reflects a broader realignment of the planning field in the LLM era. We examine three major categories of planner-generation methods, discuss their current limitations, and outline research steps towards a more reliable and efficient LLM-based generation of planners.

### [181] [Format-Constraint Coupling in Knowledge Graph Construction from Statistical Tables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21974)
*Jingxuan Qi,Zhiqiang Ye,Yuxiang Feng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了在大规模处理统计性CSV数据时，序列化格式与架构约束的耦合会导致知识图谱构建出现“灾难性错配”和保真度下降，并提出了通过直接图访问进行质量评估的方案及配套基准测试。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的知识图谱抽取模式在应用于统计性CSV文件（如国家-年份时间序列矩阵）时，往往会降低知识图谱的保真度。研究旨在量化分析序列化格式与架构约束之间的交互影响，并揭示这种影响对知识图谱覆盖率的负面后果。

Method: 该研究通过2x2析因设计分析了6个数据集，考察序列化格式与架构约束的交互作用。通过探针实验和Token消融实验分析了表层形式锚定机制，并在不同的GraphRAG主机和LLM家族上进行了验证。同时，对比了三种标准检索模式与直接图访问在评估构建质量时的有效性。

Result: 研究发现格式与约束的联合效应显著超过独立效应之和，且在不匹配的格式下会导致“灾难性错配”，使事实覆盖率下降。实验表明，传统检索模式掩盖了构建质量的缺陷（差异仅为1pp），而直接访问图结构可暴露高达47.6pp的质量差距。此外，作者发布了包含15个数据集和1892个金标准事实的CSVFidelity-Bench。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了在处理统计性CSV数据时，数据格式与架构约束之间存在“格式-约束耦合”现象，这种耦合会严重损害知识图谱的保真度。因此，评估知识图谱构建质量时，应直接访问图结构，而非依赖传统的检索模式。此外，研究发布的CSVFidelity-Bench为未来的保真度感知评估提供了必要的基准工具。

Abstract: An extraction schema should not reduce knowledge graph fidelity. On statistical CSV, however, it can. We study country-by-year time-series matrices, a common layout on open-data portals. In this setting, serialization format and schema constraints interact super-additively. Their joint effect exceeds the sum of independent effects by up to +1.180 (2x2 factorial, 6 datasets). Bootstrap 95% CIs are strictly positive on 4/6 datasets, with strongest evidence on wide Type-II matrices. More critically, a schema applied to a mismatched format can trigger catastrophic mismatch. Fact coverage falls below the unconstrained baseline on 4/6 datasets through entity inflation or extraction refusal. We call this observed pattern format-constraint coupling. Probing and token ablation support a surface-form anchoring explanation centred on column-name references. Controlled variants across format-schema pairings, GraphRAG hosts, and LLM families show the same direction within the measured scope; one LLM family shows only partial activation. The observation also has a diagnostic consequence. Three standard retrieval modes largely mask construction quality (delta <= 1pp), whereas direct graph access exposes gaps up to +47.6pp (p < 0.0001). To support fidelity-aware evaluation, we release CSVFidelity-Bench. It contains 15 datasets, 11 Type-II matrices, 4 Type-III tables, and 1,892 Gold Standard facts across 6 domains.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 受OSCE（客观结构化临床考试）启发，构建了一个模拟标准化患者的交互式诊断基准。该评估协议涵盖了468个病例，对15种大语言模型进行了测试，对比了模型在“全量信息给定”与“多轮主动询问诊断”两种情境下的表现差异。

Result: 研究发现，在多轮主动诊断情境下，模型的诊断准确率较静态全量评估下降了12.75%，证据支持质量下降了24.36%。错误分析表明，模型表现下降的主要原因是过早做出诊断结论（过早闭合）以及提问效率低下。

Conclusion: 现有的基于静态全量信息的医疗评估基准往往会高估大模型在临床诊断中的真实表现。为了实现更安全、更可靠的临床决策支持，必须将交互式评估作为现有静态评估的必要补充。

Abstract: Large language models perform well on static medical examinations, yet clinical diagnosis often requires iterative evidence gathering under uncertainty. Building on prior interactive evaluation efforts, we introduce an OSCE-inspired standardized patient simulator and a controlled, reproducible benchmark for active diagnostic inquiry. Across 468 cases and 15 models in our protocol, we observe that multi-turn evidence seeking reduces diagnostic accuracy by 12.75% and lowers supporting-evidence quality by 24.36% relative to full-context evaluation; error analyses associate these drops with premature diagnostic closure and inefficient questioning. Together, these results suggest that static full-context benchmarks may overestimate performance in interactive evidence-seeking settings, motivating complementary interactive assessment for safer clinical decision support.

### [183] [Enhancing Visual Token Representations for Video Large Language Models via Training-Free Spatial-Temporal Pooling and Gridding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22078)
*Bingjun Luo,Tony Wang,Hanqi Chen,Xinpeng Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 ST-GridPool 的视频视觉 token 增强方法。它通过无需训练的分层时序网格化与基于范数的空间池化技术，解决了视频多模态模型中 token 压缩导致的特征丢失问题，实现了在不增加训练成本的前提下显著提升模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型（MLLMs）在处理视频时，通常使用简单的池化或插值方法来压缩视觉 token，这往往导致对视频细粒度时空动态的捕捉能力不足，丢失了关键的视觉特征信息。作者旨在提出一种既能高效压缩又能保留时空交互信息的通用方案。

Method: ST-GridPool 包含两个核心组件：1. 分层时序网格化（Pyramid Temporal Gridding, PTG）：通过多粒度的层级化处理捕捉复杂的时空交互；2. 基于范数的空间池化（Norm-based Spatial Pooling, NSP）：利用 token 范数与语义丰富度之间的相关性，筛选并保留高信息量的视觉区域。该方法无需额外的训练过程即可直接应用。

Result: 在多个视频理解基准测试上的实验表明，ST-GridPool 能够在无需昂贵的重新训练的情况下，持续提升视频多模态大模型的性能，证明了其在视觉 token 表示优化方面的有效性与实用性。

Conclusion: ST-GridPool 是一种无需训练、即插即用的高效视频视觉 token 压缩方法。它通过分层时序网格化（PTG）和基于范数的空间池化（NSP）技术，有效弥补了传统池化方法在捕捉复杂时空交互和保留关键语义信息方面的不足，为提升视频多模态大模型的性能提供了一种低成本的解决方案。

Abstract: Recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have significantly advanced video understanding tasks, yet challenges remain in efficiently compressing visual tokens while preserving spatiotemporal interactions. Existing methods, such as LLaVA family, utilize simplistic pooling or interpolation techniques that overlook the intricate dynamics of visual tokens. To bridge this gap, we propose ST-GridPool, a novel training-free visual token enhancement method designed specifically for Video LLMs. Our approach integrates Pyramid Temporal Gridding (PTG), which captures multi-grained spatiotemporal interactions through hierarchical temporal gridding, and Norm-based Spatial Pooling (NSP), which preserves high-information visual regions by leveraging the correlation between token norms and semantic richness. Extensive experiments on various benchmarks demonstrate that ST-GridPool consistently enhances performance of Video LLMs without requiring costly retraining. Our method offers an efficient and plug-and-play solution for improving visual token representations. Our code is available in https://github.com/bingjunluo/ST-GridPool.

</details>


### [184] [A Camera-Cooperative ISAC Framework for Multimodal Non-Cooperative UAVs Sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22090)
*Wenfeng Wu,Luping Xiang,Kun Yang*

Main category: cs.AI

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种摄像头辅助的通信感知一体化（CC-ISAC）框架，核心包括两个模块：(1) 视觉-回波数据对齐（V2EDA）模型，利用交叉注意力机制实现视觉与雷达回波特征的对齐；(2) 基于多模态融合的估计（MMFE）模型，结合历史数据与当前观测进行稳健的状态估计。

Result: 基于DeepSense 6G数据集的评估显示，该框架在保持高角度估计精度的同时，波束导向开销平均降低了71%，跟踪开销降低了1.69%-11.15%，显著缓解了感知与通信间的资源竞争。

Conclusion: CC-ISAC框架通过视觉与通信感知的互补融合，有效地解决了无人机检测中感知资源受限和跟踪精度不足的问题，证明了多模态协同在未来6G通信感知一体化系统中的巨大潜力。

Abstract: The detection of non-cooperative unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) presents significant challenges for Integrated Sensing and Communication (ISAC) systems due to the inherent limitations of single-modal perception and the competition for shared communication and sensing resources. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel Camera-Cooperative ISAC (CC-ISAC) framework that employs multimodal sensing to enable efficient UAV beam steering and tracking. The proposed framework employs cameras for coarse-grained airspace monitoring and utilizes ISAC for fine-grained, high-precision sensing, forming a complementary perception loop that enhances both sensing accuracy and resource efficiency. Within this framework, two key modules are developed: (1) a Vision-to-Echo Data Alignment (V2EDA) model that aligns visual and echo-domain features through cross-attention mechanisms, and (2) a Multimodal Fusion-Based Estimation (MMFE) model that integrates historical multimodal data with current observations for robust state estimation. Extensive evaluations conducted on the DeepSense 6G dataset demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves an average reduction of 71% in beam steering overhead and 1.69-11.15% in tracking overhead while maintaining high angular estimation accuracy. The CC-ISAC framework effectively mitigates resource contention between sensing and communication, enabling reliable UAV surveillance while freeing substantial system resources for additional communication tasks, thereby representing a practical advancement in ISAC system design.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前知识图谱建模实践极度多样化（从轻量级词汇到复杂本体），导致集成与复用成本高昂且脆弱。特别是在神经符号AI领域，缺乏统一的理论框架限制了生成式AI在知识图谱自动化工程中的有效应用。

Method: 研究采用实证方法，通过观察真实的知识图谱工程实践，提取出“语义与语用”、“属性与可供性”两个正交维度，构建了本体论连续体框架。该框架利用形式概念分析（FCA）进行形式化描述，并通过溯源知识案例研究验证了其理论的有效性。

Result: 提出了“本体论连续体”理论构造，建立了描述和导航知识图谱建模实践的词汇体系；通过溯源知识案例展示了该框架如何捕捉不同建模关注点的表现形式；最后提出了五个开放性研究挑战，呼吁建立共享的研究议程。

Conclusion: 本体论连续体（Ontological Continuum）作为一种理论框架，为理解、描述和转换多样化的知识图谱提供了统一的语言，旨在解决知识图谱集成与复用中的碎片化问题，并为生成式人工智能在知识图谱工程中的应用提供了原则性的指导。

Abstract: Knowledge graphs have become the primary vehicle for data integration and are critical to the success of modern AI, but the diversity of KG modelling practices, from lightweight vocabularies to richly axiomatised ontologies, makes integration and reuse expensive and brittle. This challenge is particularly acute in neuro-symbolic AI, where bridging neural and symbolic components depends on the ability to reengineer KGs to fit new requirements; GenAI now offers unprecedented automation capability, but without a principled understanding of the KG space, such automation remains conceptually ungrounded. We introduce the ontological continuum as that missing conceptualisation, a theoretical construct a theoretical construct whose characterisation framework is defined by two orthogonal distinctions: semantics vs pragmatics, and properties vs affordances; together these define a vocabulary to describe, compare, navigate, and transform KGs across the full range of modelling practices. The methodological stance is empirical: rather than prescribing how KGs should be modelled, the continuum aims to define a theory of the existent, derived from observation of real-world KG engineering practices and whose structure can be made formally explicit, for example, through Formal Concept Analysis (FCA). We ground the vision through a case study on provenance knowledge, showing how a single concern manifests differently across the continuum. We articulate five open research challenges and invite the community to develop the ontological continuum as a shared research agenda.

### [187] [ArborKV: Structure-Aware KV Cache Management for Scaling Tree-based LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22106)
*Yeqiu Chen,Ziyan Liu,Zhenxin Huang,Runquan Gui,Hong Wang,Lei Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对思维树（ToT）推理中 KV 缓存占用过大导致内存瓶颈的问题，ArborKV 提出了一种结构感知的 KV 剔除与重加载框架，通过高效的资源管理显著提升了搜索规模与吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 思维树（ToT）推理方法通过多分支搜索显著提升了大语言模型的推理能力，但会导致 KV 缓存爆炸式增长，从而在固定硬件资源下限制了搜索的深度与广度。该研究旨在解决这一内存瓶颈问题。

Method: 提出了 ArborKV 框架：1) 结合轻量级价值评估器来预测各分支的未来潜力；2) 采用树感知的内存分配策略；3) 执行纯令牌提取式（token-extractive）剔除机制，并利用延迟重加载（lazy rehydration）技术，在保证回溯需求的同时显著降低内存占用。

Result: 在 ToT 推理基准测试中，ArborKV 在保持几乎不损失推理准确率的前提下，实现了高达 4 倍的峰值 KV 内存节省，使模型能够在相同的硬件预算下进行更大规模的搜索配置。

Conclusion: ArborKV 通过对 KV 缓存进行智能感知和有选择的剔除与重加载，成功打破了思维树（ToT）推理中内存瓶颈的限制，为在大规模推理任务中实现更深、更广的搜索提供了高效的内存管理方案。

Abstract: Recent progress in LLM reasoning has increasingly shifted from single-pass generation to explicit search over intermediate reasoning states. Tree-of-Thoughts (ToT) organizes inference to tree-structured search with branching and backtracking, but it substantially amplifies the Key--Value (KV) cache: retaining KV states for a frontier of partial trajectories quickly becomes a memory bottleneck that limits throughput and constrains search depth and width under fixed hardware budgets. We address this challenge by observing that KV reuse in ToT-style inference is governed by search dynamics: near-term decoding depends primarily on the active branch and its ancestors, whereas inactive subtrees have low short-term reuse probability yet must remain recoverable for backtracking. Motivated by this, we propose ArborKV, a structure-aware eviction framework that couples a lightweight value estimator with a tree-aware allocation policy, and performs purely token-extractive eviction with lazy rehydration to support revisits. Experiments on ToT-style reasoning benchmarks show that ArborKV achieves up to ~4x peak KV-memory reduction while preserving near-full-retention accuracy, enabling larger search configurations under fixed device budgets that would otherwise run out of memory.

### [188] [Perception or Prejudice: Can MLLMs Go Beyond First Impressions of Personality?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22109)
*Caixin Kang,Tianyu Yan,Sitong Gong,Mingfang Zhang,Liangyang Ouyang,Ruicong Liu,Bo Zheng,Huchuan Lu,Kaipeng Zhang,Yoichi Sato,Yifei Huang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了多模态大模型在评估人格时普遍存在“偏见鸿沟”，即模型能给出正确评分但缺乏证据支持，并通过提出GPR任务和MM-OCEAN数据集，量化了这一社会认知能力的缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型人格评估仅依赖于Big Five数值评分，缺乏对行为理解的深度，难以判断模型是真正理解了人格特质，还是仅仅基于表面模式进行了刻板印象式的推测。

Method: 1. 提出Grounded Personality Reasoning (GPR)任务，要求模型通过评分、推理和归因的链式过程来锚定人格特征。2. 构建MM-OCEAN数据集，包含1104个视频、5320个多选题，并提供带时间戳的行为观察和证据支撑。3. 设计三级评估框架及四项失败模式指标（偏见率、幻觉率、整合失败率、整体归因率），并对27种主流多模态大模型进行了全面基准测试。

Result: 研究发现模型存在显著的“偏见鸿沟”（Prejudice Gap）：在51%的正确评分中，模型无法引用对应的行为线索；整体归因率（Holistic-grounding Rate）极低，仅在0-33.5%之间。这表明大多数模型在人格评估中存在“知其然而不知其所以然”的现象。

Conclusion: 现有的多模态大模型在人格感知方面存在严重的“偏见鸿沟”，即模型往往能给出正确的人格评分，但无法提供有效的行为证据支撑。该研究指出了模型在社会认知能力方面的局限性，并为未来实现真正具有解释性、逻辑性的社会化人工智能指明了方向。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) are increasingly deployed in human-facing roles where personality perception is critical, yet existing benchmarks evaluate this capability solely on numerical Big Five score prediction, leaving open whether models truly perceive personality through behavioral understanding or merely prejudge through superficial pattern matching. We address this gap with three contributions. (i) A new task: we formalize Grounded Personality Reasoning (GPR), which requires MLLMs to anchor each Big Five rating in observable evidence through a chain of rating, reasoning, and grounding. (ii) A new dataset: we release MM-OCEAN (1,104 videos, 5,320 MCQs), produced by a multi-agent pipeline with human verification, with timestamped behavioral observations, evidence-grounded trait analyses, and seven categories of cue-grounding MCQs. (iii) Benchmark and analysis: we design a three-tier evaluation (rating, reasoning, grounding) plus four sample-level failure-mode metrics: Prejudice Rate (PR), Confabulation Rate (CR), Integration-failure Rate (IR), and Holistic-grounding Rate (HR), and benchmark 27 MLLMs (13 closed, 14 open). The analysis uncovers a striking Prejudice Gap: across the field, 51% of correct ratings are not grounded in retrieved cues, and the Holistic-Grounding Rate spans only 0-33.5%. These findings expose a disconnect between getting the right score and reasoning for the right reason, charting a roadmap for grounded social cognition in MLLMs.

*Xing Zhang,Yanwei Cui,Guanghui Wang,Ziyuan Li,Wei Qiu,Bing Zhu,Peiyang He*

Method: 提出 Ratchet 系统，这是一个包含自动编写、检索、维护和退休功能的单智能体循环。该方法整合了四种卫生机制：基于结果的退休机制、有界主动上限、元技能编写指导以及模式规范化。并通过消融实验分析了各组件的必要性。

Conclusion: Ratchet 框架证明了通过自动化的技能生命周期管理（退休机制与元技能指导），冻结权重的 LLM 智能体能够有效地积累可复用的高质量技能，从而显著超越无技能基准，并避免了技能库膨胀带来的性能退化。

Abstract: Self-evolving skill libraries, pioneered by Voyager, let frozen LLM agents accumulate reusable knowledge without weight updates, yet recent evaluation shows that LLM-authored skills deliver $+0.0$pp over no-skill baselines while human-curated ones deliver $+16.2$pp: the bottleneck is not skill authoring but lifecycle management. We introduce \textbf{Ratchet}, a single-agent loop in which a frozen LLM writes, retrieves, curates, and retires its own natural-language skills. Ratchet integrates four candidate hygiene mechanisms: outcome-driven retirement, a bounded active-cap, meta-skill authoring guidance, and pattern canonicalisation. On MBPP+ hard-100 with Claude Opus 4.7, Ratchet lifts held-out pass@1 from a $0.258 \pm 0.047$ baseline to a late-window rolling mean of $0.584$ (peak $0.658 \pm 0.042$) across 100 rounds and 3 seeds, a $+0.328 \pm 0.018$ rolling-mean gain where the no-skill control drifts at $+0.002 \pm 0.005$; the same recipe transfers to an agentic solver on SWE-bench Verified ($+0.22$ peak lift over 20 rounds). Eight ablations (A1--A8) reveal that the minimal working recipe is smaller than our design suggests: retirement and the meta-skill authoring prior are load-bearing, while explicit deduplication (canonicalisation, cover-guard) is subsumed by the meta-skill itself. A non-divergence proposition shows that bounded cap and retirement threshold together prevent expected performance from drifting below the no-skills floor.

### [190] [ST-SimDiff: Balancing Spatiotemporal Similarity and Difference for Efficient Video Understanding with MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22158)
*Bingjun Luo,Tony Wang,Chaoqi Chen,Xinpeng Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ST-SimDiff 是一种无需训练的视频压缩框架，通过协同分析视觉标记的时空相似性与差异性，在保留关键动态信息的同时高效去除了冗余，显著提升了多模态大模型处理长视频的性能与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型（MLLM）在处理长视频时产生巨大的计算开销，而现有压缩方法往往忽视了视频内容中的“变化”与“转折点”，且缺乏对时空关联的协同建模。

Method: 提出了一个无需训练的 ST-SimDiff 框架：1) 构建时空图来统一建模视觉标记的复杂关联；2) 采用并行双选择策略，即基于社区检测的相似性选择用于压缩静态信息，基于时间差异的选择用于精确定位并保留动态变化的关键点。

Result: 实验表明，ST-SimDiff 在显著降低计算成本的同时，在长视频理解任务中大幅优于现有的先进方法。

Conclusion: ST-SimDiff 通过时空图建模和“相似性去冗余、差异性捕获关键”的双重策略，在不增加额外训练开销的前提下，有效解决了长视频处理中的计算效率问题，为多模态大模型的长视频理解提供了新的高效范式。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) face significant computational overhead when processing long videos due to the massive number of visual tokens required. To improve efficiency, existing methods primarily reduce redundancy by pruning or merging tokens based on importance or similarity. However, these approaches largely overlook a critical dimension of video content, i.e., changes and turning points, and they lack a collaborative model for spatio-temporal relationships. To address this, we propose a new perspective: similarity is for identifying redundancy, while difference is for capturing key events. Based on this, we designed a training-free framework named ST-SimDiff. We first construct a spatio-temporal graph from the visual tokens to uniformly model their complex associations. Subsequently, we employ a parallel dual-selection strategy: 1) similarity-based selection uses community detection to retain representative tokens, compressing static information; 2) temporal difference-based selection precisely locates content-changing points to preserve tokens that capture key dynamic shifts. This allows it to preserve both static and dynamic content with a minimal number of tokens. Extensive experiments show our method significantly outperforms state-of-the-art approaches while substantially reducing computational costs. Our code is available in https://github.com/bingjunluo/ST-SimDiff.

### [191] [Measuring Cross-Modal Synergy: A Benchmark for VLM Explainability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22168)
*Joël Roman Ky,Salah Ghamizi,Maxime Cordy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 针对现有VLM可解释性评估中存在的跨模态冗余导致的评估失效问题，研究提出了一种基于Shapley交互指数的协同忠实度指标，旨在更准确地评估VLM跨模态推理的真实依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLM可解释性方法依赖于单模态扰动指标，由于VLM存在跨模态冗余（仅靠文本即可回答视觉查询），导致这些指标无法准确衡量模型是否真正基于视觉信息进行推理，反而惩罚了忠实的解释方法。

Method: 1. 揭示了现有评估范式中由语言先验和模态偏见导致的“评估崩溃”现象；2. 提出了一种基于Shapley交互指数的协同忠实度（Synergistic Faithfulness, F_syn）指标，用于隔离模态间的联合Harsanyi红利；3. 对比了8种XAI方法在3种VLM架构和3个数据集上的表现。

Result: 1. 现有的VLM解释方法往往过度关注视觉显著性，而在捕捉跨模态协同方面表现欠佳；2. 基于注意力的调整方法在衡量跨模态协同上表现更优；3. F_syn指标与基准指标相比，计算速度提升了24倍，且相关性高达0.92。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了现有VLM可解释性评估指标的局限性，即单模态扰动无法捕捉跨模态的协同推理。提出的Synergistic Faithfulness指标为VLM的安全性审计提供了更严谨的评估框架，并强调了未来研究应侧重于捕捉跨模态协同而非单纯的视觉显著性。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) map complex visual inputs to semantic spaces, but interpreting the cross-modal reasoning of VLMs currently relies on post-hoc explainers evaluated via unimodal perturbation metrics. We expose a limitation in this paradigm: because multimodal datasets contain language priors and modality biases, VLMs frequently exhibit cross-modal redundancy, allowing them to answer visual queries using text alone. Consequently, unimodal metrics penalize faithful explainers, triggering an evaluation collapse where visual and textual rankings fundamentally contradict each other. %(Kendall's $τ= -0.06$). To resolve this, we introduce Synergistic Faithfulness ($\mathcal{F}_{syn}$), a scalable metric rooted in the Shapley Interaction Index that strictly isolates the joint Harsanyi dividend between modalities, serving as a highly accurate surrogate ($ρ= 0.92$) while achieving a $24\times$ computational speedup. Evaluating 8 distinct XAI methods across 3 VLM architectures and 3 benchmark datasets, reveals that explainers proposed for VLMs heavily over-index on visual salience and significantly underperform adapted attention-based methods in capturing true cross-modal synergy. By decoupling visual plausibility from cross-modal faithfulness, this work provides a rigorous evaluation framework required to safely audit VLM reasoning in high-stakes deployments.

### [192] [LLM-Metrics: Measuring Research Impact Through Large Language Model Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22176)
*Si Shen,Wenhua Zhao,Danhao Zhu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型参数化记忆的新型科研影响力评价指标“LLM-Metrics”，通过评估模型对论文内容的识别能力，在无需引文数据的情况下实时衡量科研论文的影响力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的引文计数指标存在时间滞后、学科偏见和“马太效应”等局限。本文旨在探索是否可以利用大语言模型（LLM）的参数化记忆，作为一种新的、实时且独立于引文的科研影响力评估指标。

Method: 研究人员设计了四种类型的选择题探针（涵盖标题、作者、方法和会议识别），对17个不同规模（0.5B至72B参数）的大语言模型进行了测试。评估对象为2023至2024年发表的549篇计算机科学论文，旨在验证模型对这些论文的“参数化记忆”强度与论文实际影响力（引文量）之间的相关性。

Result: 实验结果显示，17个模型中有15个产生了正向预测，其中9个统计显著（p<0.05），整体Spearman相关系数为0.1495。研究发现该指标在2024年论文上表现更强（rho=0.1880），减少了反向因果的可能性；作者识别探针效果最显著；此外，模型规模与预测能力呈非单调关系，中等规模模型（如Llama-3.2-3B）表现优于部分大型模型，表明其可能存在有效的信息过滤机制。

Conclusion: LLM-Metrics 提供了一种实时、跨学科且独立于引文的科研评价新范式。研究表明，大语言模型的参数化记忆可以作为衡量论文影响力的有效指标，克服了传统引文指标的滞后性和学科偏见等局限。

Abstract: Citation counts remain the dominant metric for assessing research impact, yet they suffer from well-documented limitations: temporal lag, disciplinary bias, and Matthew effects. Here we propose LLM-Metrics, a research-impact assessment metric derived from the parametric memory of large language models (LLMs). The central hypothesis is that high-impact papers receive greater exposure in the academic community, that this exposure enters LLM training data in textual form, and that models consequently form stronger parametric memory of these papers. We designed four types of multiple-choice probes, covering title recognition, author recognition, method recognition, and venue recognition, and evaluated 549 computer science papers published in 2023-2024 across 17 LLMs spanning 0.5B to 72B parameters from six vendors. Of the 17 models, 15 produced positive predictions, 9 of which were significant at p less than 0.05, with an overall Spearman correlation of rho = 0.1495 and p = 0.0004 against citation counts. Three additional findings support the proposed mechanism. First, the predictive signal was stronger for 2024 papers, rho = 0.1880, whose citation counts were near zero at model-training time, reducing the plausibility of a simple reverse-causality explanation. Second, author-recognition probes showed the strongest discriminative power, consistent with an exposure-driven memory mechanism. Third, model scale and predictive power were non-monotonic: a 3B-parameter model, Llama-3.2-3B-Instruct, with rho = 0.1829, outperformed most larger models, supporting a selective-memory hypothesis in which the limited capacity of smaller models can serve as an effective information filter. LLM-Metrics offers a real-time, cross-disciplinary, citation-independent paradigm for research assessment.

</details>


### [193] [Skill Weaving: Efficient LLM Improvement via Modular Skillpacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22205)
*Zhuo Li,Guodong Du,Zesheng Shi,Weiyang Guo,Weijun Yao,Yuan Zhou,Jiabo Zhang,Jing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SkillWeave 是一种模块化的大模型优化框架，通过将模型能力拆解为轻量级的领域特定技能包并进行高效压缩，使得小参数模型在资源受限下能实现优于大参数模型的性能，并显著提升推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型在应对多领域任务需求时，往往面临内存占用过大和推理延迟高的问题，难以在资源受限的情况下平衡通用能力与专业领域性能。

Method: 1. SkillWeave 架构：将通用大模型的完整能力划分为轻量级的领域特定 delta 模块（即 skillpacks）；2. SkillZip 技术：对 skillpacks 进行高效压缩，使其转换为紧凑且可直接推理的格式，从而在保证低延迟的同时实现多领域能力的重组与优化。

Result: 在多任务和智能体基准测试中，9B 参数的 SkillWeave 模型表现优于多个基准模型，甚至超过了 32B 参数的单体 LLM，同时推理速度提升了最高 4 倍。

Conclusion: SkillWeave 通过模块化设计和高效压缩技术，证明了在有限的内存和计算预算下，通过特定领域的技能包（skillpacks）可以构建出性能超越更大规模单体模型的高效多领域 LLM。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly require specialization across diverse domains, yet existing approaches struggle to balance multi-domain capacities with strict memory and inference constraints. In this work, we introduce SkillWeave, a modular improvement framework that enables LLMs to specialize under fixed memory budgets. SkillWeave partitions full capabilities of a general-purpose model into skillpacks -- lightweight, domain-specific delta modules -- that reorganize and refine the model's internal knowledge. For efficient deployment, SkillWeave integrates SkillZip to compress skillpacks into compact and inference-ready format, enabling strong multi-domain performance with low-latency execution. On multi-task and agentic benchmarks, a 9B SkillWeave model outperforms several baselines and even surpasses a 32B monolithic LLM, while achieving up to 4x speedup.

</details>


### [194] [CLORE: Content-Level Optimization for Reasoning Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22211)
*Yuyang Wu,Qiyao Xue,Guanxing Lu,Weichen Liu,Zihan Wang,Manling Li,Olexandr Isayev*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CLORE是一个通过对推理轨迹进行“精简编辑”来优化大模型推理效率的框架，它在保留正确答案的前提下剔除无用信息，有效提升了模型推理的质量与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型通过强化学习后训练提升了推理能力，但往往产生冗余、重复或语义模糊的推理过程。现有的效率优化方法多局限于长度预算或长度感知奖励，缺乏对中间推理过程的精细化监督。因此，需要一种能够从内容层面优化推理轨迹、提升生成效率的方法。

Method: 提出了CLORE框架，核心在于对正确的强化学习样本进行“内容级编辑”。该方法利用外部增强模型识别并剔除重复、模糊、任务无关的内容以及得出结果后的冗余推理，保留正确的最终答案；随后通过辅助的无参考直接偏好优化（Reference-free DPO）目标函数，与标准策略梯度训练相结合进行优化，确保编辑后的轨迹维持在策略分布附近，减少偏移。

Result: 在DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B和Qwen2.5-Math-7B模型及五个数学推理基准测试中，CLORE显著优化了准确率与效率的平衡。实验表明，CLORE有效减少了重复推理、不可读内容及解题后的多余探索，并能与GRPO、DAPO等多种现有方法良好兼容。

Conclusion: CLORE证明了在强化学习后训练阶段，通过内容级优化（删除冗余和无关信息）可以有效提升推理效率。相较于仅关注长度的控制方法，内容级监督不仅能显著改善推理轨迹的质量，还能作为一种补充手段，提升大语言模型的准确率与效率权衡。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning post-training has improved the reasoning ability of large language models, but often produces unnecessarily long, repetitive, or semantically opaque reasoning traces. Existing efficient reasoning methods mainly regulate response length through explicit budgets or length-aware rewards, leaving intermediate reasoning content weakly supervised. We propose CLORE, a content-level optimization framework that improves reasoning efficiency by editing correct on-policy rollouts. CLORE uses an external augmentation model to delete repetitive segments, illegible or task-irrelevant content, and superfluous reasoning after the solution is established, while preserving the final answer. The resulting augmented--original pairs are optimized with an auxiliary reference-free DPO objective alongside standard policy-gradient training. By restricting augmentation to correct trajectories and performing local deletion, CLORE keeps edited rollouts close to the policy distribution and mitigates off-policy mismatch. Experiments on DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-7B and Qwen2.5-Math-7B across five mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that CLORE improves the accuracy--efficiency trade-off and remains compatible with GRPO, DAPO, Training Efficient, and ThinkPrune. Content-level analyses further show that CLORE reduces repetitive reasoning, illegible content, and post-answer exploration, supporting content-level supervision as a complementary direction to length-level control.

</details>


### [195] [SGR-Bench: Benchmarking Search Agents on State-Gated Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22219)
*Ningyuan Li,Haiyang Shen,Mugeng Liu,Yudong Han,Zhuofan Shi,Sixiong Xie,Yun Ma*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了 SGR-Bench 基准测试，旨在解决大型语言模型智能体在专业网站中处理复杂状态配置（如过滤器、层级选择）时的不足，实验表明当前智能体普遍难以正确建立检索状态，这是制约其处理专业检索任务的关键瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试未充分关注“状态受限检索”（State-Gated Retrieval, SGR）任务，即用户需要通过特定的筛选器、视图或层级配置才能获取证据的专业网站检索任务，旨在弥补当前智能体在专业化数据获取能力上的评估缺失。

Method: 研究者构建了包含100项专家策划任务的 SGR-Bench 基准测试，涵盖了6个来源家族和12个公共数据生态系统。该基准采用约束引导（constraint-guided）和目标导向（goal-oriented）两种配对方式，并对8个基于CLI的开源智能体和3个商业搜索智能体产品进行了评估，通过手动审计失败轨迹分析了智能体的失效原因。

Result: 最强模型的单项 F1 分数仅为 66.18%，行级 F1 分数更低。错误分析显示，智能体主要失误在于无法建立正确的网站检索状态，其中“检索范围漂移”（37.2%）和“标准不匹配”（27.6%）是主要原因，而最终答案合成错误仅占 10.3%。

Conclusion: SGR-Bench 揭示了现有大型语言模型智能体在处理需要复杂状态配置的专业网站时存在显著短板，尤其在处理检索范围偏移和标准不匹配问题上表现不足，为未来开发更具精准控制能力的智能体指明了研究方向。

Abstract: Recent advances in large language models and tool-using agents have expanded the range of benchmarked web tasks. Yet an important class of specialized retrieval tasks remains undercharacterized. On many specialized data-retrieval websites, answer-bearing evidence becomes accessible only after establishing the correct site-specific retrieval state through filters, views, hierarchies, or scopes. We term this capability state-gated retrieval (SGR). We introduce SGR-Bench, a benchmark for this setting containing 100 expert-curated tasks spanning six source families and 12 public data ecosystems. Each task requires discovering the appropriate website and configuring its site-specific retrieval state to produce a structured answer. SGR-Bench pairs constraint-guided and goal-oriented formulations of the same underlying problems, enabling controlled comparisons between explicit and implicit guidance for state-gated retrieval. We evaluate eight CLI-based agentic LLM systems and three commercial search-agent products. On SGR-Bench, the strongest system reaches only 66.18% item-level F1, while row-level F1 remains much lower. A manual audit of 156 analyzable failed CLI trajectories shows why: agents often reach a relevant web source, but establish the wrong site-specific retrieval state. Retrieval-scope drift (37.2%) and criterion mismatch (27.6%) dominate, whereas final answer composition accounts for only 10.3%. The dataset and single-case evaluation instructions are available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/PKUAIWeb/SGR-BENCH.
